# Cerebrum

> OpenWolf's learning memory. Updated automatically as the AI learns from interactions.
> Do not edit manually unless correcting an error.
> Last updated: 2026-05-27

## User Preferences

- 2026-07-12 — Cast-time choices (adventure creature-vs-instant, kicker) must ALWAYS be presented side by side as direct one-tap buttons; an unavailable option greys out with the reason instead of disappearing. No mode-switch + second Cast press.

- 2026-07-11 — Board spotlight: the big field must follow the ACTIVE (turn) player and stay put for the whole turn; priority is signalled only by the moving gold border. Jordy rejected priority-following (too jumpy) after trying v0.12.0.

<!-- How the user likes things done. Code style, tools, patterns, communication. -->

- **App is landscape-only.** Design/layout decisions can assume a wide viewport; do not optimize the controller UI for narrow portrait.
- **Playable hint = your turn only (2026-06-15).** On opponents' turns the controller hand should NOT highlight cards as playable — keep it calm. The user accepts that this is non-MTG (you legally CAN cast instants on opponents' turns), because the highlight is purely visual: instants stay castable by TAPPING a card (server gates legality). Implemented by gating `hasPriorityWindow` on `isActivePlayer` in `ControllerListV4` MainArea. So the playable-highlight logic = `isActivePlayer && (canCastInstants || (canCastSorceries && isLand))`.
- **Controller restyle (2026-06): user chose the "Clean HUD" visual direction** — flat, high-contrast, color-coded zones (creatures=green / lands=cyan / attackers=red), mono numerics, minimal chrome. Explored in `mockups/controller-concepts*.html`; action-panel deep-dive in `mockups/clean-hud-action.html`. Mockups are throwaway, not wired into the app.
- **Action panel direction:** non-modal bottom-docked bar (board stays visible), one bold primary + ghost secondaries color-coded, live mana affordability on the cast button, inline targeting (board becomes the target picker), slide-to-confirm + 5s undo for destructive actions. **Hold-to-peek** a card shows a full-size preview WITH oracle text (user agreed oracle text is wanted) — Scryfall art_crop as art + legible oracle block + inline {symbols}.
- **Drag re-introduced narrowly:** user OK'd a drag-to-attack arrow (drag the ATTACK button onto a player) as an OPTIONAL shortcut. Tap-to-attack remains the default. This does NOT reverse the general "tap > drag" preference for card interaction below.
- **Minimize pass-priority taps (2026-06-15).** The user's recurring complaint is too many manual "Pass" clicks between actions. Bias toward auto-skipping any step where the player has NO legal action to take. First case: auto-pass your own `declare_attackers` when you control no creature that could legally attack (`hasEligibleAttacker` in ControllerListV5, gated under the `own` "My empty phases" toggle). Do NOT auto-skip steps where a real choice exists (e.g. attackers available but none selected = a deliberate "no attack" choice). Second case: `declare_blockers` was a blanket hard-exemption in the auto-pass effect; now only held when `hasBlockDecision` (you're being attacked AND control an untapped creature). With no possible block it falls through to the normal `op`/`stk`/`rsp` logic, so a held combat trick still stops auto-pass via `rsp`. Blocker eligibility = `!is_tapped` (mirrors DeclareBlockersLayout); stay conservative — only skip when NO block is possible (protection/evasion only narrow further). Third/fourth cases (user opted into both): your own `declare_blockers` as the ATTACKER auto-passes when `!iHaveResponse`; and your own main phase auto-advances when `isMainPhaseStep && empty stack && !hasMainPhaseAction`. `playerHasMainPhaseAction` (shared.ts) = land-drop OR affordable castable spell OR affordable usable activated ability (any speed, since it's your main); mirrors playerHasInstantResponse's approximate affordability. Beat = AUTOPASS_BEAT_EMPTY_MS (250ms) — may feel fast for main phase, tunable. GRANULAR TOGGLES (2026-06-16, user wanted them individually settable): these were folded under `own`; now `AutoPassSettings` = op/own/stk/rsp/**atk/blk/mn** (V5 only — V4 untouched). own = empty phases ONLY; atk = declare_attackers no-eligible-attacker; mn = dead main phase; blk = declare_blockers no-block (BOTH defender no-untapped AND attacker passive, `blk && !iHaveResponse`, +stk guard) AND drives the layoutState blocker-screen suppression (`hasBlockDecision || !autoPass.blk`). The declare_blockers branch is now a dedicated case BEFORE the active/opp split (covers both players). Defaults all true; `loadAutoPassSettings` backfills atk/blk/mn from `own` for pre-existing localStorage so returning players don't lose the skips. Popover regrouped (My turn / Opponents') + scrollable (max-h-[80vh]). Server pod-skip (mig 309) only reads own/op/rsp from the JSONB blob, so extra keys are harmless; server `own`-chaining is empty-steps-only, matching the new client `own`. NOTE (2026-06-18): V5 is now the SOLE controller — V4 was deleted (ControllerListV4.tsx removed, `?v=4` route dropped). page.tsx routes `/controller/<id>` → V5; `?v=1` is the legacy ControllerList. `controller-style-lab` (untracked HandFan lab) was left in place at the user's discretion. V5 promotion blockers handled: discard cue restored (HandFan `discardMode` → red ring + cast disabled), reorder documented as intentionally cosmetic/non-persisted. REMAINING (user-only): real-device gesture validation of HandFan (click-vs-drag, viewport-fraction CAST_LINE). Auto-pass infra: `AutoPassSettings`, `OWN_SKIP_STEPS`, the auto-pass effect, `playerHasInstantResponse`/`playerHasMainPhaseAction` (shared.ts), server-side pod auto-skip (mig 309). EXTRACTED (2026-06-16): the decision is now pure `shouldAutoPass(input)` in `lib/game/auto-pass.ts` (also exports `AutoPassSettings` type + `OWN_SKIP_STEPS`, both moved out of ControllerListV5). The V5 effect builds the input from live state, calls it, and owns only the beat timer + pass_priority RPC. Covered by `tests/unit/auto-pass.test.ts` (38 cases — every switch + hard exemptions). Input takes `currentStackKey`/`ackStackKey` strings (empty key ⟺ empty stack); `stackUnacked = key !== '' && key !== ack`. Any future change to the skip rules should update the pure fn + its tests, not re-embed logic in the effect.
- **Card interaction = tap to open a bottom sheet** (`CardActionSheet` in components/ControllerListV4.tsx), shared by hand AND played cards via single `selectedCard` state. Prefers this over drag (drag in v1/v2 felt bad). Sheet layout: pinned card preview on the LEFT, scrollable actions/abilities/target-pickers on the RIGHT, so the card stays visible while picking targets. Actions are behavior-engine-derived per card+zone, not hardcoded.

## Key Learnings

- (2026-07-13) **"Pick a card in zone X" effects follow the parked-decision template** (mig 392: grant_flashback, hand_to_library_top): apply_trigger_effects branch builds options + inserts game_pending_decisions + sets awaiting_decision/resume_index; submit_decision adds the type to the generic-validation list + a handling branch ending in resume_or_finalize; UI is FREE by adding the type to CARD_PICK_DECISIONS (ControllerListV5) — submit contract {chosen:[ids]}. Decisions can also be assigned to a NON-controller (pay_or_be_countered decides by the countered spell's controller; ConfirmBody contract {confirmed:bool}). Stack handlers park by returning non-null from handle_* (resolve_top_of_stack leaves the item awaiting). Grants that expire with the turn = turn-stamped counter on the card (counters.flashback_until_turn), not a continuous-effect row (rebuild_scripted_continuous_effects would wipe/re-add it wrongly).

- (2026-07-13) **Engine-function changes go through functions_src + new-migration.mjs, NOT hand-written migrations.** Workflow: edit `supabase/functions_src/<fn>.sql` → `node scripts/new-migration.mjs <NNN_name> <fn>` → hand-add non-function DDL at the top → apply to BOTH DBs. Mig 389 (card_cda_value) was hand-written from the mig-268 body and left functions_src stale — backfilled 2026-07-13. Grep functions_src FIRST when changing an engine function.

- (2026-07-13) **Harness `resolveStack()` resolves ONE stack item** (resolve_top_of_stack). A test that spawns multiple ETB-trigger permanents must flush with `while ((await s.pendingCount()) > 0) await s.as('A').resolveStack()` — a single call leaves the rest pending and asserts against a half-resolved board (cost 1 debug round on Dockside DC1).

- (2026-07-13) **After any bulk-scripting session, audit token refs across ALL of card-scripts.json** (every `"token":"X"` needs an is_token fixture) — the per-deck scan in deck:upsert misses cards scripted for decks that were never upserted. The 2026-07-13 audit found 8 silent no-op tokens, including Talrand's own Drake. See bug-1279.

- (2026-07-13) **Bulk-pipeline quality note:** the scions-spellcraft-build workflow run for prosper+talrand (13 cards, 26 agents) produced 0 silently-stripped fields and 0 validation failures — verify agents grounded claims in engine SQL (file:line). The mandatory post-check (validateCardScript + deep-diff vs safeParse) stays cheap insurance. needs_engine verdicts were accurate; 3 of 5 were unlocked with small additive engine work (2 counts, 1 color filter, 1 schema-only), Snapcaster Mage remains a real multi-part feature (graveyard flashback grant), see talrand triage.

- (2026-07-12) **CDA count extension pattern (mig 389, Wight of Precinct Six):** reproduce the LATEST `card_cda_value` (was mig 268 — no later redefinitions, grep migrations to confirm) verbatim, add one `when '<count>'` branch, and extend the `CdaValueSchema` count enum in lib/game/card-behavior-schema.ts. New count `creature_cards_in_opponents_graveyards` counts creature cards (`cards.is_token = false AND game_cards.is_token = false`, mig 239 convention) in every other player's graveyard. "Gets +1/+1 for each X" on a printed 1/1 = `cda: { power/toughness: { count, plus: 1 } }`.

- (2026-07-12) **Sacrifice-ONLY mana abilities work out of the box** via the mig 226 (Treasure) cost parser — `costs: [{type:'sacrifice_self'}]` with no `tap_self` is valid (Eldrazi Scion/Spawn tokens, proven in tests/feature/eldrazi-spawn-tokens.test.ts).

- (2026-07-12) **deck:upsert "DIFFERS (kept)" can mean the DB script is OLDER, not hand-improved.** Edgar Markov had 4 differing cards; in all 4 the curated card-scripts.json version was richer (DB missed the Etchings/Banner anthem; Sanctum Seeker only triggered on itself instead of any attacking Vampire). Diff DB-vs-curated before deciding, then `--force` if curated wins.

- Test DB vs dev DB: the harness runs against `leyline_test` (rebuilt via `npm run test:db:setup` from local-bootstrap + all migrations); `npx supabase migration up` only touches the dev `postgres` DB. A new migration must be applied to BOTH before feature tests can see it.

- Board/TV performance: TV browsers choke on per-frame GPU effects. The spectator board (shareToken) gets `.tv-flat` (kills `backdrop-filter: blur` on leyline-glass-panel + the priority border pulse) and `MotionConfig reducedMotion='always'` (kills transform/layout animations, keeps opacity). Decorative blur-2xl/3xl washes are skipped in tvMode. Don't add per-frame effects to GameBoard without gating them on `!tvMode`.

- TV room code (mig 379): originally only rendered as a lobby-modal footnote; since v0.11.x also via TvCodePopup (controller 📺 button). NOTE: the 2026-07-11 'discoverability, not data' diagnosis was WRONG — normalizeGameSession was silently dropping tv_code (bug-1506).
- **The card-script validator must match the ENGINE's leniency, not be stricter (2026-06-30).** `validateCardScript` (lib/game/card-behavior-schema.ts) required `amount` on the `draw` action, but the engine defaults a missing amount to 1 ("draw a card") — the `draw-floor` DF3 test is a deliberate regression guard using a no-amount `{type:'draw'}` fixture (Plain Drummer Test). The over-strict schema made that fixture (+ its " Test"-stripped name) fail and ABORTED the whole `seed-scripts-local --force` (collects all invalid, then aborts → 0 cards seeded). Fix: `amount: AmountSchema.optional()`. Lesson: when a fixture/script that the engine runs fine fails the validator, the VALIDATOR is usually wrong (loosen it) — don't mangle a fixture that a test relies on. Quick checks: `npm run validate:fixtures` (test-cards.json) and `tests/unit/card-scripts-validation.test.ts` (curated card-scripts.json) — these are SEPARATE validation surfaces.
- **Controller load is ONE RPC: `get_controller_state(session, player)` (2026-06-30, mig 370).** Previously `use-controller-game-state.ts` did ~19 separate PostgREST reads per reload (every game action) PLUS a `cards`-catalog re-fetch (getLinkedCardsById) for board+hand cards each time — heavy request volume over a long game. Now one `security definer` PL/pgSQL fn returns a jsonb bundling: session, turn_state, players, combat_action_state, combat_assignments, stack_items, pending_decisions (these EMBED the existing helper RPCs via `(select jsonb_agg(to_jsonb(t)) from public.get_x(...) t)`; get_combat_action_state returns jsonb directly; get_turn_state is `setof` returning 0/1 rows → `to_jsonb(t) ... limit 1`), mana_pool, restricted_mana, commander_damage (joined to card name), board_cards + controller_cards (catalog fields JOINED in SQL — board has name/image/type/keywords inline, controller has a nested `cards` object with script), and ONE raw `continuous_effects` array. The client (`getControllerState` in lib/game/data.ts) derives pump/protection/status/granted-keywords/cost-reductions/cast-from-top/play-from-exile from that single array (same transforms as the old 7 per-effect-type queries) and returns the SAME 19 named values the hook destructured, so the hook body barely changed. SECURITY: locked to `p_player_id = auth.uid()` + `is_session_player` (private zones owner-scoped). VERIFY PATTERN before trusting a shape-sensitive consolidation: call the RPC as the player (set request.jwt.claims) and deep-compare section counts/fields vs raw legacy queries on a LIVE session (did this → board 34=34, controller 106=106, ce 39=39, etc.). Test: tests/feature/controller-state.test.ts (CS1, incl. cross-player deny). The legacy getX in data.ts are kept (still used elsewhere / fallback). **Board got the same treatment: `get_board_state(session)` (mig 371) — the big-screen counterpart, ~8 reads → 1, no player param/private zones (public board state, gated to a session member), status narrowed to animated+attack_tax. Client `getBoardState` in data.ts; `useBoardGameState` rewired. Shared mappers `mapBoardCardRow` + `groupCommanderDamageRows` are used by BOTH getControllerState and getBoardState. Verified byte-equal on a live 4-player session (board 62=62, players 4=4, cmd 6=6). Test: tests/feature/board-state.test.ts (BS1, incl. non-member deny).** NOTE: piles (graveyard/exile/log) render ONLY when their sheet is open and MotionCard uses next/image (lazy by default), so there is NO persistent unbounded DOM pile to cap — the only always-rendered growing zone is the battlefield (inherent). [[bug-IDLE-POLL-STORM]]
- **"Nth spell you cast each turn" cost reduction + per-turn spell counter (2026-06-30, mig 369, Alisaie's Dualcast).** Per-turn spell-cast tally lives on `game_session_players.turn_spells_cast(+_turn)` (turn-stamped, lazy reset — same pattern as `turn_graveyard_casts`/`turn_creatures_died`: stored value valid only when `_turn = current turn_number`, else read as 0; NO advance_step reset needed). `note_spell_cast(session,player)` bumps it and is called from `fire_watcher_triggers` whenever `p_event='spell_cast'` and `p_changed_controller is not null` (caster) — so it counts exactly what the engine treats as a cast (lands return early and don't fire spell_cast; bot/system casts have null auth.uid() and are skipped). `resolve_count_amount` exposes it as `'spells_cast_this_turn'` = spells ALREADY cast (the spell being cast now is index count+1). `reduced_mana_cost` gained an `nth_spell` predicate on the STATIC cost_reduction path: payload `{amount, nth_spell:K}` applies ONLY when `spells_cast_this_turn = K-1` (exactly the Kth spell, not Kth-or-later). Card registers it as an `affected:'controller'` `cost_reduction` continuous effect `{amount:2, nth_spell:2}`. CRITICAL TIMING: in cast_card_from_hand, `reduced_mana_cost` (charge, line ~432) runs BEFORE the `spell_cast` fire (line ~505) that increments — so the current cast sees the PRE-increment count (1st spell→count 0, 2nd→count 1=discount, 3rd→count 2=no discount). reduced_mana_cost only reduces the GENERIC token, floored at 0. [[bug-DUALCAST-ALISAIE]] **EXTENDED to triggers (mig 372, Alphinaud's Eukrasia "whenever you cast your SECOND spell each turn, draw"):** a `spell_number` filter on the spell_cast watcher in fire_watcher_triggers fires only when `resolve_count_amount('spells_cast_this_turn', p_changed_controller) == filter.spell_number`. Works because note_spell_cast runs at the TOP of fire_watcher_triggers (before the watcher scan), so the current cast is already counted (2nd spell → 2). MUST add the new filter key to the trigger-filter Zod schema in card-behavior-schema.ts (~line 1313) or validateCardScript STRIPS it on seed. Script: `triggered_abilities:[{event:'spell_cast', filter:{controller:'you', spell_number:2}, effects:[{type:'draw',amount:1}]}]`. Test: tests/feature/second-spell-trigger.test.ts (SS1 — library count isolates the Eukrasia draw; resolveStack only pops the TOP item, so DRAIN the stack — the trigger stacks above its spell). FF-deck scan (Scions Spellcraft) also found Lyse Hext ("2+ NONCREATURE spells this turn → double strike" needs a noncreature-only counter variant) and Hraesvelgr / Summon: Good King Mog II-III (per-CAST noncreature triggers, not per-turn-count) as separate unbuilt gaps.
- **Realtime fallback poll must gate on EVENT DELIVERY, not just channel health (2026-06-30).** The two active-path game-state hooks (`use-controller-game-state.ts` → ControllerListV5/"Controller v2"; `use-board-game-state.ts` → GameBoard big screen) each run a `setInterval(fallbackRefreshIntervalMs=2000ms)` fallback poll (`enableFallbackRefresh` defaults ON unless `NEXT_PUBLIC_ENABLE_FALLBACK_REFRESH==='false'`). The OLD guard was realtime SILENCE (`Date.now()-lastRealtimeAt>=interval`) — turn-based play is idle most of the time, so during think-time every client reloaded its FULL state every 2s (controller ~18 queries, board ~8). **CRUCIAL GOTCHA (do NOT just trust SUBSCRIBED):** Supabase realtime `postgres_changes` is RLS-filtered PER SUBSCRIBER. An AUTHENTICATED player receives events for every game table (verified empirically: raw pg write like bot-runner → 401 game_cards events reach the player, via the cloudflared tunnel `supabase.dweemo.nl` AND direct). But an UNAUTHENTICATED client (the board page `app/board/[id]` has NO login gate, and nothing calls `realtime.setAuth`) gets a SUBSCRIBED channel that delivers ZERO events (anon RLS denies SELECT). bot-runner writes via raw pg `:54322`, and no browser triggers a refresh for a bot turn, so an anon board's ONLY update path is the poll — gating purely on `channelHealthy` (SUBSCRIBED) froze the anon board on bot/opponent moves. FINAL FIX: poll if `(!channelHealthy || !hasEverReceivedEvent) && silent`. Wire `.on('postgres_changes', …, onRealtimeEvent)` where `onRealtimeEvent` sets `hasEverReceivedEvent=true` (the re-subscribe catch-up calls `scheduleReload`/`scheduleRefresh` directly so it does NOT flip the flag). Authed clients flip the flag on the first event → stop idle-polling (the network win); anon clients never flip it → keep polling (stay correct). **ROOT CAUSE of why even a logged-in player got zero realtime events (2026-06-30):** supabase-js `_handleTokenChanged` calls `realtime.setAuth(token)` ONLY on `SIGNED_IN`/`TOKEN_REFRESHED`/`SIGNED_OUT` — NOT on `INITIAL_SESSION`. `@supabase/ssr` restores the cookie session on EVERY page load as `INITIAL_SESSION`, so realtime stays on the anon apikey after a reload → RLS `postgres_changes` deliver nothing even to authed players → the fallback poll never stops (constant fetches). FIX (lib/supabase/client.ts): after `createBrowserClient`, once (module flag + `window` check), `client.auth.getSession().then(({data})=> data.session && client.realtime.setAuth(data.session.access_token))`. Verified: anon realtime=0 events; `setAuth(token)` before OR AFTER subscribe → events flow (273 game_cards events). This fixes realtime app-wide (controller, board-if-authed, GameLogPanel, judge). **The board route `app/board/[id]/page.tsx` is now SERVER-SIDE LOGIN-GATED (2026-06-30): `createClient()` (lib/supabase/server.ts) → `auth.getClaims()` → `redirect('/auth/login?next=/board/'+id)` when no `claims.sub` — same pattern as collection/protected pages; login supports a safe `?next=`. So the board can't run anon → realtime delivers (via the client.ts setAuth) → its fallback poll stops after the first event.** A logged-in NON-member still gets 0 events (RLS) and keeps polling, but that isn't the couch-play board operator (host = a session member). `createClient()` (@supabase/ssr 0.10.2) is a browser SINGLETON (54 call sites → ONE websocket). LEGACY/judge code (use-judge-game-state, use-legacy-controller-game-state, useGameLoopState, the 6 *Panel components) has WORSE UNGUARDED `setInterval(refresh,...)` pollers but only mounts on /judge and ?v=1, NOT the active board+v5 path.
- **Anthem branch supports a `commander_only` predicate (2026-06-29, mig 368, Dancer's Chakrams).** The "other commanders you control get +2/+2 and have lifelink" clause is an ability GRANTED to the equipped creature, so model it from the Equipment as affected:'controller' pump+lifelink rows with `payload.commander_only=true`. The accessors (`card_layered_power`/`card_layered_toughness` anthem branch + `card_has_lifelink`) gate the anthem on `game_cards.is_commander` AND `game_cards.id is distinct from source_card.attached_to` (the "OTHER" = exclude the equipped creature). `register_card_continuous_effects` SKIPS commander_only effects when `v_source_card.attached_to is null`, so the buff is active only WHILE a creature is equipped (not unconditionally on the battlefield). `getActivePumpTotals` (lib/game/data.ts) sums ALL pump rows incl. static affected:'equipped' ones, so equipped buffs already show on the controller board (the user's "+2/+2 until EOT" was the missing commander clause, not a real EOT expiry). FF "Job select" Equipment (mig 297) enters attached to a 1/1 Hero token, so it's effectively always equipped. [[opponent-view-design]]
- **Local dev DB (:54322) has PHANTOM-VERSION drift (2026-06-29).** `supabase_migrations.schema_migrations` claims a high version (367) but the actual FUNCTION BODIES are behind — e.g. its `card_layered_power` predated mig 342 and `library_top_is_color` was missing entirely. `supabase migration up --local` refuses with "Found local migration files to be inserted before the last migration on remote database" and applies nothing. REPAIR that works: apply the missing canonical dep from functions_src FIRST (here library_top_is_color, needs only card_color_set), then run the new migration's SQL directly via `pg` in one tx and `insert into supabase_migrations.schema_migrations(version,name)`. Canonical accessor upgrades are safe because every newer predicate is payload-gated (older rows lack the key → no-op). [[local-migrations]] [[never-purge-user-data]]
- **`scripts/seed-scripts-local.mjs --force` aborts wholesale on ANY invalid script (2026-06-29).** Two pre-existing invalid entries ("plain drummer" / "plain drummer test": triggered_abilities effect with invalid fields) make the bulk local seeder validate-then-abort, so NO cards get written. To seed one card despite this, UPDATE `public.cards.script` directly via pg for that name (the curated script already passes the card-scripts-validation unit test). Worth fixing those two scripts eventually so the seeder works again.
- **Scryfall image CDN requires a custom User-Agent (2026-06-29).** `cards.scryfall.io` now returns HTTP 400 (`subcode: generic_user_agent`) to any request with a default HTTP-library UA. Next's `<Image>` optimizer fetches upstream with Node's default `fetch` UA, so EVERY `/_next/image?url=...cards.scryfall.io...` 400s ("upstream response is invalid") while the browser/curl load the same URL fine (their own UA is accepted). The optimizer gives no hook to set the upstream UA. FIX: custom loader `image-loader.ts` returns `cards.scryfall.io` URLs unchanged (browser loads them directly, bypassing the optimizer) and keeps the default `/_next/image?...` path for everything else; wired via `images.loader:'custom'` + `loaderFile` in next.config.ts. Requires a dev-server restart (next.config loads only at startup). [[bug-IMG-UA]]
- **Keywords are stored as `game_continuous_effects` rows keyed by `effect_type` = the keyword name (2026-06-27).** A printed flyer registers a SELF row (`affected_card_id = own id`); an aura/equipment/combat-trick GRANT registers a row pointing at the granted creature; an ANTHEM grant has `affected_card_id = null` + predicates in `payload` (creature_type / controller via affected_player_id / exclude_source / token_only / condition_top_card_color). The `card_has_<kw>(session, card)` accessors read this table applying those predicates (+ `source_zone_required`). So the EFFECTIVE keyword set ≠ the catalog `cards.keywords` line (printed only). The opponent view's `KeywordIconRow` showed catalog-only and missed grants → combat misreads. FIX (client-only, no migration): `getGrantedKeywords(supabase, session)` (lib/game/data.ts) queries keyword effect_types with a non-null `affected_card_id` → `{cardId: effect_type[]}`, merged onto `BoardCard.keywords` in `use-controller-game-state` (NOT use-board — the big-screen GameBoard renders no keyword icons, so merging there is dead data). `normalizeKeywords` (components/controller/KeywordIcon.tsx) now `replace(/_/g,' ')` so the underscored effect_type ('first_strike') maps via the space-form ALIASES; printed+granted dedupe via its Set. SCOPE: direct grants only — ANTHEM grants (null affected_card_id, e.g. Death Baron typed deathtouch) need the server predicate logic and stay deferred. Tests: tests/unit/keyword-icons.test.ts. [[opponent-view-design]]
- **Engine effect-resolution architecture (2026-06-26, while building 5 card features).** Two parallel resolvers exist: `apply_trigger_effects` (the PROGRAM resolver — handles modes/targets/choose/edicts/`may`, has a resume_index mechanism for parking decisions mid-program) and `apply_triggered_ability_effects` (the per-effect applier — grant_keyword, add_counters, tap_all, draw, lose/gain_life, and now `tap_self`). BOTH the multi-effect activated-ability path (`activate_ability` routes >1 effect through a `spell_effect` stack item → `handle_spell_effect`) and triggered abilities (`handle_triggered_ability`) funnel through `apply_trigger_effects`, which delegates non-targeted unknown effects to `apply_targeted_triggered_ability_effects` → `apply_triggered_ability_effects` with the source as target. So a new SELF/untargeted effect goes in `apply_triggered_ability_effects`; a new decision-parking effect goes in `apply_trigger_effects`. Stack actions map to handlers via the `stack_action_handlers` table; `handle_*` bodies live in MIGRATIONS, not functions_src (grep migrations for the latest def). Watcher/self events: card-subject events ride `fire_watcher_triggers(session, changed_card, controller, event)` / `fire_card_triggers(session, card, text[])`; PLAYER-scoped events (no card subject — e.g. the new `you_gain_life`) need a dedicated scanner (`fire_lifegain_triggers`) called after each mutation site. The trigger `filter` object is non-strict — `fire_watcher_triggers` already honours `max_power`/`token`/`nontoken`/`min_power` even when the Zod schema strips them, so some "needs_engine" cards are SCHEMA-ONLY fixes. Migration workflow: edit `functions_src/*.sql` → `node scripts/new-migration.mjs <name> <fn>...` → hand-add non-function DDL (CHECK constraints! e.g. `game_continuous_effects_effect_type_check` must list a new effect_type) at the TOP → `npm run test:db:setup` (rebuilds `leyline_test`) → `npm test -- <filter>`. A type-filtered continuous anthem (`continuous_effects:[{type, affected:'all'|'controller', payload:{creature_type}}]`) is read by `card_layered_power`/keyword accessors; a "choose a type" anthem bakes `$chosen` into `copied_script` in `submit_decision` then needs `rebuild_scripted_continuous_effects` to re-register with the concrete type. Reflexive "when you do" = a `may` with `program:true` (confirm enqueues inner effects as a fresh program so each parks its own decision — sacrifice edict then `destroy_up_to` pick), gated by the may's `condition` count. Tokens resolve by `lower(name)` against `cards` where `is_token` — add fixtures to tests/fixtures/test-cards.json so `deck:upsert` can create catalog rows. New action types must be added to `KNOWN_V2_ACTION_TYPES` AND either the registry or `JSON_ONLY` in tests/unit/registry-schema-drift.test.ts. [[bug-1484]]
- **Engine vocabulary added 2026-06-26 round 2 (migs 345-353, Deadpool deck — copy/reanimate/return cluster).** `grant_dies_effect` (grant a creature "when this dies, <effects>") is now spell-targetable (added to `trigger_effect_target_type` creature family) and `return_self_to_battlefield` re-fields the source from its graveyard (tapped/+counter). CRITICAL put_in_graveyard pattern: granted_dies_effect payloads must be CAPTURED into a variable BEFORE the zone→graveyard move — a TOKEN's cease trigger fires on that move and deletes the rows (and the token) first; apply them AFTER the move so `return_self` finds the card in graveyard. Reanimation = `return_from_graveyard` with `from:'all_graveyards'`+`control:'decider'` (works in the spell resolver; the workflow's `reanimate_from_graveyard` does NOT — activate_ability-only) + a `lose_life_mana_value` rider (Reanimate). Copy-token cluster: `copy_permanent` ALREADY works fully (target:'triggering_creature', target_filter pick, `except.keywords:['haste']`); added `except.cleanup_at_end_step` (create_copy_token stamps a counter, advance_step's end-step block removes the token), `except.dies_effect` (stamps a granted_dies_effect on the copy — Jaxis), `count` (N copies — Orthion), `target:'attached'` (copy the source's equipped host — Helm, on the existing `begin_combat` event), and routed `copy_permanent` through activate_ability's single-effect spell_effect list (activated copy). `blink` effect (apply_creature_effect): exile+return a creature, re-fires ETB (Conjurer's Closet); tokens cease on exile. `gain_control` gained `to:'opponent'` (donate — Harmless Offering). The `may` (mig 339) now carries `triggering_card_id` in its decision params so a confirm-program's reflexive copy_permanent target:'triggering_creature' keeps its subject (Flameshadow). GOTCHA: an OPTIONAL targeted trigger (`optional:true`) does NOT set target_required, so `choose_triggered_ability_creature_target` rejects it ("does not require a trigger target") — make the target required (approximate "you may" as mandatory) if you need the picker. Test loop must call chooseTriggerTarget ONCE per trigger (it resolves it; a second call on the same item fails). ensureTestCards seeds `where not exists` — changing a fixture's script needs `npm run test:db:setup` (drops cards) to take effect. [[bug-1484]]
- **Engine vocabulary added 2026-06-26 (migs 335-344, the full Edgar Markov needs_engine set — all 63 deck cards now scripted).** Reusable mechanics now in the engine: `tap_self` (tap the source, fires becomes_tapped); `you_gain_life` + `permanent_sacrificed` PLAYER-scoped watcher events (fired by `fire_lifegain_triggers` / direct `fire_watcher_triggers` calls after EVERY mutation site — life gain has ~6 sites, sacrifice has 4: the edict in submit_decision + sac-self/creature/artifacts costs in activate_ability; player events use the `''` type-default in fire_watcher_triggers); `choose_creature_type` persistent anthem (bake `$chosen` → `rebuild_scripted_continuous_effects`) and its `who:'each_player'` per-player decision QUEUE (params.player_queue popped one at a time in submit_decision, $chosen injected into pump_all/count/`return_all_from_graveyard`); `fear` keyword (card_has_fear + declare_blocker, mirrors intimidate); reflexive "when you do" = `may` with `program:true` + `condition` gate (confirm enqueues inner effects as a fresh program); `destroy_up_to` gained a `nonland` filter; `return_from_graveyard` filter gained `max_mana_value_of:'source_power'` + `permanent`; `pump` gained `target:'triggering_creature'` and a `shared_type_attackers` count (subtype-overlap among declared attackers, resolved at trigger resolution); `library_top_is_color` predicate (`condition_top_card_color` payload) read by card_layered_power/toughness + card_has_flying for top-of-library conditional anthems; `grant_dies_effect` action stores a `granted_dies_effect` continuous effect on a creature that put_in_graveyard fires on death (the "grant an ability" primitive). KNOWN approximations shipped: Clavileño skips the "becomes a Demon" type-addition (no type-grant mechanic); Welcoming Vampire / Mavren Fein / Clavileño use once_per_turn for the team/whenever-you-attack triggers. New CHECK-constraint effect_types must be added to `game_continuous_effects_effect_type_check` (hand-added DDL at the top of the migration).
- **Priority clarity ("waiting on whom", 2026-06-25).** `get_turn_state` returns `priority_username` (coalesced: priority holder's name, falling back to active player; CPU 🤖 <seat> for bots) and `priority_player_id` (coalesced to active when the raw column is null). The controller **PriorityPanel** (ControllerListV5) now names the priority holder in its Wait state (+ "on the stack" sub-hint when stackCount>0) and bottom indicator; the **BoardViewChrome** shows a "Waiting on {name}" amber chip ONLY when `priority_player_id !== active_player_id` (a real response window — quiet otherwise, since the active-seat highlight covers a player's own turn). Testing gotcha: `get_turn_state` is security-definer but gates on `auth.uid()`/is_session_player, so calling it as the raw postgres role returns ZERO rows — impersonate (set request.jwt.claims sub + `set local role authenticated`) like bot-runner does. Also: scripts that mutate `game_turn_state.priority_player_id` to simulate must restore in a finally/guard — at rest priority == active_player_id.
- **The rules ENGINE performs game state changes — NOT per-player manual table actions (2026-06-25, user-confirmed design principle).** I built a "manual table actions" feature on the controller (life ±, player counters ±, make tokens, sacrifice, ±1/+1) and the user rejected it: *"het is eigenlijk niet de bedoeling dat iedereen handmatige tafelacties kan uitvoeren — hiervoor hebben we de complete rule engine."* It was fully reverted. So: life changes, counters, tokens, sacrifice, etc. happen through proper game actions resolved by the engine (a spell that makes a token does it; sacrifice via an effect/cost; life via damage/effects). Player-scoped state-mutation RPCs (`adjust_player_life`, `adjust_card_counters`, `adjust_player_counter`, `create_token`, `move_card_to_zone`) exist but are **judge/correction tools** (JudgePlayerCardTools / LifeTotalsPanel) — they are NOT to be surfaced as routine controller actions. When my analysis flags "manual life adjust / token UI / sacrifice button" as a *missing* capability, treat it as INTENTIONALLY absent, not a gap. See Do-Not-Repeat. (Technical note still true: those RPCs only gate on `is_session_player`, and `create_token` writes game_cards rows whose token-ness lives on `cards.is_token`, not on the row.)
- **Filter / multi-mana lands already work end-to-end (verified 2026-06-25).** Cards like Darkwater Catacombs (`{1},{T}: Add {U}{B}`), Skycloud Expanse, Mossfire Valley, Sungrass Prairie, Desolate Mire are FIXED two-colour lands (NOT "choose from a subset" — current Scryfall/DB oracle is "Add {X}{Y}", and their scripts are two add_mana effects). Flooded Grove is the one true filter land (`{T}: Add {C}` + `{G/U},{T}: Add {G}{G}/{G}{U}/{U}{U}`), modelled as 4 separate abilities (one button per combination). The engine `activate_mana_ability` already pays a `mana`/`pay_life` activation cost (via pay_mana_cost, which handles `{G/U}` hybrid with a default choice) and adds ALL add_mana effects. The UI: **CardActionSheet** (components/controller/CardActionSheet.tsx ~L955) renders an ability with a non-tap cost OR >1 produced colour as ONE atomic button → `onActivateManaAbility(card.id, index)` (index is the full activated_abilities index, mapped before filter at L136). A simple tap on the board card opens this sheet because `getAutoTapMana` returns null for multi-cost/multi-ability sources. So NO schema `choices` / `p_chosen_colors` array was ever needed. Empirically tested both cards against local DB. **Known limitation:** the cast-time `autoPay` only taps cost-free single-colour sources (`getAutoTapMana`), so it will NOT auto-tap a filter land — the player must tap it manually via the sheet first. Latent (unrelated) bug to watch: ControllerListV5 `tapForMana`'s engine path computes the index with `findIndex(a => a === ability)` against a FRESH normalize() tree, so it always yields -1→0; only correct for index-0 abilities (sheet's onActivateManaAbility path is unaffected — it carries the real index).
- **Optional ("up to one target …") triggered-ability targets (mig 326, 2026-06-24).** Previously enqueue_triggered_ability marked EVERY trigger with a target_type as required (`v_requires_target := v_target_type is not null`), so a "you may choose up to one target" trigger soft-locked: resolve_top_of_stack → handle_triggered_ability raises "Triggered ability requires a target" when a legal target exists but none was chosen, rolls back, and every subsequent pass re-raises. Fix spans 5 places: (1) **enqueue_triggered_ability** reads `optional:true` on the targeting effect (found via trigger_effect_target_type) → `target_required=false` + new `target_optional=true` in the payload, and still emits target_type/controller/count/filter so a picker can be offered; the no-legal-target fizzle guard only applies to REQUIRED targets. (2) **apply_trigger_effects** — a targeted effect whose `target_card_id` is null now NO-OPs (skips) instead of calling apply_targeted_triggered_ability_effects with null (covers optional-declined AND required-fizzle). (3) **choose_triggered_ability_creature_target** accepts target_required OR target_optional (it used to reject non-required). (4) **controller** (ControllerListV5 TargetedTriggerPrompt): shows the picker for target_optional too, with a **Skip** button wired to onPassPriority (threaded through the board component). (5) **bot-runner** resolveTriggerTargets picks targets for optional triggers too (so the bot still uses Obuun's animate). Mark a script effect optional with `"optional": true` (same flag apply_trigger_effects already used for pick-effect min 0). Obuun's begin-combat animate is now optional. Tests: tests/feature/optional-trigger-target.test.ts. See [[bug-trigger-target-softlock-bot-obuun]].

- **Controller state sync = realtime subscriptions + full reload (2026-06-24).** `lib/game/use-controller-game-state.ts` `loadControllerState` runs an **18-query `Promise.all`** and is triggered by ~12 `postgres_changes` subscriptions (session-scoped) for one game. Three perf fixes applied: (1) **debounce** the subscription handler (`RELOAD_DEBOUNCE_MS=60`) so the burst of table-change events one action emits (a cast touches game_cards + game_stack_items + game_turn_state + …) collapses into a single reload instead of 18 queries × N events; (2) the **fallback poll** (`enableFallbackRefresh`/`fallbackRefreshIntervalMs` from ./dev, env `NEXT_PUBLIC_FALLBACK_REFRESH_MS=2000`) now only runs WHILE realtime is disconnected (`realtimeConnected` flag set in `.subscribe` status callback); (3) **dropped the global `cards` subscription** (the catalog has no session_id so it can't be filtered, is static during play, and fired a game-wide reload on every catalog import/edit) and **added a `session_id` filter to the `game_combat_blockers` subscription** (it was global too). The board hook `use-board-game-state.ts` had the SAME pattern and got the SAME three fixes (debounce `REFRESH_DEBOUNCE_MS=60`, poll-only-when-disconnected, dropped global `cards` sub + filtered `game_combat_blockers`). For couch-play scale this load is fine on local/hosted; the redundant multi-event reloads + idle 2s poll were the real waste. `refresh` (returned to actions for post-mutation reload) stays the immediate `loadControllerState`, not the debounced one.

- **Lobby deck flow: "spawn" = ready, and it's reversible now (2026-06-23).** A player picks a deck (select) then locks it in — `spawn_deck_for_session` materialises the deck template into per-game `game_cards` (library + commander to command zone) and that IS the "ready" signal (`getSpawnedDeckOwnerIds` → `readyPlayerIds`, derived, no DB column). `spawn_deck_for_session` HARD-BLOCKS a second spawn ("You already have a deck in this session"). UX feedback: "spawn" is jargon for ready, and you couldn't switch decks. Fixed: button renamed **"Lock in deck"** (and modal/status wording de-jargoned), and a **"Change deck"** action added via new RPC **`clear_deck_from_session(p_session_id)`** (mig 324) — deletes the caller's `game_cards`, refusing unless session status = 'open' (lobby; 'locked' = started, set by start_game_session which also inserts game_turn_state). Client wrapper `clearDeckFromSession` in actions.ts; lobby disables the deck `<select>` + swaps the button to "Change deck" when `iAmReady`. Session statuses are only **'open' / 'locked' / 'finished'** (start_game_session flips open→locked). Tests: tests/feature/change-deck.test.ts (note: an RPC that RAISES aborts the withRolledBackTx transaction, so don't run a query after `assert.rejects` — the rejection is the assertion).

- **Running the phone PWA against LOCAL Supabase via cloudflared (2026-06-23).** The phone loads the app over the cloudflared https tunnel (app.dweemo.nl → localhost:3000, named tunnel 28b93d77…, config at ~/.cloudflared/config.yml). Two non-obvious requirements: (1) **NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_URL must be a publicly reachable https URL**, NOT http://127.0.0.1:54321 — on the phone 127.0.0.1 is the phone, and http-from-https is mixed-content blocked → 'Failed to fetch' at signInWithPassword. Fix: tunnel kong too (ingress supabase.dweemo.nl → http://localhost:54321) + DNS route + set NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_URL=https://supabase.dweemo.nl, then restart cloudflared AND `npm run dev` (NEXT_PUBLIC_* bakes at dev-server start). Jordy uses the **public link (app.dweemo.nl) on desktop too**, so one tunnel URL serves everyone and lib/supabase/client.ts stays plain `process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_URL`. (An origin-based split — local URL on localhost, tunnel on public hosts — was tried and reverted as unnecessary given that.) NOTE: routing the desktop browser through the tunnel can give occasional 'Failed to fetch' on the controller's frequent polling even though curl/CORS are fine; if that becomes annoying, loading the app on plain localhost (swap NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_URL back to http://127.0.0.1:54321) avoids the tunnel hop. The local bot talks to pg directly on :54322, unaffected. (2) **PWA install needs manifest/sw/icons reachable WITHOUT auth** — they sit behind the app's Cloudflare Access OTP app and the browser fetches them cookieless → Access login HTML instead of the file → no install. Fix: a SECOND path-scoped Access self-hosted app (destinations app.dweemo.nl/manifest.webmanifest, /sw.js, /icon*, /screenshot* — max 5 destinations so use wildcards) with policy Action=Bypass/Everyone; Access matches most-specific path so it wins for those files. sw.js does NO caching, so stale bundles are browser/PWA HTTP cache → reinstall / clear site data. See [[bug-pwa-login-failed-to-fetch-localhost-supabase]] [[bug-pwa-install-blocked-by-access]]. Also: two local Supabase projects can't share the default ports (54321-54327) — a stray 'Jordy' project once stole 54322 → bot hit the wrong db [[bug-bot-runner-wrong-supabase-port-collision]].

- **Adding a combat keyword to the engine — the full recipe (2026-06-22, Defender, mig 323).** Keywords are NOT stored as a column flag; they're rows in `game_continuous_effects` (effect_type = the keyword), read by per-keyword accessors `public.card_has_<kw>(session_id, card_id)`. The evergreen combat set is already complete: declare_blocker enforces flying/reach + protection + intimidate; advance_step enforces menace; declare_attacker does vigilance (no-tap) + haste; resolve_combat_damage does first/double strike + deathtouch + trample + infect + wither; apply_damage_to_player/creature do lifelink (mig 283). To add a NEW keyword (e.g. defender) you touch FOUR things: (1) **accessor** — new `card_has_<kw>.sql` cloned from the mig-200 family (card_has_flying form: checks game_continuous_effects with creature_type/exclude_source/token_only filters + is_session_player); (2) **register_card_continuous_effects.sql** — add the keyword to the `continuous_effects` type whitelist AND its source-default `affected` list AND the printed-keyword `case` whitelist (~line 257); (3) **the CHECK constraint** `game_continuous_effects_effect_type_check` (latest def in mig 303 pacify) — must list the new effect_type or inserts throw [[bug-defender-effect-type-check]]; (4) the **enforcement site** (declare_attacker/declare_blocker/resolve_combat_damage). Workflow: edit functions_src, `node scripts/new-migration.mjs <name> <fn>...`, then HAND-ADD non-function DDL (the constraint) at the top of the generated migration, then `npm run test:db:setup && npm test`. GOTCHA: the printed-keyword path reads `cards.keywords` (the COLUMN, from Scryfall import), but the test seeder never populates that column — so test fixtures must express a keyword as a `continuous_effects:[{type,affected:'source',source_zone_required:'battlefield'}]` entry, like Menace Brute Test [[bug-defender-keywords-source]].
- **Bot combat is keyword-aware (2026-06-22).** `lib/game/bot-brain.ts` `Creature` now carries an optional `keywords` ({flying,reach,trample,menace,deathtouch,firstStrike,doubleStrike}) — optional so the older P/T-only tests/callers keep working. The core test is `freeKills(blocker, attacker)` (attacker dies, blocker survives), which folds in strike order (first/double strike deals in the FS step) and deathtouch (any ≥1 damage is lethal). `decideAttacks` adds evasion (flier unblockable without flying/reach), menace (unblockable vs <2 blockers), and defensive reserves (hold back the highest-toughness creature against a lethal swing-back when not attacking for lethal — gated on the new optional `opts.myLife`). `decideBlocks` adds evasion + menace (needs two blockers) + trample (a chump only soaks blocker toughness; excess leaks, so the lethal-chump loop may need extra blockers). DB keywords come from **`public.card_has_<kw>($session, $card_id)` accessor functions** (flying/reach/trample/menace/deathtouch/first_strike/double_strike — signature is (session_id, card_id)→bool; only `card_has_lifelink` has a functions_src file, the rest live inline in migrations). The runner (`scripts/bot-runner.mjs`) selects these via a shared `KEYWORD_COLS` snippet + `toCreature` mapper (the declareBlocks attackers query is the exception — it keys off `ca.attacker_card_id`, not a `gc` alias, so its keyword cols are spelled out). Tests in `tests/unit/bot-brain.test.ts` (30 total). No lookahead yet.

- **Local TEST DB and PLAY DB are now SEPARATE (2026-06-18).** They used to be the same Postgres (`:54322/postgres`): the app/Supabase API uses `postgres`, and the test harness ALSO defaulted there — so `npm run test:db:setup` (which `drop schema public cascade`) wiped the play catalog/decks/games, and a test run reseeded only the 353 `% Test` fixtures (that's why the local DB kept looking "empty"). FIX: the harness (`tests/harness/db.ts`) and `setup-local-test-db.mjs` now default to a dedicated **`leyline_test`** database (override via `TEST_DATABASE_URL`). setup auto-creates it and installs stubs the GoTrue/`postgres` DB normally provides but a fresh DB lacks: `auth.uid()` (reads `request.jwt.claims->>'sub'`), a minimal `auth.users(id,email,raw_user_meta_data)` (FK target; 01_relax_fks drops the FKs), and the `supabase_realtime` publication. The auth schema is rebuilt each run (it survives a public-schema drop, so `if not exists` kept a stale shape). A footgun guard refuses to rebuild `postgres` without `--force-play-db`. `npm test` is otherwise harmless (rolled-back txns + additive fixture seed). To restore the play DB after a wipe: **`npm run seed:local-play`** (import:cards → seed-scripts-local → deck:seed-precons). Verified: 530 engine tests pass on leyline_test.
- **Restricted ("spend only") mana model (mig 320, 2026-06-18).** Cards like Haven of the Spirit Dragon, Ixalli's Lorekeeper, Unclaimed Territory, Secluded Courtyard, Vedalken Engineer produce mana that may only pay matching casts/abilities. Modelled server-authoritatively: an `add_mana` script effect with a `restriction` object (`{spell_type_line?, ability_source_type_line?, commander?}`) routes its mana to a NEW per-player column **`game_players.restricted_mana jsonb`** (array of `{color,amount,...restriction}`) instead of `mana_pool`. **`pay_mana_cost` gained a 7th param `p_pay_context jsonb`** (`{kind:'cast'|'ability', type_line, is_commander}`); it folds ELIGIBLE restricted mana into the working pool, runs the normal algorithm, then deducts spend RESTRICTED-FIRST (use-it-or-lose-it). Every cast/ability call site passes context (cast_card_from_hand/cast_spell_effect/cast_commander/put_action_on_stack = `kind:'cast'`; activate_ability = `kind:'ability'`). `cycle_card`/`turn_manifest_up` pass NOTHING (null) so restricted mana correctly can't pay them. `clear_mana_pool_for_step` empties `restricted_mana` each step like the open pool. Eligibility: `commander:true`→context.is_commander; else cast→`spell_type_line` null or `type_line ILIKE %x%`; else ability→`ability_source_type_line` present and matches. **Chosen-type cards reuse `$chosen`**: the script stores `"spell_type_line":"$chosen"` + an ETB `choose_creature_type` trigger; `submit_decision` already bakes the chosen type into `game_cards.copied_script` (text-replaces `"$chosen"`). Client: `selectFirstManaAbility` falls back to an `any`/`commander` producer for a chosen colour ([[bug-913]]); `tapForMana` routes any ability whose `add_mana` has a `restriction` through `activate_mana_ability` (like the sacrifice branch) so the engine writes restricted mana; `RestrictedManaDisplay` shows it tagged in the StatusBar. **ALWAYS verify each card's real oracle_text before assigning a restriction** — Drover/Atzocan/Relic of Legends/Progenitor's Icon turned out to have NO "spend only" clause; Haven's is cast-only (no ability clause), contrary to first assumption. Known v1 limit: client `autoPay`/`planAutoTap` only sees the open pool, so it may tap one extra source; the server still consumes restricted mana first. Tests: `tests/feature/restricted-mana.test.ts` (RC1-8 direct pay_mana_cost branches + RM1-3 Haven end-to-end). [[bug-restricted-mana-deferred]]

- **AI CPU test bot = `scripts/bot-runner.mjs` (2026-06-17).** LOCAL-only test opponent. Talks to local Postgres (:54322) via direct `pg`, satisfies `auth.uid()` by setting `request.jwt.claims` per call (like tests/harness/db.ts) but COMMITS each call in its own tx (the harness rolls back). IN-APP SELECTION (mig 315, 2026-06-17): the lobby has an **"Add CPU"** button → `add_bot_to_session(p_session_id)` RPC (seats a synthetic player flagged `is_bot` on `game_session_players`, life per format, autopass {op,own}, and seeds a shuffled vanilla library directly — basic land + cheapest script-free creature). `get_session_players` labels `is_bot` rows "CPU 🤖". Drive with **`node scripts/bot-runner.mjs --watch`** (primary): it polls for `is_bot` seats in `status='locked'` sessions and plays each via `tick(session, bot)`. Workflow: run `--watch` once → in-app Add CPU → Start. add_bot_to_session requires the caller be a session member (so --session manual mode impersonates seat-1 creator to call it). NOTE: `game_turn_state` has `lands_played_this_turn` but NOT `land_play_limit` (computed; default to 1). All LOCAL-only (bot uuid has no auth.users row; hosted FKs forbid it). Legacy: `node scripts/bot-runner.mjs --session <id>` — human creates the session in the app (must be pointed at LOCAL Supabase + logged in locally, since every gameplay RPC is `auth.uid()`-scoped and the host browser canNOT act for another seat). Bot: join_game_session → spawn a generated vanilla deck (basic land + cheapest script-free creature, queried from catalog since names differ per DB; spawn with `p_enforce_legality:false`) → set_autopass {op,own} so the server chains its empty passes → loop: keep_opening_hand([]) / auto-resolve its pending decisions / on its main play a land + cast ≤2 creatures (once per main via `lastMainKey`) / on declare_attackers attack with all untapped / else pass_priority. It's a TEST bot: it CHEATS mana (writes its own game_players.mana_pool). (It no longer clears summoning sickness — see the engine fix below; it now attacks legally with creatures that entered a prior turn.) Verified end-to-end vs the live local DB (reached turn 7, cast + attacked, no soft-lock). Decision auto-resolver covers scry/surveil/choose_mode/player/color/creature_type/confirm + a generic "pick min_choices" fallback; exotic types (divide_damage/vote/pay_x_mana_damage) are logged, not handled — add as they appear. CONFIRMED + FIXED (mig 314, 2026-06-17): `handle_cast_permanent` (the stack handler resolving any permanent SPELL to the battlefield) never stamped `entered_battlefield_turn_number`, so EVERY hard-cast creature stayed NULL → permanently summoning-sick (declare_attacker: `coalesce(entered,turn)>=turn`). Tokens/effect creatures use move_card_to_zone/create_token which stamp it, so only SOME creatures were stuck. Fix stamps `entered = coalesce(turn_number, entered, 0)` on the battlefield UPDATE. Param type qualified `public.game_stack_items` for the migration search_path. `handle_cast_permanent` previously had NO functions_src file (inline in an old migration) — now canonical at `supabase/functions_src/handle_cast_permanent.sql`. Full suite 1559/1559 green. See [[bug-cast-permanent-entered]].

- **AI CPU now plays a REAL deck (mig 319, 2026-06-18).** `add_bot_to_session` previously seeded a vanilla pile (22 land + 18 cheap creature). It now seeds a shared **precon** (`is_precon=true`; in Commander, one with a `commander_card_id` → seated in the command zone, library excludes it), mirroring `spawn_deck_for_session` but for the bot's uuid. Vanilla is the fallback when no precon exists. New optional `p_deck_id` (caller-owned or precon) pins a specific deck. The signature changed `(uuid)`→`(uuid, uuid default null)`, so mig 319 DROPs the old 1-arg overload first (else a one-arg call is ambiguous). **LOCAL-only** (bot uuid has no auth row); applied to local + PostgREST reloaded; NOT pushed to hosted. Smoke (rolled-back): bot gets 99-card library + commander. The bot NOW CASTS its commander: `decideMainPlays` takes an optional `commander {id, manaValue}` (manaValue = base + 2×`command_zone_casts` tax) and casts it FIRST when affordable; the runner reads the command-zone row and calls `cast_commander(session, card)` (pays from the cheated pool, incl. tax). MULTIPLE CPUs work out of the box: the lobby "Add CPU" button is repeatable, each `add_bot_to_session` call seats the next seat with its own precon, and `--watch` drives every `is_bot` seat (smoke seated 2 bots, each with a commander). No engine player cap. Requires the local catalog to be scripted (see basic-land/[[bug-local-cards-no-script]] seeder) so real cards actually function.
- **Opponent cards are now tap-to-zoom in V5 (2026-06-18).** `OpponentBoardOverlay` rendered plain `MotionCard`s with no handler. Each board/GY/exile card is now a button → `CardZoomOverlay` (z-[55], above the sheet's z-40). Adapter `toZoomCard` maps a `BoardCard`/zone-item to the `ControllerCard` shape CardZoomOverlay needs (`cards.{image_url,type_line,power_toughness}`; no oracle_text on BoardCard — the image carries the text). `GameZone` had to be added to the types import. Your OWN GY/exile zones (`MyZonesSheet`) also got tap-to-zoom (2026-06-18).
- **Casting from non-hand zones: the engine gates on `v_source_zone` per-RPC, and `play_from_exile` is the exile permission (2026-06-18).** `cast_card_from_hand` accepts source zone in `('hand','graveyard','exile','library')` and validates each (graveyard→`cast_from_graveyard` perm/flashback, exile→`play_from_exile` perm, library→top + `cast_from_library_top`). It ALREADY fully handled exile permanents/lands (mana + perm + zone). BUT the NON-PERMANENT spell RPCs — `cast_spell_effect` (spell_effect/draw/modal plans) and `put_action_on_stack` (damage/pump/multi/permanent_effect/divided_damage/fight) — historically charged mana and moved-to-graveyard ONLY when `v_source_zone = 'hand'`, so an instant/sorcery cast from exile would be FREE and never leave exile. **Mig 321 (cast_from_exile)** changed both to: require the `play_from_exile` perm for an exile source, pay the printed cost for `v_source_zone in ('hand','exile')`, and send spent non-permanents to the graveyard. **Client**: `getPlayableFromExileIds` (data.ts) loads the player's `play_from_exile` perms (effect_type, flatten `payload.card_ids`); `useControllerGameState` exposes `playableFromExileIds`; `MyZonesSheet` exile tab badges castable cards "PLAY" and routes them through `onCardTap`→`CardActionSheet`; `CardActionSheet` got a `playableFromExile` prop and, when true for an exile card (`castableFromExile`), sets local `zone='hand'` AND a `planBase` with `zone:'hand'` so `canCastHandSpell` (which checks `card.zone==='hand'`) lights up the cast UI. NOTE: `selectedCardLive` re-fetches the card from `cards` by id, so you CANNOT masquerade the zone via `setSelectedCard({...card,zone:'hand'})` — must thread a flag. Verified by AT4/AT5 in atsushi.test.ts. Still un-handled from exile (rare): cast_modal_spell / cast_scry / cast_surveil / cast_fight (same `='hand'` pattern, not yet patched). See [[bug-929]].
- **Bot brain = pure TS heuristic (`lib/game/bot-brain.ts`, 2026-06-17).** SUPERSEDES the bot's inline decision logic described above. Pure, side-effect-free, unit-tested (`tests/unit/bot-brain.test.ts`, 15 cases) like `shouldAutoPass`. Functions: `shouldMulligan` (mull <2 or >5 lands, stop after 2), `chooseBottom`, `decideMainPlays(hand, availableMana, canPlayLand)` → land + cheapest-first casts within REAL mana (untapped land count) so it sequences on-curve even though the runner still cheats the *payment*, `decideAttacks` (attack unless a blocker free-kills: kills it AND survives; alpha for lethal into empty board), `decideBlocks` (value blocks first, then chump-to-survive only when unblocked dmg ≥ life). `bot-runner.mjs` is now just the I/O shell calling these → it imports the `.ts`, so RUN IT VIA **`node --import tsx scripts/bot-runner.mjs`** (or `npm run bot -- --watch`). Combat inputs use SQL helpers `public.card_effective_power(session, card_id)` / `card_effective_toughness(...)` (counters/effects folded); life is `game_session_players.life_total`; mana value is `cards.cmc`; combat tables `game_combat_assignments` (attacker/defending_player/blocker) + `game_combat_blockers`; blocks via `declare_blocker(session, blocker, attacker)` during step `declare_blockers` when the defender has priority. Runner now ALSO declares blocks (new `declareBlocks`) when `!myTurn && step='declare_blockers'`. Per-action once-per-turn fences via `did(action, session, bot, scope)`. Mulligan IS wired (`resolveMulligan`): `shouldMulligan` → `mulligan_hand(session)` (increments `game_session_players.mulligans`, bounded — keeps at ≥2) or on keep `chooseBottom(hand, required)` → `keep_opening_hand(session, bottomIds)` where required = London `mulligans` / Commander `max(mulligans-1, 0)` (read `game_sessions.format`). NOT YET live-verified (needs local Supabase up + a seated bot).
- **Card behaviours live in `public.cards.script` (jsonb), NOT in the schema (2026-06-18).** The engine *mechanisms* (trigger/effect/cast handlers) are all in the migrations → fully present in any DB built from them. But per-card behaviour is a `script` on the catalog row, resolved from two source files: `docs/commander-decks/card-scripts.json` (503 real-name overrides) and `tests/fixtures/test-cards.json` (353 fixtures, 324 scripted, named `<Name> Test`). `deck:upsert` pushes scripts to the **HOSTED** catalog only. The **test/local DB**: `test:db:setup` seeds NO catalog; the harness `ensureTestCards()` seeds only the fixture rows. **GOTCHA:** after `import:cards` LOCAL has all 31802 rows but ~empty scripts (scripts never auto-reach local); and the real card name `Haven of the Spirit Dragon` ≠ the fixture `Haven of the Spirit Dragon Test`, so a real decklist imports the real-named row which had NO behaviour. FIX = `scripts/seed-scripts-local.mjs` (localhost-guarded): applies card-scripts.json + stripped fixtures + BASIC-LAND mana scripts onto local rows by name. **Even BASIC LANDS need a `script`** — there is NO subtype→mana synthesis anywhere: both the client (`selectFirstManaAbility`/`getAutoTapMana` read `cards.script`) and the engine (`activate_mana_ability` reads `effective_script`, which does NOT inject basics) require an `activated_abilities` mana ability. Hosted basics got theirs from archived seed mig 202605010051 (`{actions:[add_mana],triggers:[manual_tap]}` v1), which `test:db:setup` does NOT apply; import:cards leaves them empty → local basics couldn't tap. The seeder now injects v2 basic+snow scripts (Island→U, …). Gap analysis: 408/503 overrides have no dedicated engine feature-test (schema-validated only) — list in `.wolf/scripts-without-fixture.txt`. See [[bug-local-cards-no-script]].
- **Trigger target type-line filter (mig 310, 2026-06-15).** Triggered-ability targets can now be narrowed by type line via an effect's `target_filter: { type_line_any: [...] }` (OR over substrings) or `{ type_line: "X" }`. Plumbing: `trigger_effects_target_filter` extracts it → `enqueue_triggered_ability` stamps `target_filter` into the stack payload AND uses it in a filter-aware has-legal-target check (so a "choose target" trigger with no legal target is NOT enqueued — no soft-lock); `choose_triggered_ability_creature_target` rejects a mismatched pick; the client (`matchesTargetFilter` in ControllerListV4 — used by both `mustChooseTriggerTarget` and `TargetedTriggerPrompt`) only offers matching permanents. Helper `card_type_line_matches_filter(type_line, filter)` is shared (pure text ILIKE-any). First user: Opportunistic Dragon ("Human or artifact"). `gain_control` has no strict schema object (catch-all/passthrough), so adding `target_filter` to the script needed NO schema change. NOTE: `choose_triggered_ability_creature_target` is now canonical in functions_src. **Catalog upsert still pending** — card-scripts.json change needs `deck:upsert` to the hosted catalog to take effect in real games (test fixture covers tests).
- **Auto-pass early-game pacing (2026-06-14).** The op/own/stk/rsp auto-pass engine (`ControllerListV4.tsx`) was fully built but **dormant**: `AUTOPASS_OFF` was the load fallback for fresh sessions, so nobody got the benefit unless they opened the popover — that, not missing features, is why "early game feels slow." Fix: `AUTOPASS_DEFAULT = {op,own,stk: true, rsp: false}` returned only when there's no stored value (explicit stored prefs, incl. the v1 `'1'` migration, are still respected). Second cost is the **sequential pod pass**: priority is one player at a time and each opponent's client waits a beat then passes, so an empty step ≈ beat×(n−1) + network. Beat is now adaptive: `AUTOPASS_BEAT_EMPTY_MS=250` (empty stack) / `AUTOPASS_BEAT_STACK_MS=700` (object on stack, give it a visible beat). The "correct" structural fix (server-side chained pod auto-skip in `pass_priority`) is unbuilt — client still does N hops.
- **Client decision-rendering is at FULL 28/28 parity (verified 2026-06-14).** `docs/client-coverage-audit.md` is STALE — it claims "9 of 28 decision types handled," but `ControllerListV4.tsx` now renders all 28: a `CARD_PICK_DECISIONS` Set routes the 13 card-pick types to `CardPickBody`, and the 5 once-missing bodies exist (`ChooseWordBody` for choose_creature_type+vote, `ChooseColorBody`, `DivideDamageBody`, `PayXDamageBody`). The engine's decision vocabulary = the 28 types `submit_decision` branches on; `choose_up_to`/`job_select`/`saga_chapters` are NOT decisions (script field / effect-dispatch type / card-script field). **CardPickBody contract (verified):** options `[{game_card_id, name, …extra ignored}]`, submit `{chosen:[game_card_id]}`, bounds via min/max_choices — every engine park site builds `jsonb_build_object('game_card_id', id, 'name', c.name, …)` so labels always populate. Don't re-do "Tier 1 decision rendering" from the audit; it's done. **The audit's Tier-2 "invisible state" list is now ALSO essentially closed** (audit is badly stale): monarch (👑 on opponent pills + 74 refs), attack_tax (⛔), animated-lands, and poison (☠ with ≥3 corrupted highlight on player pills, lethal@10 in judge tools) are all surfaced. **Attachments DONE 2026-06-14**: `game_cards.attached_to` (set by `attach_permanent`, mig 134) is now plumbed into `ControllerCard` (getControllerCards select + type) and rendered on the controller battlefield — 📎N amber badge on a host (tooltip lists attachments), 🔗 sky badge on the Equipment/Aura (tooltip names the host). `getControllerCards` is owner-scoped, but the 🔗 host-name tooltip resolves cross-owner hosts anyway: `ControllerListV4`'s `cardNameById` is built from `boardCards` (whole-table snapshot) with `battlefieldCards` merged as fallback (DONE 2026-06-22, was an edge case). **The big-screen board IS built** — `components/GameBoard.tsx` (NOT `components/board/`, which is just chrome) renders per-seat battlefields (focus/grid/minimap variants) via `useBoardGameState` + `buildBoardSeats`. Board badges DONE 2026-06-14: a shared `SeatStatusBadges` (monarch 👑 + poison ☠ with ≥3 corrupted/≥10 lethal) in all 3 seat panels, reading board-loaded data (turnState + player.counters). Board-side TODO needing data plumbing: attachments (`attached_to` not in `getBoardCards`), attack-tax (no board query), animated lands (`animated` not selected). **LESSON: this codebase is consistently MORE built than docs/anatomy suggest — verify by reading the actual component before declaring a gap or a stub (burned 4× this session: auto-pass, decisions, cost-picks, board view).**
- **Engine-vs-UI scan results (2026-06-14).** Diffed 102 authenticated RPCs vs 78 client-called + checked state/decisions/keywords. **Essentially everything is wired** — the 67 granted-but-uncalled RPCs are nearly all internal engine helpers (`apply_*`/`fire_*`/`card_has_*`/`resolve_*`, called via `perform`/`select` inside other RPCs). `order_pending_triggers` (APNAP) is auto-invoked by `resolve_top_of_stack` (not a gap). **Genuine UNSURFACED gaps, prioritized:** (1) **HIGH — commander damage**: `game_commander_damage` (mig 137: session/defender/source_card_id/damage, player-readable; 21-from-one-commander lethal server-side) is NEVER loaded client-side — invisible loss condition. (2) LOW/MED — `set_commander_redirect` (command-zone-vs-graveyard preference, unsurfaced). (3) LOW/MED — `commander_deck_legality` (no deck-editor legality feedback). (4) LOW — `cleanup_finished_session` (housekeeping). NOT gaps: energy/experience counters (shown generically via `formatCounterBag` on current player), keyword badges (shared.ts KEYWORD map), manifest-flip/amass (wired).
- **Pod auto-skip — server-side priority chaining (mig 309, 2026-06-14).** `pass_priority` is now canonical in `functions_src/pass_priority.sql` (was baseline, last def mig 140). The priority model: `advance_step` seats priority on the active player and resets `priority_pass_count=0`; each pass increments it; `>= count(living players)` → resolve top of stack OR `advance_step`. The slowness was N separate `pass_priority` RPCs (one client hop + realtime push per opponent) for every empty round. Fix: persist each player's auto-pass intent on `game_session_players.autopass_settings` (jsonb `{op,own,stk,rsp}`, default `'{}'`), synced from the controller's localStorage via the new `set_autopass_settings(session, settings)` RPC (security-definer, updates `auth.uid()`'s row). `pass_priority` then chains: **only when the stack is empty AND step ≠ declare_blockers**, after the caller's pass it walks downstream seats and counts any whose settings say they'd auto-pass here (opponent: `op && !rsp`; active player: `own && empty-step`), stopping at the first who wouldn't (→ hand them priority) or completing the round (→ advance/resolve). Faithful to the client decision — never skips a player the client wouldn't have. Default `'{}'` = never skipped (old behavior), so chaining is opt-in via sync. Non-empty stack keeps per-client stk/rsp windows. Loop is bounded by `pass_count >= player_count`. Tests: `tests/feature/pod-auto-skip.test.ts` (PA1–PA5); harness gained `s.setAutoPass(seat, blob)` + `s.turnStep()`. `dev_set_turn_state` resets pass_count to 0.
- **Decks model + precons.** The `decks` table (id, owner_id, name, list_data jsonb of card_ids, commander_card_id, created_by, **is_precon**) is owner-scoped by RLS. Precons (mig 308) are shared rows: `is_precon=true`, `owner_id` null (column made nullable), exposed to all via the "Anyone can read precon decks" SELECT policy. `getUserDecks` (own decks, created_by/owner filter) powers DeckManager; `getPreconDecks` (is_precon filter) is unioned into the lobby dropdown as a separate "Precons" optgroup. `spawn_deck_for_session` + `commander_deck_legality` lookups are relaxed to `(owner_id = auth.uid() OR is_precon)`. Precon decklists live as text in `docs/commander-decks/*.txt`; `scripts/seed-precon-decks.mjs` (service role, dry-run default, `--apply` to write) resolves names→catalog ids and seeds only catalog-complete decks. The lobby spawns precons with legality enforcement OFF (curated/trusted; a subset catalog can leave them shy of 100). NOTE: hosted needs mig 308 applied before the seeding script runs.
- **Mana is a POOL model, casting does NOT auto-tap.** Tapping a source (`add_mana_from_card` for basics, `activate_mana_ability` for scripted producers) fills `game_players.mana_pool`; `pay_mana_cost` then DRAINS the pool and throws "Not enough X mana" if short. So the controller must fill the pool BEFORE the cast RPC. Client "auto-pay" (`lib/game/auto-tap.ts` `planAutoTap`) does this: safe-greedy, taps only untapped single-colour cost-free sources (`getAutoTapMana` in ControllerListV4 classifies them), pool-first then coloured-pip-first to avoid stranding, returns null when it can't be met unambiguously (multi-colour/any/extra-cost sources, {X} costs) → leaves those to manual tapping. Wired into every mana-paying cast action in ControllerListV4 (castSpell/castAura/spellEffect/damage/counter/etc.), skipping commander-tax and adventure/alt-cost paths.
- **Exposing the dev server on a new public hostname requires adding it to `allowedDevOrigins` in next.config.ts** — otherwise login "silently" fails: signInWithPassword succeeds but Next blocks the post-login `router.refresh()` RSC request from the foreign origin, so the page just reloads on /auth/login with no error. Already whitelisted: LAN IPs, `*.ts.net` (tailscale), `app.dweemo.nl`/`*.dweemo.nl` (Cloudflare Tunnel). Config changes need a dev-server restart. (bug-727)
- **"Cloudflare one-time password / OTP redirect" = Cloudflare ACCESS (Zero Trust), NOT Supabase email OTP (2026-06-15).** `app.dweemo.nl`/`dweemo.nl` are fronted by Cloudflare Access; the email One-Time PIN login panel is the gate IN FRONT of the Next app. None of this is in the repo — `.cloudflared/config.yml` is pure tunnel ingress (hostname→localhost:3000); Access applications/policies live only in the Zero Trust dashboard. **bug-NNN: new users weren't redirected to the OTP panel because the Access policy Action was "Bypass" (Include: Everyone).** Bypass explicitly skips auth AND short-circuits (a matching Bypass wins even if an Allow exists below). Fix = change the policy to **Allow** (Include Everyone or tester emails). Gotcha: testers who got in during the Bypass window keep a valid `CF_Authorization` cookie until it expires — verify in incognito. SEPARATE, still-unfixed issue found same session: the app's own Supabase email-OTP login is mis-wired (signUp `emailRedirectTo:/protected` + reset `/auth/update-password` never route through `/auth/confirm`'s token_hash `verifyOtp`, and `@supabase/ssr` defaults to PKCE `?code=` which nothing exchanges; proxy.ts also strips auth params off `/protected` by redirecting unauthed users to /auth/login). Don't conflate the two.
- The hosted card-script upsert scopes to a DECKLIST FILE (default docs/commander-decks/next-deck.txt; pass another path as the first arg). After any in-app precon/deck import, re-run it with THAT deck file — imports create fresh printing rows with null scripts. DFC catalog rows use the full "Front // Back" name.

- **Dragons deck COMPLETE (2026-06-12, migs 239-252)**: all 92 cards (86 implemented + 6 as-is). New primitives this arc: token/become copies, modal splice, mana_value, X activation costs, shuffle_into_library, pump_all-from-programs, pay-X-mana damage, MV-capped bounce, cast_from_library_top, mode-gated modal permanents (`` bake), beginning_of_main, add_mana-from-triggers, exile_until_nonland, dragons_combat_damage event (p_extra on enqueue/fire_card_triggers), command-zone borrow, hideaway, goad, forced-defender pins, dethrone guard, EXTRA COMBAT (game_turn_state.extra_combats), manifest (manifested marker + turn_manifest_up), council's-dilemma vote chains.
- **Vote/each-player decision chains**: park one decision per player, accumulate state on the STACK ITEM payload (votes/free_votes), only the last submit resumes the program — the park_edict_sacrifice pattern generalized (Selvala, mig 252).
- **Never script-flag a row you insert OUTSIDE register_card_continuous_effects** (bug-635): something re-registers after stack resolution, and register deletes every `registered_from_card_script=true` row for the source that isn't derived from the script — a hand-inserted flagged row vanishes. Insert plain rows and clean them up in your own revert/leave path instead.
- **become_copy (mig 240)**: card_id flip + copy_original_card_id; reverts BOTH on leaving the battlefield (revert_copy_before_leave BEFORE-UPDATE trigger — AFTER triggers see the reverted original, so dies-triggers are the printed card's) and at end step for until-EOT copies (advance_step). Both paths delete every effect row the card sources before re-registering.
- **game_cards.copied_script already existed pre-copy-primitive** (baseline mig 044): `effective_script = coalesce(copied_script, cards.script)`, plus a `set_card_copied_script` RPC. Mig 239 builds on it: token copies carry the source's copied_script; choose_creature_type bakes a chosen type into copied_script wherever the script holds the `"$chosen"` placeholder (Reflections of Littjara).
- **Token copies are game-level tokens** (mig 239): `game_cards.is_token` marks a copy whose catalog row is NOT a token; cease_token_if_off_battlefield / put_in_graveyard nontoken tally / fire_watcher nontoken filter all check BOTH flags. `create_copy_token(session, recipient, copied_game_card, except)` is the one creation path.
- **choose_mode (trigger_modal) SPLICES since mig 239**: the chosen modes' actions are spliced into the parked program at resume_index and resumed — so modes may contain parking actions (copy_permanent, choose_player). Untargeted actions reach the same applier as before via the fallthrough.
- **Scenario.create seeds NO library**: any test asserting draws must first `s.spawn(seat, name, 'library')` enough cards, or the draw silently moves 0 cards (bug-634).
- **Trigger functions live in the BASELINE, not functions_src**, until first edited (cease_token_if_off_battlefield was only in 00_baseline.sql; mig 239 created its canonical functions_src file).

- **Reflexive watchers (mig 227) â€” "it gains X":** the EVENT SUBJECT (entering/attacking creature) receives the effect, no target pick. Mechanism: enqueue_triggered_ability gained p_triggering_card_id (stamped into the stack payload as `triggering_card_id`; DROP the 5-arg signature first â€” overload ambiguity); fire_watcher_triggers passes p_changed_card_id; apply_trigger_effects intercepts an effect with `target:'triggering_creature'` BEFORE the generic else and routes it via apply_creature_effect(kind=v_type, triggering_card_id, effect) â€” works for grant_keyword/pump/add_counters/deal_damage (any creature kind). NEW event `creature_attacks` broadcast from fire_attack_triggers (Atarka watches any Dragon attacking, incl. itself). **ORDERING GOTCHA:** at the entry instant the granted-flying continuous-effect row is NOT registered yet (the resolver registers AFTER the move, and the zone-change DB trigger fires DURING it), so a `has_keyword:'flying'` watcher filter (Dragon Tempest "with flying") must check INTRINSIC flying â€” cards.keywords ILIKE flying OR a source-scoped flying continuous_effect in the effective script â€” not just card_has_flying. Atarka grants on attack (registration already done), so it uses the simpler path. Dragon Tempest's SECOND ability (Dragon enters â†’ deals X damage, X = Dragons you control, to any target) is deferred (dynamic-amount targeted damage from a watcher).
- **Treasure / sac-for-mana (mig 226):** a Treasure is a TOKEN catalog row with a mana ability `{costs:[tap_self, sacrifice_self], effects:[add_mana any 1]}` â€” no bespoke effect. activate_mana_ability gained (1) sacrifice_self cost handling (put_in_graveyard the source AFTER producing â€” token then ceases to exist) and (2) a p_chosen_color arg used when an add_mana color is 'any' (the multi-colour engine path previously REJECTED 'any', line ~120). **Client routing was the real work:** addManaFromCard taps but can't sacrifice, so tapForMana now detects a sacrifice_self cost and routes through activate_mana_ability(cardId, index, undefined, color) instead â€” index = findIndex of the ability in normalized.activated_abilities. AND CardActionSheet's single-atomic-button path (taken for any non-tap cost) would skip the colour pick, so a `needsColorChoice` guard (any/commander producer) forces the per-colour buttons even with a non-tap cost. Signature change â†’ drop old 4-arg first. In THIS deck it only unlocks Rapacious Dragon (Treasure ETB); Atsushi (modal dies + impulse-exile) and Gadrak (died-this-turn count + attack restriction) still need more.
