- **Landfall / `land_entered` watcher (mig 238).** fire_zone_change_triggers broadcasts a `land_entered` watcher event on EVERY battlefield entry (alongside creature_entered); fire_watcher_triggers defaults that event's type filter to 'land' (the spell_cast bypass pattern), so only land entries actually match â€” no need to check is-land in the broadcast. Nesting Dragon = `land_entered {controller:'you'}` â†’ create_token 'Dragon Egg Token'. **Nested-token chains work via seeded catalog rows:** the Egg token catalog row carries its OWN dies-trigger script (â†’ create 'Dragon Hatchling Token'), and the Hatchling row carries flying + firebreathing â€” create_token just instantiates the catalog row, so the made token's triggers/abilities come along for free. Seed every token in BOTH test-cards.json (for tests) AND the hosted catalog (for play). **Sarkhan, Soul Aflame** shipped cost_reduction-only (become-a-copy not modelled â€” copy is the big unbuilt primitive: Will of the Temur / Deceptive Frostkite / Reflections of Littjara / Sarkhan all need token-copy or become-a-copy, none done).
- **Dragon lands (mig 237).** enters_tapped `unless` was an exclusive if/elsif (only the first of count/hand_has_type/control_type checked) â€” made them INDEPENDENT ifs (any satisfied â†’ untapped) so a land can OR several conditions (Temple of the Dragon Queen: "unless you revealed a Dragon OR control a Dragon" = `unless:{control_type:['Dragon'], hand_has_type:['Dragon']}`). Added `return_from_graveyard` to activate_ability's spell_effect-insert routing list â†’ Haven's "{2},{T},Sacrifice: return a Dragon from your graveyard" works (sac_self puts the land in the gy, then the spell_effect resolver parks the return_from_graveyard pick decision; the effect needs `filter:{type_line:'Dragon'}` + `to:'hand'`). Tap-for-"any color in commander identity" and Haven's "any, Dragons only" are approximated as plain add_mana 'any'; Path of Ancestry's scry-on-spend rider deferred. **TEST GOTCHA:** playing two lands in one test turn hits the land-play limit â€” reset `game_turn_state.lands_played_this_turn = 0` between plays (setTurn does NOT reset it).
- **Exert + untargeted set_pt (mig 236).** **Exert** (Glorybringer): declare_attacker gained `p_exert boolean` (SIGNATURE CHANGE â†’ the migration must `drop function if exists public.declare_attacker(uuid,uuid,uuid,uuid)` first AND the functions_src grant lines must be bumped to the new arg list, else the migration fails applying the stale grant â€” bug-236a). On exert it sets an 'exerted' counter-bag marker and enqueues the card's top-level `exert` effects (a normal targeted attack trigger â€” resolved via topStackItem + chooseTriggerTarget). advance_step's untap step skips untapping creatures with the marker (`counters ? 'exerted'`) and then clears it (`counters - 'exerted'`) â€” "won't untap during your NEXT untap step." Harness declareAttacker gained an `exert` 3rd arg. **Untargeted `set_pt` â†’ source** added beside untargeted grant_keyword (both call apply_creature_effect on p_source_card_id, EOT-expiring) â€” Nogi "becomes 5/5 + flying until EOT" via an attacks-trigger `conditional` (dragonsâ‰¥3). Type-addition ("becomes a Dragon") is NOT modelled (cosmetic). **TEST GOTCHA (bug-236b):** card_has_flying / card_has_* are auth-gated (`is_session_player(auth.uid())`) â€” a harness `client.query` runs as postgres (auth.uid() null) so they return FALSE regardless. Assert keyword grants by querying game_continuous_effects directly (affected_card_id + effect_type), not the card_has_* accessor. (card_effective_power/toughness are NOT auth-gated, so those work in direct queries.)
- **`becomes_target` event + `power_of` amount + recipient_player_id (mig 235).** (1) **"Becomes the target of a spell/ability an opponent controls"** (Thunderbreak Regent): a dedicated `fire_becomes_target_triggers(session, target_card, targeting_player)` broadcast from put_action_on_stack right AFTER the stack item is inserted (target locked, actor = auth.uid()) â€” NOT the generic watcher, because it needs the TARGETING player both for the opponent check and as the damage recipient. It gates on (target controlled by the watcher) + (targeting player â‰  watcher) + type_line filter, then enqueues the trigger effects with `recipient_player_id` INJECTED into each effect = the targeting player. (2) **recipient_player_id** = a new sole-recipient option in apply_triggered_ability_effects' lose_life/deal_damage branch ("deals N to THAT player"); checked before the v_recipient enum. (3) **`{power_of:'source'|'target'}`** dynamic amount (resolve_dynamic_amount â†’ card_effective_power) = "damage equal to Eshki's power." (4) **Eshki's power tiers reuse the spell_cast watcher with the EXISTING min_power filter** â€” three separate spell_cast {controller:you, type_line:'creature', min_power:0/4/6} watchers (no new tier machinery; min_power reads the cast creature's effective power on the stack). **DRAIN GOTCHA:** a card that enqueues N triggers from ONE event (Eshki: 3) needs N resolveStack() calls â€” each resolves one stack item. **Spit Flame** shipped as 4-dmg removal only; its graveyard recursion is unreachable (watchers fire for battlefield permanents / the changed card, never graveyard sources).
- **Spell-cast watcher (mig 234) â€” `spell_cast` event.** Both cast chokepoints broadcast it: cast_spell_effect (instant/sorcery, after the spell_effect stack insert, guarded on a non-null source) and cast_card_from_hand (permanents â€” AFTER the cast_permanent insert; lands `return` earlier so they never fire). Caster = auth.uid(). Reuses the existing watcher machinery â€” fire_watcher_triggers(session, spell_card, caster, 'spell_cast') â€” with ONE change: the type-filter default is 'creature' for permanent watchers but EMPTY for spell_cast (the changed card is a spell of any type; a watcher may still set type_line:'creature' for "a creature spell"). The controller filter (you/opponent relative to the watcher) already does what "you/an opponent casts" needs. Taurean Mauler = spell_cast {controller:'opponent'} â†’ may add_counters self. **Changeling (counts as every creature type) is NOT modelled** â€” only Mauler's counter ability; faithfully making it a Dragon for tribal synergy would need touching the many `type_line ilike '%X%'` checks. **`return_self_to_hand`** effect = move the SOURCE permanent battlefieldâ†’owner's hand + rebuild (Encroaching/Breaching Dragonstorm "when a Dragon you control enters, return this to hand" â€” a creature_entered {type_line:'Dragon', controller:'you'} watcher; the enchantment isn't a creature so it never self-triggers). NOTE: a watcher only fires for BATTLEFIELD permanents (or the changed card), so graveyard-based recursion triggers (Spit Flame) still aren't reachable.
- **Divided damage from triggers/abilities (mig 233) â€” a parked decision, reused by both.** Targeted TRIGGERS only carry ONE target (enqueue_triggered_ability stamps target_required/target_count); "N damage divided among any number of targets" needs its OWN decision. `divide_damage` effect â†’ apply_trigger_effects parks a `divide_damage` decision (options from `divide_damage_options(session, controller, {controller, types})` â€” battlefield creatures/planeswalkers + optionally players); submit_decision validates the allocation (each amountâ‰¥1, sum = parked amount, each target was offered, count â‰¤ max_targets) then `apply_damage_allocations` applies it (creatureâ†’apply_creature_effect, PWâ†’apply_damage_to_planeswalker, playerâ†’life loss; one zero-loyalty sweep + game-end check). Decision result shape: `{allocations:[{game_card_id|player_id, amount}]}`. ACTIVATED divided damage (Skarrgan) reuses the SAME park by adding 'divide_damage' to activate_ability's spell_effect-insert list â€” the spell_effect stack item resolves via apply_trigger_effects, which parks the decision (no per-action-type plumbing). decision_type is UNCONSTRAINED (no CHECK), so a new one needs no DDL. **Activation gate:** activate_ability now reads an ability `condition` ({counters, of, at_least}) via resolve_dynamic_amount BEFORE paying costs (Skarrgan "only if it has a +1/+1 counter"). **Riot** = an ETB `choose_one` (mig 230) with modes [add_counters self 1] / [grant_keyword haste] â€” and untargeted single `grant_keyword` now resolves to the SOURCE via apply_creature_effect (it was only wired as grant_keyword_all + the reflexive triggering_creature path before).
- **Monstrosity (mig 232) + the per-recipient-amount gotcha.** `monstrosity` effect = a once-only "level up": read a 'monstrous' counter-bag marker; if absent, add N +1/+1 counters + set the marker, then recursively apply its `on_monstrous` effects (the "when this becomes monstrous" rider) via apply_triggered_ability_effects â€” a no-op once monstrous. Routed by adding 'monstrosity' to activate_ability's spell_effect-insert list (the create_token route), so it resolves with p_source_card_id = the activating card and acts on itself. **PER-RECIPIENT DYNAMIC AMOUNTS NEED A BESPOKE LOOP:** the generic lose_life/deal_damage each_opponent path computes v_eff_amount ONCE (for the controller) and applies it to every recipient â€” so "each opponent loses life = THAT player's OWN hand size" (Stormbreath) can't use it. Implemented as a dedicated `damage_each_opponent_by_hand` branch that loops opponents and reads each one's hand count. Any "each player by their own X" effect needs this shape, not a recipient list with a shared amount. Counter-bag markers (loyalty_turn / kicked / gy_cast_turn / monstrous) are the standard once-per-permanent state â€” survive stackâ†’battlefield and rebuilds.
- **Cost reduction (mig 231) â€” generic-only, two shapes, one helper.** `reduced_mana_cost(session, caster, card, cost)` reduces the GENERIC token of a printed cost (never coloured/hybrid pips; floored at 0; a cost with no `{N}` is unchanged) by the sum of: (a) the card's own top-level `cost_reduction` script prop `{amount, if?:{count,type_line?,at_least}}` (Draconic Lore self-reduction, conditional via resolve_count_amount), and (b) `cost_reduction` continuous-effect rows the caster controls whose `payload.type_line` matches the cast card (Dragonlord's Servant / Sarkhan "Dragon spells you cast cost {1} less"). The STATIC reducer is a script `continuous_effects` entry `{type:'cost_reduction', affected:'controller', payload:{type_line, amount}}` â€” register_card_continuous_effects gained 'cost_reduction' in its whitelist (defaults to affected:'controller' â†’ affected_player_id = controller, since it's not a source-keyword) and the effect_type CHECK gained it. Wired into BOTH cast paths: cast_card_from_hand (permanents â€” passes the reduced string to pay_mana_cost; **client cost display still shows full price, TBD**) and cast_spell_effect (instant/sorcery â€” generic is AUTO-paid from pool with a null generic payment, so the reduced cost just works, no client change). regexp_replace WITHOUT 'g' reduces only the first `{N}` (a mana cost has at most one generic token). **TEST GOTCHA:** dev_spawn_card a permanent with an ETB (Rapacious Dragon) fires the ETB onto the stack â†’ a later sorcery cast raises "stack not empty"; use an ETB-less Dragon (Dragon Token) when you just need "control a Dragon", and call s.rebuild() after spawning a static-lord so its continuous effect registers. Regs unlocked: Dragonlord's Servant, Draconic Lore, and the cost-reduction halves of Sarkhan Soul Aflame.
- **Atsushi (mig 230) â€” modal-trigger framework + impulse-exile.** (1) **MODAL TRIGGER:** modal "choose one" previously existed ONLY for spells (cast_modal_spell â†’ choose_mode â†’ resolve_top_of_stack applies the chosen mode's `actions`). For a TRIGGER, a new `choose_one` effect `{prompt, choose?, modes:[{label, actions:[â€¦]}]}` in apply_trigger_effects parks a choose_mode decision with `params.trigger_modal=true` (resume_index set like every park). submit_decision gained a choose_mode APPLY branch (there was NONE before â€” spell modals resolve via the stack, not submit_decision): if trigger_modal, loop chosen indices, apply `options[idx].actions` via apply_triggered_ability_effects, then resume_or_finalize. Spell modals carry no trigger_modal flag so the branch no-ops for them. Modes use `actions` (not `effects`) to match the existing choose_mode target-detection validation. (2) **IMPULSE ("exile top N, play until end of your next turn"):** an `impulse` effect in apply_triggered_ability_effects moves the top N library cards to exile and inserts a `play_from_exile` continuous effect (affected_player=controller, payload={card_ids[], created_turn}, NO expires_at_phase â€” custom expiry). cast_card_from_hand now accepts zone `exile` gated on a play_from_exile row whose `payload->'card_ids' ? card_id`. **"Until end of your NEXT turn" timing** = advance_step deletes the row when leaving step='end' for the active player where `created_turn < current turn` â€” survives the creation turn, dies at the first end-step of a LATER turn of that player (works whether created on your own or an opponent's turn; turn_number is monotonic so created_turn<current â‡” a later turn). New effect_type `play_from_exile` added to the game_continuous_effects CHECK (latest list was mig 199). **DEFERRED:** instant/sorcery casts from impulse-exile need the same exile gate in cast_spell_effect (cast_card_from_hand is permanents/lands only â€” it rejects instant/sorcery); and the CLIENT does not yet surface playable exiled cards. Schema: `impulse`+`choose_one` added to KNOWN_V2_ACTION_TYPES + JSON_ONLY allowlist (no guided form).
- **Gadrak (mig 229) â€” three small additive primitives:** (1) **Game-wide "nontoken creatures died this turn"** = a SECOND per-controller turn-stamped tally on game_session_players (turn_nontoken_creatures_died + _turn), bumped in put_in_graveyard alongside the existing all-creatures tally (read cards.is_token; bump only on nontoken, but ALWAYS reset-on-stale-turn so it self-clears). The count source SUMS across all players (each stale stamp contributes 0) â†’ game-wide total regardless of controller. Mirrors mig 193; no turn-advance hook. (2) **create_token DYNAMIC count:** when `count` is an OBJECT, resolve via resolve_dynamic_amount and DON'T floor at 1 (0 deaths â†’ empty `1..0` loop â†’ 0 tokens); a literal/absent count keeps greatest(1,â€¦). Same 0-vs-1 trap as Syphon Flesh. (3) **Attack restriction `cant_attack_unless`** = top-level script prop {count, at_least} read in declare_attacker (after summoning-sickness, before tap) via effective_script + resolve_count_amount(controller=auth.uid()); raises if under. Added `artifacts_you_control` count source. **TEST GOTCHA (re-confirmed):** the harness has NO savepoints â€” a raised RPC aborts the whole withRolledBackTx tx (25P02 on the next query), so an `assert.rejects` must be the LAST action in its test; split positive/negative attack cases into separate tests.
- **Dragons Tier-1 (migs 224-225):** `deal_damage_all` = untargeted mass damage in apply_triggered_ability_effects: loop matching battlefield creatures through apply_damage_to_creature (run_sweep FALSE per hit), optionally planeswalkers via apply_damage_to_planeswalker, then ONE move_lethal + move_zero_loyalty sweep at the end. filter.with_keyword/without_keyword gate on card_has_flying (the `X is distinct from 'flying'` trick: null filter passes everything), filter.exclude_source skips the source ("each OTHER creature" â€” Harbinger green half). - **Precon batch 2026-06-10 (migs 200-215, 17 cards) â€” the conventions that emerged:** (1) **Cost-target-slot convention:** activation costs that consume a chosen card (exile_from_graveyard, discard) ride `p_target_card_id`; after paying, NULL the param or the cost card leaks into the effect's target routing (bug-575). (2) **Bag markers as cast-state:** 'kicked' (mig 211) and 'gy_cast_turn' (mig 207) live in the game_cards counter bag â€” survives stackâ†’battlefield and rebuilds, cleared by bounce/graveyard resets; loyalty_turn precedent. "Was kicked" conditionals = `{counters:'kicked', of:'self'}` via resolve_dynamic_amount â€” NO new conditional machinery. (3) **Turn-stamped per-player counters** (mig 193 pattern) now also: turn_graveyard_casts (note_graveyard_cast helper, bumped in BOTH cast paths). (4) **Until-EOT mass keyword grants** = grant_keyword_all rows (expires ending/cleanup, no source_zone_required, not script-flagged); player hexproof = payload.includes_player + the put_action_on_stack player gate (mig 203). (5) **choose_color / choose_creature_type park-and-inject pattern:** the decision's params carry what to build (anthem shape); submit_decision writes a continuous-effect row with the choice baked in (colour-filtered pump fold via card_color_set, mig 209). (6) **Alternative/optional cast costs are cast_card_from_hand params** (p_kicked, p_sacrifice_ids) + top-level script props (kicker, graveyard_cast_cost) â€” each signature change needs the drop-old-signature prelude AND the grant line updated (bug-574). (7) **Form-canonical object fields**: conditions authored for form-settability must materialize empty optional text sub-fields (type_line:'', bug-230/576). Documented gaps: type/colour ADDITION ("becomes a black Zombie in addition") has no layer â€” Necromantic Selection/Grimoire reanimate without it; Havengul Lich's ability-copy rider unbuilt; cast path still owner-only (opponent-graveyard casts).

- **NEW ENGINE-CHANGE WORKFLOW (2026-06-10): `supabase/functions_src/` is the canonical CURRENT definition of 25 hot engine functions.** To change a function: edit its functions_src file (git diff shows just the branch you added), then `node scripts/new-migration.mjs <name> <fn...>` emits the migration from those files verbatim (hand-add non-function DDL like CHECK constraints at the top + a real header). NEVER extract-by-line-range from past migrations again â€” that whole over-capture bug class (mig 194 awk disaster) is dead. Seeder: `scripts/extract-functions.mjs` (dollar-quote-aware: bodies close at `$TAG$;`, e.g. pay_mana_cost's `$_$;` â€” a bare `$$;` search over-captures). Faithfulness was verified by applying all 25 files over the live local DB + full suite (704/704). Tests: `npm test` now runs `scripts/run-tests.mjs` (recursive readdir glob, Windows-safe, optional substring filters: `npm test -- vela amass`) â€” package.json no longer carries the test-file list; new test files are auto-discovered.
- **Keyword-grant mass filters (mig 200) + creature_left watcher (mig 201) + grant_keyword_all (mig 202).** (1) The 12 grantable-keyword accessors' mass branch now honours payload `exclude_source` ("OTHER Zombies have â€¦", Death Baron/Vela) and `token_only` ("Zombie TOKENS have â€¦", Gleaming Overseer â€” tokenness = cards.is_token); register passes payloads through verbatim so NO register change; form: BuilderKeywordGrant gained excludeSource/tokenOnly checkboxes. (2) `creature_left` watcher event broadcast from fire_zone_change_triggers' leaves branch â€” fires on ANY battlefield exit incl. bounce/exile (a death fires BOTH creature_died and creature_left); Vela the Night-Clad. (3) `grant_keyword_all` effect = mass keyword until-EOT continuous row (expires ending/cleanup like mass pump mig 179; no source_zone_required, NOT script-flagged so it outlives source + rebuilds); branch in apply_triggered_ability_effects (hits spells+triggers) + activate_ability routes it via the spell_effect direct-insert list ('create_token','search_library','grant_keyword_all'); payload.includes_player reserved for the player-hexproof gate (Lazotep Plating).

- **Player-aura ("enchant player") WITHOUT a cast-path refactor (mig 199, Curse of Disturbance).** Instead of adding `attached_to_player` + targeting a player at cast, the curse's ETB `choose_player` picks the enchanted player and a new `curse_attack_zombie` effect (in `apply_triggered_ability_effects`) registers a `curse_attacked` continuous effect on them (`affected_player_id = p_controller_id` â€” the chosen player after choose_player's recipient rewrite; `source_card_id = the curse`). `declare_attacker` then queries `game_continuous_effects` for `curse_attacked` on the defending player (joining the source card on `zone='battlefield'`) and `enqueue_triggered_ability`s a create_token for the curse's controller AND, when `auth.uid()` differs, the attacking player ("each opponent attacking does the same"). Test gotcha: an ETB trigger is ENQUEUED by spawn â€” call `resolveStack()` to resolve it (which parks the choose_player decision) before reading `pendingDecision()`; and `resolveStack`/`resolve_top_of_stack` resolves ONE item, so drain the stack in a loop when multiple triggers are enqueued. (And: `sed` over a test can clobber a helper's own `resolveStack()` line â€” caused an infinite-recursion hang.)
- **`may` gained an optional `condition` + `cost` (mig 197) â€” a reusable "you may pay X" primitive.** Liliana's Devotee ("if a creature died this turn, you may pay {1}{B} â€” if you do, create a Zombie"). In `apply_trigger_effects`' may branch: a `condition` (count object, like `conditional`) is evaluated via `resolve_dynamic_amount` and the may is SKIPPED (not offered) when it fails; the `cost` (mana string) rides into the confirm decision's params. In `submit_decision`'s confirm branch: when confirmed, `pay_mana_cost(session, deciding_player, params.cost, null)` runs BEFORE the inner effects (raises if unaffordable â€” client should only offer when affordable). This avoids the conditional-wrapping-may nesting problem (conditional resolves in `apply_triggered_ability_effects`, can't park a may decision) by putting the condition ON the may itself. Reproduced apply_trigger_effects + submit_decision (mig 191) by exact line range.
- **Mana value / CMC: there is NO cmc column â€” parse `mana_cost`.** `card_mana_value(session, card)` (mig 196): `sum over regexp_matches(mana_cost, '\{([^}]+)\}', 'g')` of `case when sym ~ '^[0-9]+$' then sym::int when X then 0 else 1`. Feed the Swarm ("lose life = its mana value") uses it as a dynamic `then`-rider amount `{mana_value_of:'target'}` in `handle_permanent_effect` (latest mig 152). **Cast-path gotcha:** a removal SPELL's `then` rider ONLY resolves via the `permanent_effect` stack action (`putOnStack('permanent_effect', {kind, target_card_id, target_type, then})`) â€” NOT via `cast_spell_effect`'s spell_effect program (which routes destroy through `apply_targeted_triggered_ability_effects` and DROPS the rider). So test removal-with-rider via `putOnStack('permanent_effect', â€¦)`, like targeted-spell-riders.test.ts; the client translates a removal spell's authored `spell_effect` form into that action at cast time.
- **Intimidate + hexproof enforcement (mig 195).** Intimidate ("blockable only by artifact creatures and/or creatures sharing a colour") is a per-blocker gate in `declare_blocker` (next to the flying/protection gates): reject if `card_has_intimidate(attacker)` and the blocker is neither an artifact (`type_line ilike '%artifact%'`) nor shares a colour (`game_card_color_set(blocker) && game_card_color_set(attacker)`). Hexproof ("can't be targeted by opponents") is a gate in `put_action_on_stack` next to the protection target-check: reject if the target `card_has_hexproof` and its controller `is distinct from auth.uid()` (you can still target your own). Both need the keyword in the CHECK + register's 3 lists + an accessor (mig 184 pattern) + the form keyword list. Reproduced register (mig 194), declare_blocker (mig 133), put_action_on_stack (mig 131) by EXACT line range â€” confirmed `grep -c "create or replace function"` = exactly the expected count (no over-capture this time; lesson from mig 194 applied). Combined with mig 194 menace, all combat-keyword-blocked precon cards (Vela, Lazotep Plating, Gleaming Overseer, Lord of the Accursed) are unblocked.
- **Menace enforcement (mig 194) + a NASTY extraction gotcha.** Menace ("can't be blocked except by 2+") needs FOUR things: (1) `'menace'` in the `game_continuous_effects` effect_type CHECK (latest list was mig 173); (2) `'menace'` in `register_card_continuous_effects`'s THREE lists (the continuous-effects whitelist, the source-default `affected` list, the intrinsic-keyword CASE â€” latest register is mig 159); (3) a `card_has_menace` accessor (mig 184 pattern); (4) the check in `advance_step` (latest mig 140) at the `declare_blockersâ†’combat_damage` exit. Blockers are counted from **`game_combat_blockers`** (one row per blocker), NOT `game_combat_assignments` (which keeps only the first via coalesce). **THE GOTCHA:** `awk '/create.../,/grant.*fnname/'` OVER-CAPTURES when the function has no trailing grant (mig 159's register ends at `$$;` with no grant) â€” it ran to EOF and dragged in mig 159's STALE `resolve_combat_damage`, silently reverting planeswalker loyalty damage (2 PWC tests failed). ALWAYS extract by exact line range, then `grep -c "create or replace function"` to confirm you grabbed exactly ONE. When a core-function reproduction breaks an UNRELATED test, suspect over-capture of a co-located function.
- **`creatures_died_this_turn` count source (mig 193) â€” turn-stamped, no turn-advance hook.** A new `resolve_count_amount` source for both dynamic amounts (Liliana's Standard Bearer "draw X = creatures died under your control this turn") and `conditional` conditions ("if a creature died this turn"). Tracked on `game_session_players` as TWO columns: `turn_creatures_died` + `turn_creatures_died_turn` (the turn it belongs to). Incremented in `put_in_graveyard` (the battlefieldâ†’graveyard chokepoint â€” it no-ops for non-battlefield cards, so it only counts true deaths) when the dying card is a creature, for its controller. Read lazily: `case when stamp_turn = current turn then count else 0` â€” so it self-resets each turn with NO modification to the hot turn-advance function. Pattern for any "this turn" counter: stamp the turn, compare on read. `put_in_graveyard` is a core chokepoint called everywhere â€” the change is purely additive (a conditional counter bump), full suite confirmed no regression.
- **`conditional` effect = a new COMPOSITION primitive (mig 192), built purely as a registry data-entry.** "If a count is at least N, then <effects>." Engine: one branch in `apply_triggered_ability_effects` evaluates `resolve_dynamic_amount(condition)` (a `{count, type_line?}` object) vs `condition.at_least`, and if it holds, RECURSIVELY applies the inner effects through the same resolver (non-decision inner effects only). Form: ONE registry entry with an `object`-kind `condition` field (count enum + type_line text + at_least number) + an `effect-list` field â€” no new form component; it round-trips exactly. This proves the "general spell/effect builder" the user asked about already exists: the registry's `object` + `effect-list` field kinds compose arbitrarily nested effects (cf. `may`/`choose_player`). Routing note: a SPELL program (`apply_trigger_effects` mig 170) reaches non-decision effects via its else-branch â†’ `apply_targeted_triggered_ability_effects` â†’ `apply_triggered_ability_effects`, so a branch added there is hit by both spells and auto-resolving triggers. The condition vocab is count-based today (creatures_you_control / lands / cards_in_graveyard); extend `resolve_dynamic_amount`-style sources for more.
- **VERIFY card behavior against `lib/oracle-cards-*.json` â€” never seed from memory.** A planning workflow seeded with remembered oracle text produced several WRONG cardâ†’behavior mappings (Laboratory Drudge is "draw at end step if you cast/activated from a graveyard this turn", NOT a cast-watcher; Necromantic Selection reanimates a CHOSEN destroyed creature as a black Zombie, NOT highest-mana-value, so it needs type/color-addition NOT a CMC parser; Loyal Subordinate is a commander-"Lieutenant" conditional, not "3+ creatures"; Scourge of Nel Toth is an alternative CAST cost from graveyard, not an activated ability). The repo ships the full Scryfall oracle dump at `lib/oracle-cards-20260531210653.json` (array of {name, type_line, oracle_text}) â€” query it for ground truth before designing or building any card. Codebase-only scout agents are great on engine SURFACES but blind on card BEHAVIOR; feed them verified oracle text.
- **Edict create_token dynamic count (sacrifice tally).** Syphon Flesh ("create a Zombie for each creature sacrificed this way", mig 191): `submit_decision`'s sacrifice branch accumulates `sacrificed_count` on the spell's own stack item payload across the each-opponent chain (`+ jsonb_array_length(v_top)` per decision); a `create_token` with `count:{count:'sacrificed_this_way'}` is substituted in `apply_trigger_effects`' create_token pre-block (reads `v_item.payload.sacrificed_count` on resume) â€” and SKIPS when the tally is 0 (the create_token resolver floors count at `greatest(1, â€¦)`, so 0 would wrongly make 1). Required reproducing apply_trigger_effects (mig 170) + submit_decision (mig 179) verbatim â€” extract with awk, apply surgical edits, don't hand-retype 600 lines.
- **A counterspell rider reads its OWN source script in `handle_counter_spell` â€” no client/builder change.** Undermine ("Counter target spell. Its controller loses 2 life", mig 190): the handler already locks the target stack item (which carries `controller_player_id` of the countered spell) and reads the TARGET's script for `cant_be_countered`; the rider amount is read symmetrically from the COUNTER spell's own `p_stack_item.source_card_id` script (`spell_effect.actions[] where type='counter' â†’ controller_loses_life`) and deducted from the target's controller. Applies even when the target is uncounterable (the two instructions are independent). The counterspell cast path (`putCounterSpellOnStack` â†’ `put_action_on_stack('counter_spell', {target_stack_item_id})`) is untouched, so the card is live with only the handler + a schema field on the `counter` action. Counterspells aren't in the form registry (JSON/AI-authored). Test gotcha: a counter fixture WITH a `mana_cost` must have the caster's mana set (`put_action_on_stack` pays the source's cost from hand); the older counter tests used a mana-cost-less fixture (Doom Blade Test) to skip that.
- **Multi-agent feature builds: parallel AUTHORING + serial INTEGRATION is the pattern that works here (not worktree CI).** Experiment (2026-06-08, Undead Augur â€– Liliana's Mastery): two agents authored disjoint free-composition cards concurrently in ~98s each (~106k tok total), then the orchestrator integrated. Two structural facts make literal `git worktree` isolation NOT pay off: (1) `node_modules` is gitignored, so each worktree needs a full `npm install` to run tsc/lint/tests; (2) ONE shared local Postgres â€” agents can't run `test:db:setup`/`npm test` concurrently without stomping each other. So: agents work in the shared checkout, each create only their OWN new file (distinct test filename â€” no collision), static-check (tsc/lint/round-trip, NO DB), and REPORT additive snippets; the orchestrator adds the fixtures + `package.json` test entries and runs the DB suite ONCE. Shared-file collision points to coordinate centrally: `tests/fixtures/test-cards.json`, `package.json` test list, migration numbers (pre-assign, e.g. Aâ†’190/Bâ†’191), and **`.wolf/memory.md`+`anatomy.md`** (the OpenWolf auto-update made both agents append concurrently â€” survived by timing luck, but concurrent appends can lose writes). Multi-agent pays off most for read/triage/review fan-out and disjoint-lane authoring; it does NOT help `activate_ability`-bound work (serial â€” reproduced wholesale each change).
- **A new STACK ACTION TYPE is gated in THREE independent places** (learned mig 186, Withered Wretch's `exile_from_graveyard` effect): (1) the `stack_action_handlers` registry (dispatch â†’ handler fn); (2) `put_action_on_stack`'s hardcoded action-type allowlist (latest reproduction was mig 131); (3) the `game_stack_items.action_type` CHECK constraint (latest list was mig 129). Registering the handler alone yields "Unsupported stack action type"; passing the allowlist still hits the CHECK constraint. Cheapest path for a one-off targeted action: **direct-insert the stack item** in `activate_ability` (status 'pending', as the `create_token` branch does) to skip the `put_action_on_stack` allowlist, AND drop+re-add the CHECK constraint with the new type. The dispatcher resolves it via the registered handler. Targeted ability effects carry the target as `p_target_card_id` â†’ into the stack payload's `target_card_id`; the untargeted `apply_triggered_ability_effects` resolver is NOT where single-target effects resolve.
- **`pay_life` mana-ability cost + the client "simple vs complex" mana split.** `activate_mana_ability` (mig 189) now accepts a `pay_life` cost (validate life â‰¥ N per CR 119.4, then deduct). Talisman of Dominance ("{T}, Pay 1 life: Add {U} or {B}") is authored as THREE single-colour {T} mana abilities (C free, U/B each pay 1) â€” only one taps per untap, so it's functionally "choose one", avoiding a "choose U or B" concept. CRITICAL client detail: ControllerListV4 only routes a mana ability through `activate_mana_ability` when it has a **non-tap cost** (`c.type !== 'tap_self'`) or multiple colours; a tap-only ability resolves CLIENT-SIDE via `add_mana_from_card` and would SKIP a pay_life/other cost. So any new mana-ability cost must also be reflected in that routing condition. Builder: the mana variant gained `payLife` (0 = none); an effect (non-mana) ability carrying pay_life round-trips to JSON (not modelled there).
- **Activated removal of a NON-creature permanent routes through `permanent_effect`.** `activate_ability`'s destroy/exile/bounce/tap/untap branch defaults to `<kind>_creature`, whose builder REJECTS non-creature targets ("Target is not a legal creature"). When the effect's `target_type` isn't creature-only (`behavior_target_type_is_creature_only` is false â€” note: null target_type â†’ false), route to the type-flexible `permanent_effect` action (mig 113) instead; `apply_creature_effect`'s removal kinds work on any permanent. Unstable Obelisk (mig 188). Form already supports it (`removalTargetField` offers artifact/enchantment/permanent). Existing creature destroys set `target_type:'creature'` explicitly, so they're unaffected.
- **Form-settability â‰  green tests.** Engine tests don't prove a card is authorable in the guided form. A `parseScriptToForm` SWEEP over the `*Test` fixtures (script: iterate, count null=JSON-only) is the way to find "engine works but form can't set it" gaps. As of the 2026-06-08 sweep: 61/87 V2 fixtures are form-settable. The JSON-only remainder is mostly INTENDED (dynamic amounts `{counters}`/`{count:devotion}`, X spells, modal, multi-target, loyalty/planeswalkers, top-level flags `cant_be_countered`/`doubles_counters`/`enters_with_counters`, auras, energy cost, multi-effect activated abilities, `set_pt` which isn't in the registry). The real fixable gaps found: (1) `search_library` `tapped` not registry-exposed â†’ fixed [[bug-527]]; (2) `deal_damage_target` was `'spell'`-only though the engine resolves targeted damage from a trigger (`trigger_effect_target_type` lists deal_damage) â†’ added `'trigger'` context (Flame Mage). The typed keyword grant gap is now BUILT: `BuilderForm.keywordGrants` (`{keyword, creatureType, scope:'controller'|'all'}`) round-trips `continuous_effects` keyword effects with `affected:'controller'|'all'` (+ optional `payload.creature_type`); `parseContinuousEffects` routes a keyword-typed effect with affected controller/all to a grant, and `KeywordGrantEditor` is the form widget (parallel to static buffs). Eternal Skylord/Vizier are now form-settable (62/87).
- **Activated abilities reuse the SPELL resolver for parked-decision / token effects.** `activate_ability` handles most effects via per-branch `put_action_on_stack`, but `create_token` and `search_library` (and any multi-effect program) instead **direct-insert a `spell_effect` stack item** carrying the effect(s), so resolution reuses the spell-effect resolver (tutor decisions, `tapped`/`filter`, token builder). To make another spell-style single effect (scry/surveil/mill/â€¦) activatable, add its `v_eff_type` to that routing branch â€” no new handler needed. Wayfarer's Bauble = sacrifice_self cost + this route (mig 187). The form already offers these (activated-ability picker uses `effectsForContext('spell')`), so often it's fixture+test only.
- **No "activated-ability-only" effect context.** The activated-ability effect picker (CardBehaviorForm.tsx ~L940) and the spell-action picker both use `effectsForContext('spell')`. So an effect that only works for activated abilities (e.g. `exile_from_graveyard`, wired only in `activate_ability`) must be registered in `'spell'` context and will ALSO appear as an instant/sorcery action. The shared resolver silently skips unknown effect types (no final `else` raise), so as a real spell it's a harmless no-op, not a crash â€” documented as a known limitation in the registry comment rather than blocked.
- **Behavior authoring has THREE layers â€” keep them in sync.** A new card behavior must be wired in up to three places, and they are independent: (1) **engine** (SQL migration) â€” makes it work; (2) **Zod schema** [card-behavior-schema.ts] â€” validates hand-written/AI JSON; (3) **guided builder** [card-behavior-registry.ts effect entries + card-behavior-builder.ts BuilderForm for top-level props + CardBehaviorForm.tsx for the widget] â€” exposes it in the no-code form. The guided form is driven by the **registry** (`effectsForContext`), NOT the Zod schema, so adding to the schema does NOT surface it in the form. Effect-level options (e.g. create_token `tapped`, new contexts) = one registry entry. Top-level card props (flashback, loyalty_abilities) are NOT in the registry â€” they need a `BuilderForm` field + build/parse wiring + a widget. If a script uses anything the form can't model, `parseScriptToForm` returns null and the editor drops to JSON mode. The cheap mistake (made this session): updating engine + schema + LLM docs but forgetting the registry, so the card only authors via AI/JSON, not the guided form.
  - **Three distinct wiring SHAPES in the guided builder, depending on what the behavior IS:** (a) a **resolution effect** (deal_damage, create_token, â€¦) applied at trigger/spell/rider resolution = ONE registry entry (`effectsForContext` drives the dropdown + fields). (b) a **flat top-level prop** (flashback string) = a `BuilderForm` scalar field + build/parse + one widget. (c) a **`continuous_effects` entry** (keywords, static anthems/lords) â€” these are STATIC, registered at rebuild, NOT resolution effects, so they bypass the registry entirely: they need a dedicated `BuilderForm` list + a hand-written parse that partitions `continuous_effects` (`parseContinuousEffects`) + a bespoke editor component. Static type-lords ("Other Zombies you control get +1/+1" = `{type:'pump', affected:'controller', payload:{power,toughness,creature_type,exclude_source}}`) are shape (c): wired via `BuilderForm.staticBuffs` + `StaticBuffEditor` in CardBehaviorForm.tsx (Cemetery Reaper, this session). Engine already existed (typed-lords mig 164 = `Zombie Lord Test`); only the form layer was missing.
  - **`BuilderStaticBuff` gained a `scope` ('controller' | 'all') field** so the form authors both "creatures you control" (affected:'controller') and global/sliver anthems "all creatures" (affected:'all', engine support from mig 145). `parseStaticBuff` accepts either `affected` value.
- **A type in the Zod schema does NOT prove engine support (bug-464).** The schema (`card-behavior-schema.ts`) is permissive â€” it validates author *intent* and lists capabilities the engine may not implement (e.g. `sacrifice_self` cost was a known cost type but `activate_ability` raised on it). When triaging "is X supported," grep the migrations for the actual handler; the engine is the source of truth for what runs. **`sacrifice_self` activated-ability cost (mig 175):** reproduced `activate_ability` (from mig 162) with a `v_has_sac` branch that `put_in_graveyard`s the source after other costs, before the ability hits the stack (`put_action_on_stack` tolerates a non-battlefield source). Form: the `effect`-kind activated ability gained a `sacSelf` boolean (a "Sacrifice this" checkbox); mana abilities reject `sacSelf` on parse. Commander's Sphere now works (engine + form).
- **"Exile a creature card from a graveyard" activated-ability cost + create_token effect (mig 178, Cemetery Reaper).** Two activated-ability gaps closed at once: (1) a new `exile_from_graveyard` cost (`{type:'exile_from_graveyard', type_line:'creature'}`) â€” the chosen graveyard card is passed as `p_target_card_id` (these abilities' EFFECT is untargeted, so the target slot carries the cost target); the engine validates it's a matching card in ANY graveyard and exiles it (controller:=owner). (2) `create_token` as an activated-ability effect â€” `activate_ability` had NO token builder and `put_action_on_stack` has no token handler, so it routes the token through a DIRECT INSERT of a `spell_effect` stack item (reusing the spell-effect resolver â†’ apply_triggered_ability_effects' create_token, incl. tapped). Form: an "Exile a creature from a graveyard" checkbox on the effect-kind activated ability (creature filter only; other filters â†’ JSON mode). **Token-name two-list gotcha:** the form's `EFFECT_TOKEN_NAMES` (registry) and the SEEDED test-card tokens are DIFFERENT lists â€” a token must be in BOTH to be form-authorable AND engine-resolvable in tests. `Zombie Token` is in EFFECT_TOKEN_NAMES but wasn't seeded; added it to test-cards.json. The in-game PICKER is done: ControllerListV4 detects an `exile_from_graveyard` cost (`needsGraveyardCard`), and the activated-ability target picker (`abilityPick.canTargetGraveyard`) lists creature cards from ANY graveyard (`graveyardCreatures = boardCards.filter(zone==='graveyard' && creature)`) â€” choosing one calls activate_ability with it as targetCardId. Also taught getAbilityEffect/ABILITY_EFFECT_TYPES that `create_token` is a supported untargeted ability effect. Committed via hunk-split (the ControllerListV4 two-column reflow stays uncommitted). Cemetery Reaper ability #2 is now fully playable end-to-end.
- **Watcher-trigger FILTER in the guided form (Champion of the Perished).** The form's triggers were event+effects only; the watcher events (creature_entered/died/got_counter) need a `filter` (`{type_line, controller, exclude_self}`) to be useful, which wasn't exposed (engine mig 165 + schema already supported it). Added `BuilderTrigger.filter` (`{typeLine, controller, excludeSelf}`) + `parseTriggerFilter` + a filter UI shown only for watcher events (a type box, a you/opponent/anyone select, an "another (not this)" checkbox). **Controller-default gotcha:** the ENGINE defaults an ABSENT `controller` to `'you'` (mig 165 line 76: `coalesce(... ,'you')`), and `'any'` needs to be EXPLICIT (`else true` branch). So the form default is `'you'`, build OMITS controller when `'you'` (canonical minimal JSON) and emits it for opponent/any. A bare watcher (no filter) already means "a creature you control". Champion of the Perished = `creature_entered` + `{type_line:'Zombie', exclude_self:true}` (controller you implied) + `add_counters 1`.
- **Mass typed P/T debuff `pump_all` (mig 179, Crippling Fear).** "Choose a creature type. Each creature that isn't of the chosen type gets -3/-3 until end of turn." Three pieces: (1) **`exclude_type` in the P/T fold** â€” `card_layered_power/toughness` (reproduced from mig 164) gained a `payload.exclude_type` flag that INVERTS the creature_type filter (creatures NOT of the type get the pump). (2) **`apply_mass_pump_until_eot(session, source, controller, effect)`** helper â€” inserts a `pump` continuous effect (`affected:'all'` when scope!='controller'; affected_player_id=null) with `expires_at_phase='ending'/step='cleanup'` (the existing sweep removes it), then runs `move_lethal_damaged_creatures_to_graveyard` (a -X/-X reads EFFECTIVE toughness, so it can kill). (3) **`choose_creature_type` (submit_decision, reproduced from mig 170) now injects the chosen type into a `pump_all`'s `creature_type`** and applies pump_all via the helper (separating it from the rest, which still go through apply_triggered_ability_effects). **Leaner choice:** handled pump_all inside choose_creature_type's branch (the injection HAS to live in submit_decision anyway) rather than ALSO reproducing the huge apply_triggered_ability_effects. **Form: now authorable.** Added `choose_creature_type` (effect-list, contexts:['spell'], itemContext:'spell') + `pump_all` (power/toughness/scope/creature_type/exclude_type, contexts:['trigger','spell']) as REGISTRY entries â€” that was sufficient (the form, dropdown, defaults, parse/build all derive from the registry; NO builder-union or component change needed, since BuilderSpellEffect is a loose cast and BUILDER_SPELL_EFFECT_TYPES = effectsForContext('spell')). Crippling Fear authoring: Spell effect â†’ "Choose a creature type, thenâ€¦" â†’ inner "All creatures get Â±X/Â±X" (power -3, toughness -3, scope all, âœ“ "Creatures NOT of that type", Creature type BLANK â€” injected from the choice). Distant Melody's count-draw still isn't form-representable (count-amounts aren't), but choose_creature_type + pump_all is. Authoring JSON: `{type:'choose_creature_type', effects:[{type:'pump_all', power:-3, toughness:-3, scope:'all', exclude_type:true}]}`.
- **`choose_player` = "target player X" â€” the chosen player is the recipient of ALL inner effects.** On resolution the engine REWRITES every inner effect's `recipient` to `'controller'` and applies them with `p_controller_id` = the chosen player (`submit_decision`, mig 170 line ~582: `e.value || jsonb_build_object('recipient','controller')`). So inside `choose_player` the recipient field is meaningless (overridden), and the subject is the chosen player, never the caster. **"Target player draws N" (Deep Analysis) = `choose_player(filter:'any') â†’ draw N`** â€” already fully supported (engine + form + flashback); no new primitive needed (another false-alarm triage item, like Champion of the Perished). **Form labeling caveat (fixed this session):** the `draw` effect was labelled "You draw cards", which misread inside choose_player. Fixed by (a) neutralizing draw's label to "Draw cards" (the drawer is the effect's controller â€” source's controller in a trigger/spell, caster in a `then` rider, chosen player in choose_player), and (b) binding the subject at the wrapper: choose_player's label is "Choose a player, then that playerâ€¦" and its effects field label is "That player:". NOTE: the registry disambiguates effect VARIANTS by field-shape (`resolveEffectDef`), so you can't add a same-shape variant (e.g. a "chosen-context draw" with the same `[amount]` fields) â€” distinguish by a differing field (the rider variants drop `recipient`) or fix the label instead.
- **Flashback (mig 174):** This engine moves a non-permanent spell out of its cast zone AT CAST TIME (handâ†’graveyard inside `cast_spell_effect`), keeping a separate `spell_effect` stack item that resolves the program. So flashback's "then exile it" is modelled as the graveyardâ†’exile move at cast time (card ends in exile whether the spell resolves or is countered â€” correct for flashback). `cast_spell_effect` already had NO source-zone filter, so a graveyard source was structurally castable; the flashback branch reads the card's `script ->> 'flashback'` cost, pays it instead of the printed cost, and requires it (graveyard cast without a flashback cost now raises). Tapped tokens: the `create_token` branch of `apply_triggered_ability_effects` honours a `tapped` flag (spell-effect tokens route there via apply_trigger_effects â†’ apply_targeted_triggered_ability_effects â†’ apply_triggered_ability_effects).
  - **Flashback "Pay N life" additional cost (mig 176):** flashback is a plain mana-cost STRING (`script.flashback`) consumed in 5 places (schema, card-behavior type/normalize, builder build/parse, `cast_spell_effect`, ControllerListV4 button). An additional life payment is a SEPARATE optional `flashback_life` integer (NOT an object â€” keeps every string consumer untouched). `cast_spell_effect`'s graveyard branch pays the mana then deducts `flashback_life` from `game_session_players.life_total` (raises if life < cost; can't pay life you don't have). Form: a "+ pay N life" number beside the flashback mana input; build emits `flashback` (possibly '') whenever flashback mana OR life is present so the engine's graveyard-cast gate (needs the `flashback` key) still fires for a life-only flashback. Deep Analysis = `{flashback:'{1}{U}', flashback_life:3}`. The controller flashback button now also renders "+N life".
  - **Flashback that does DIFFERENT/extra stuff than the hand cast (mig 177, the "Increasing" cycle).** Optional `flashback_effect: { actions: [...] }` (same shape as spell_effect) REPLACES spell_effect when cast from the graveyard. **Engine-ENFORCED, not client-trusted:** `cast_spell_effect` selects the program by cast zone (`if v_source_zone='graveyard' and flashback_effect.actions present â†’ use it, else p_actions`) BEFORE the X-resolution â€” so the client can pass the normal actions and the engine still runs the flashback program (can't be substituted). Because the engine enforces it, NO client change was needed for untargeted "do more" cards (the controller keeps sending the normal actions). Authoring: `BuilderForm.flashbackEffect` (a second spell-action list, rendered by the factored `SpellActionList` shared with the normal Spell-effect section); build emits `flashback` (possibly '') whenever any flashback facet (mana/life/effect) is present. Increasing Devotion = `spell_effect` create 5 + `flashback_effect` create 10. Caveat: a flashback_effect that needs NEW targets/decisions the client didn't set up for the normal cast isn't wired in the controller yet (untargeted programs only).
- **Cast-from-graveyard (mig 173):** Alternate cast ZONES are modelled as a player-scoped permission, not a rewrite of the cast path. A `cast_from_graveyard` continuous-effect row (`affected_player_id` + `payload.type_line` filter, `expires_at_phase='ending'/step='cleanup'`, NOT flagged `registered_from_card_script` so rebuild leaves it) is written by a `grant_cast_from_graveyard` effect branch; `cast_card_from_hand` then accepts `zone in ('hand','graveyard')` and gates a graveyard source on a matching permission. End-of-turn sweep is automatic via the existing `expire_continuous_effects_for_step`. This was the deferred "Noctis-class" frontier â€” turned out small because the cast path is one function and the permission reuses existing continuous-effect machinery.
- **Project:** LeylineSync
- **Description:** Realtime Magic: The Gathering style board/controller app built with Next.js and Supabase.
- **Card behavior resolution chain:** runtime reads behavior as `coalesce(game_cards.copied_script, cards.script)` across ~10 SQL functions (casting, rebuild_scripted_continuous_effects, activate_ability, combat keyword registration). `copied_script` = per-instance copy override; `cards.script` = base.
- **The Scryfall importer never writes `cards.script`** (scripts/import-scryfall-cards.mjs `mapScryfallCardToRow` omits it) and upserts `onConflict: 'id'`, so `ON CONFLICT DO UPDATE` leaves `cards.script` untouched â†’ authored behavior survives reimports. This is why Phase 2 authored directly onto `cards.script` instead of building a separate oracle_id-keyed override table.
- **`cards.id` is the Scryfall printing id, not oracle identity.** `oracle_id` (added migration 075) is the card identity shared across printings; importer now persists it. Use `relink_card_scripts()` to re-attach a script if the representative printing for an oracle changes between imports.
- **State-based actions:** 0-toughness death (rule 704.5f) ignores indestructible; lethal marked damage (704.5g) is prevented by indestructible. Both handled in `move_lethal_damaged_creatures_to_graveyard` (migration 074).
- **Triggered abilities (migrations 076â€“077):** events detected by DB row triggers (mirrors the `cease_token` pattern). `fire_zone_change_triggers` on `game_cards` handles ETB (zoneâ†’battlefield) and dies (battlefieldâ†’graveyard); `fire_upkeep_triggers` on `game_turn_state` stepâ†’upkeep; `fire_attack_triggers` on `game_combat_assignments` insert. Each match calls `fire_card_triggers` â†’ `enqueue_triggered_ability`, which inserts a `triggered_ability` stack item with effects + controller + source card name (`label`) baked into the payload (so resolution + display survive the source leaving). `resolve_top_of_stack` applies untargeted effects (gain_life/lose_life/deal_damage to controller|each_opponent, draw). Zone-change trigger name `trg_a_fire_zone_change` sorts before `trg_cease_token_off_battlefield` so a token's dies trigger enqueues before cease-to-exist; `game_stack_items.source_card_id` is ON DELETE SET NULL so the stack item survives, and `get_stack_items` coalesces `source_card.name` with the payload `label`. **Only targeted triggers remain unbuilt.**
- **`get_stack_items` was redefined in migrations 030â†’032â†’033**; the live version (033) has extra `target_player_id`/`target_username` columns. When reproducing it, base on 033, not 030, or you silently drop columns the client `StackItem` type depends on.
- **Triggered-ability effects live in `apply_triggered_ability_effects` (migration 078)** â€” a helper `resolve_top_of_stack` calls for the `triggered_ability` branch. To add a new auto-resolved trigger effect, edit this one function (no longer reproduce the whole resolve_top_of_stack). Supported: gain_life, lose_life, deal_damage (recipient controller|each_opponent), draw, create_token (by token name from seeded catalog), add_counters (+1/+1 on source). create_token inserts battlefield game_cards which itself fires the ETB zone-change trigger â€” intended.
- **Card behavior authoring stack:** `/cards/behavior` editor has Form mode (guided builder, `components/CardBehaviorForm.tsx` + model/codec in `lib/game/card-behavior-builder.ts`), JSON mode, and âœ¨ Generate-with-AI. The builder's vocabulary constants are the single source of truth: the form dropdowns, the LLM prompt (`lib/game/card-behavior-llm.ts` â†’ `buildBehaviorAuthoringGuide`), and validation (`validateCardScript`) all derive from / agree on them. To add a new effect type, extend the builder + the Zod schema; the form and AI follow. AI route: `app/api/cards/generate-behavior/route.ts` â€” auth-gated, `claude-opus-4-8`, adaptive thinking, cached system prompt, validates output with `validateCardScript` and retries once; guarded by `ANTHROPIC_API_KEY` (returns 501 if unset). SDK: `@anthropic-ai/sdk`.
- **Reusable internal effect helpers:** `draw_card`/`adjust_player_life` RPCs gate on `auth.uid()` so they can't be reused for an arbitrary trigger controller; triggered-ability resolution applies life/draw inline against the payload's `controller_player_id` instead.
- **Spell effect types via the stack (migration 079):** `spell_effect.actions` types map to stack action types in `getSpellPlan` (ControllerListV4): `deal_damage`â†’deal_damage_creature/player, `pump`â†’pump_creature, `destroy/bounce/tap/untap`â†’`*_creature` (kind `creature_effect`, one shared V4 picker via `CREATURE_EFFECT_MAP`), `draw`â†’`draw_cards` (untargeted, kind `draw`, cast button calls onDrawCards not onCastCard). `draw_cards` resolution reuses `apply_triggered_ability_effects` with a synthetic `{type:draw}` effect (pass null source). destroyâ†’owner's graveyard (fires `dies` triggers, intended), bounceâ†’owner's hand (does NOT fire dies â€” that's only battlefieldâ†’graveyard); both reset is_tapped/damage/counters and controllerâ†’owner. **Gotcha:** `doesCardRequireStackTarget` returns true for ANY instant/sorcery whose oracle_text contains "target", which would gate these on a non-empty stack (counterspell behavior). `getSpellPlan` must classify the new kinds BEFORE the counterspell fallback, and `canCastHandSpell` special-cases damage/pump/creature_effect/draw to cast at natural speed bypassing `getCanQuickCast`.
- **Trigger event detection is fully decoupled from targeting (migrations 076â€“082).** `fire_card_triggers(session, game_card, events[])` scans the card's effective script for `triggered_abilities` whose `event` matches and calls `enqueue_triggered_ability` â€” identically for every event. So adding a new event = add a DETECTOR that calls fire_card_triggers with new event names; targeting/target_controller work automatically. Detectors: `fire_zone_change_triggers` (game_cards zone change â†’ enters_the_battlefield/dies/leaves_the_battlefield), `fire_turn_step_triggers` (game_turn_state step change â†’ beginning_of_upkeep/draw_step/end_step; migration 082 replaced the upkeep-only `fire_upkeep_triggers`), `fire_attack_triggers` (game_combat_assignments insert â†’ attacks), `fire_block_triggers` (game_combat_blockers insert â†’ blocks), `fire_target_triggers` (game_stack_items insert for creature-target action_types â†’ becomes_targeted; INSERT-only so it's loop-free and lands above the targeting item). Builder vocabulary `BUILDER_TRIGGER_EVENTS` (card-behavior-builder.ts) must list a new event's primary value or the form rejects it (parseTriggeredAbilities) and the LLM guide won't mention it; SQL accepts the aliases. Event field in Zod schema is just z.string() (no validation gate).
- **Targeted creature triggers + controller restriction (migrations 080â€“081):** triggered_ability stack items carry `target_required`/`target_card_id`/`target_controller` in payload. Controller picks the creature via `choose_triggered_ability_creature_target` RPC (client: `chooseTriggeredAbilityCreatureTarget`; UI: `TargetedTriggerPrompt` + `mustChooseTriggerTarget` blocks passing priority via `blockPassReason`). A trigger effect requires a chosen creature target ONLY when its type is targetable (deal_damage/destroy/bounce/tap/untap/add_counters) AND `target_type` is **creature-only** (`behavior_target_type_is_creature_only`) â€” "any target" damage triggers fall through to `apply_triggered_ability_effects`' each_opponent default instead of being dropped. `target_controller` (any|opponent|you; normalized from any/opponent/you/self/controller) enforced by SQL helpers `session_has_targetable_creature` + `creature_target_controller_ok`, used in enqueue (existence check), choose, resolve fizzle guard, and put_action_on_stack (spell casts). Client mirror: `creatureMatchesController` / `readTargetController` filter pickers; SpellPlan kinds carry `targetController`; put-on-stack action fns take a trailing optional `targetController` param. No-legal-target softlock avoided: enqueue won't enqueue if no legal creature; resolve guard only raises when a legal creature still exists, else fizzles.
- **Battlefieldâ†’graveyard chokepoint `put_in_graveyard(session, game_card)` (migration 084, Phase 0 of the rules-engine cleanup).** Single primitive for the dies/leaves-to-grave transition (returns bool; standard cleanup: zoneâ†’graveyard at owner's next position, controllerâ†’owner, is_tapped=false, damage_marked=0, dealt_deathtouch_damage=false, plus_one_counters=0). It does NOT rebuild continuous effects or fire triggers â€” the per-row zone-change trigger fires dies/leaves automatically; callers rebuild once after a batch. All three death sites route through it: `move_lethal_damaged_creatures_to_graveyard` (now snapshots the dying id set with array_agg, then loops put_in_graveyard â€” preserves "evaluate dying set once"), `resolve_top_of_stack` destroy_creature, `apply_targeted_triggered_ability_effects` destroy. This is the seam for the future finality counter / death-replacement layer (change one function) and for moving resolution to app code. Note: exileâ†’exile and bounceâ†’hand stay inline (different zones); counter_spell stackâ†’graveyard is NOT a battlefield death and is untouched. Deliberate harmless unification: SBA deaths now also reset controllerâ†’owner (graveyard cards are owned, not controlled). **The decision (from the architecture discussion): keep authority + atomicity in Postgres; centralize in SQL (put_in_graveyard, future apply_effect / effective_characteristics); only build a pure-TS `reduce(state,action)` rules core at the replacement-effect/layer frontier (Noctis-class) â€” justified by shared client/server optimistic UI + deterministic replay, NOT a rewrite-now.**
- **Effect roadmap + exile/mill (migration 083, README "Effect roadmap" `<details>` block).** Adding a creature-targeting effect = mirror destroy everywhere it appears: the action_type CHECK constraint, `trigger_effect_requires_creature_target` list, `apply_targeted_triggered_ability_effects` branch, `put_action_on_stack` (not-in list + combined creature-target validation branch + payload case), `resolve_top_of_stack` branch, plus client `CREATURE_EFFECT_MAP` (key = spell action type e.g. `exile`â†’`exile_creature`), `TargetedCreatureActionType`, and schema (`z.enum(['destroy','exile','bounce','tap','untap'])` + KNOWN_V2_ACTION_TYPES). exile â†’ owner's exile zone (fires leaves_the_battlefield, not dies). Adding an auto-resolved (untargeted) effect = edit ONLY `apply_triggered_ability_effects` + Zod member + KNOWN_V2_ACTION_TYPES + LLM prose; mill lives there (recipient controller default/each_opponent/each_player, mills top-of-library â†’ graveyard). mill is trigger-only â€” no spell action yet (player-targeted mill needs a player picker). Effects authored via JSON/AI + Zod, NOT the guided form (BUILDER_EFFECT_TYPES), same as the targeted-creature effects â€” only add to BUILDER_EFFECT_TYPES if you also add form model/parse/serialize/UI.
- **Effective-script accessor `effective_script(session, game_card)` (migration 085, Phase 0).** Single STABLE SECURITY DEFINER function returning `coalesce(game_cards.copied_script, cards.script)` (null if the card isn't in the session). Replaces the inlined coalesce in the 3 *live* callers: `register_card_continuous_effects` (was 067), `activate_ability` (was 072), `fire_card_triggers` (was 077) â€” all other historical hits (044/048/049/050/055/063/064/067 register redefinitions) were superseded. Each caller reproduced verbatim with ONLY the script fetch swapped (activate_ability keeps its zone+ownership check by selecting `zone` alone then calling the accessor; register keeps reading `cards.keywords` separately since keywords are base-card data, not script). Behavior-preserving today; it is the one seam where DFC active-face â†’ face-specific script selection will live. NOTE: `rebuild_scripted_continuous_effects` (063) uses a *different* shape â€” `card_behavior_has_continuous_effects(coalesce(copied_script,'{}'))` (presence prefilter, no fallback to cards.script) â€” left untouched, not part of this accessor.
- **Creature-effect primitive `apply_creature_effect(session, kind, target_card_id, params)` (migration 086, Phase 0).** Single SECURITY DEFINER function owning every targeted-creature mutation â€” kind âˆˆ {deal_damage, destroy, exile, bounce, tap, untap, add_counters, pump}; params jsonb carries `amount` (deal_damage/add_counters) or `power`/`toughness` (pump). No-ops if target null or off-battlefield (fizzle). destroy â†’ put_in_graveyard; deal_damage re-runs move_lethal SBAs. Both former call sites now delegate: `apply_targeted_triggered_ability_effects` passes the effect `type` as the kind (non-creature effects still defer to `apply_triggered_ability_effects`); `resolve_top_of_stack` collapsed its 8 `*_creature` action branches into ONE `in (...)` branch that derives the kind via `regexp_replace(action_type,'_creature$','')` and hands the whole payload as params. This was the last logic duplication of the "mirror destroy in 2 places" tax. **Updated rule for adding a creature-targeting effect:** implement the mutation ONCE in apply_creature_effect, then only the declarations/validation remain (action_type CHECK constraint, `trigger_effect_requires_creature_target` list, `put_action_on_stack`, client `CREATURE_EFFECT_MAP`/`TargetedCreatureActionType`, Zod enum + KNOWN_V2_ACTION_TYPES) â€” no duplicated branch logic. Safe because `trigger_effect_requires_creature_target` only admits types apply_creature_effect handles, so a trigger effect can't hit its `else raise`. With this + effective_script (085) + put_in_graveyard (084), the two SQL Phase-0 centralizations from the Decision Log are complete; remaining Phase-0/1 work is the untargeted side already lives solely in apply_triggered_ability_effects, then the generic "pending decision" state machine.
- **Rules-engine test harness (`tests/`, the "test chamber").** Programmatic regression suite driving the real RPCs against **local Supabase** Postgres. Key facts: (1) uses a **direct `pg` connection, not supabase-js**, because `auth.uid()` resolves from `request.jwt.claims ->> 'sub'` and only a raw connection can set that GUC on the same connection before the RPC â€” `harness/db.ts` `asPlayer(client, playerId, fn)` does `set_config('request.jwt.claims', {sub,role}, true)` + `set local role authenticated`, then `reset role` so assertions read tables as postgres (RLS bypassed). (2) Each test runs in a transaction rolled back at the end (`withRolledBackTx`) â†’ isolation without `db reset`. (3) **No `auth.users` seeding needed** â€” `game_session_players.player_id` has NO FK to auth.users (migration 009), so any random uuid is a valid player. (4) Setup reuses existing `dev_*` RPCs (`dev_spawn_card`, `dev_set_turn_state`, `dev_clear_summoning_sickness`). (5) `resolve_top_of_stack` can be called directly (doesn't require priority to have passed â€” that's `pass_priority`'s job), so it's a clean unit-resolve. Runner: `node --import tsx --test` (node:test, no vitest); Node's `--test` glob is unreliable on Windows so package.json points at the file explicitly. `Scenario` API in `harness/scenario.ts`: create/spawn/spawnCreature/setTurn/as(seat).putOnStack|activate/resolveStack + inspectors. **VERIFIED WORKING 2026-06-02** â€” proving trio (R1 destroyâ†’put_in_graveyard, R8 activateâ†’effective_script, R11 draw) passes. **Local schema = SQUASH, not migration replay** (see Decision Log + bug-104): `supabase/migrations/` holds only `00000000000000_baseline.sql` (full hosted `db dump --schema public`, reproduces prod incl. 079-086) + `00000000000001_local_test_relax_fks.sql` (LOCAL ONLY â€” drops the auth.users/profiles FK chain so throwaway player UUIDs work; never apply to hosted). The 88 incremental migrations were moved to `supabase/migrations_archive/` (Supabase ignores them; kept as history). `% Test` cards are schema-only-dump-excluded, so the harness seeds them from `tests/fixtures/test-cards.json` via `ensureTestCards` (committed once, idempotent). Gotchas burned in: turn **phases** are `beginning|main_1|combat|main_2|ending` (NOT the step names â€” `precombat_main` is a step; a main-phase instant window = phase `main_1` + step `precombat_main`); `asPlayer` cleanup must be try/catch-wrapped or a failed RPC's real error is masked by 25P02 on the aborted tx; FK chain is `game_cards.owner_id -> profiles.id -> auth.users.id`. `supabase/_hosted_schema.sql` is the gitignored scratch dump used to author the baseline.
- **Phase 1 pending-decision state machine (migrations 087-088).** 087 extracts `finalize_stack_resolution(session, stack_item)` â€” the shared resolve tail (mark resolved â†’ rebuild_scripted_continuous_effects â†’ reset priority â†’ maybe_finish â†’ return json); `resolve_top_of_stack` now ends with `return finalize_stack_resolution(...)`. 088 adds `game_pending_decisions` (id, session, deciding_player_id, source_stack_item_id, decision_type, prompt, options jsonb, min/max_choices, status pending|resolved|cancelled, result jsonb), `submit_decision(decision_id, result)` (the single entry point â€” validates deciding player + legal choice), `get_pending_decisions(session)`, `stack_item_has_pending_decision(item)`, and the **modal Tier-A** vertical slice: `cast_modal_spell(session, modes jsonb, choose, source)` puts a `modal_spell` stack item + a `choose_mode` decision; `resolve_top_of_stack` gained a `modal_spell` branch that refuses to resolve until the decision is `resolved`, then runs the chosen mode(s)' actions via `apply_triggered_ability_effects`. **Tier-A modes are UNTARGETED only for now** (targeted modes need target-selection, a later slice). Added `modal_spell` to the `game_stack_items_action_type_check` constraint. Result shape for choose_mode: `{"chosen":[idx,...]}` (or a single int). This is the seam for scry/distribute/choose-player (more decision_types) and Tier-B resolution-time decisions (park item â†’ submit_decision applies outcome â†’ finalize_stack_resolution).
- **Phase 1 Tier-B resolution-time decisions â€” scry (migration 089).** First true suspend/resume through `finalize_stack_resolution`. Contrast with Tier-A modal (088), where the decision is created on announcement and resolution merely refuses until it's chosen: in Tier-B the decision exists ONLY because resolution reached a point needing input. Flow: `cast_scry(session, amount, source)` pushes a `scry` stack item (no decision). `resolve_top_of_stack`'s `scry` branch looks at the top N of the caster's library, creates the `scry` decision (options = `[{game_card_id,name,library_position}]`), sets the stack item status to **`awaiting_decision`**, and **returns early `{awaiting_decision:true,...}` WITHOUT calling finalize** â€” so the `where status='pending'` resolve query never re-picks it (no re-entry guard needed). `submit_decision`'s `scry` branch (result `{top:[id...],bottom:[id...]}`, each ordered top-to-bottom) validates the submitted ids are exactly the revealed set (count match, no dups, all in options), renumbers the WHOLE library (chosen top first in order â†’ un-revealed cards keeping order â†’ chosen bottom in order, `row_number()`-1), then calls `finalize_stack_resolution(session, source_stack_item_id)` to resume. Required two constraint widenings: `'scry'` added to `game_stack_items_action_type_check` (full list = 088 + scry) and **`'awaiting_decision'`** added to `game_stack_items_status_check` (was pending|resolved|cancelled). Library convention: top = LOWEST zone_position (matches draw / dev_undo_last_draw). Empty library â†’ finalize immediately (nothing to scry). Harness: `Scenario.castScry(amount)` + `libraryIds(seat)` (ordered top-to-bottom); test gotcha â€” in Tier-B the decision only appears AFTER `resolveStack()`, so call castScry â†’ resolveStack â†’ pendingDecision (SC3/4/5 failed first run by reading pendingDecision before resolving). Suite now 34/34. This validates the 087 seam end-to-end; the same parkâ†’submitâ†’finalize shape generalizes to surveil/order_cards/distribute.
- **Scry authorable in the card behavior editor (no migration â€” TS only).** Added `scry` as a V2 spell action: `card-behavior-schema.ts` (`KNOWN_V2_ACTION_TYPES` + union member `{type:'scry', amount:number}` â€” added BOTH per the catch-all gotcha), `card-behavior-llm.ts` (spell-action list entry + a "Scry 2. (instant)" example so the AI generator authors it), and the cast path in `ControllerListV4.tsx`: `SpellPlan` gained `{kind:'scry',amount,timing}`, `getSpellPlan` detects a `scry` action (after `draw`), `canCastHandSpell` casts it at natural speed, the card sheet got an `onScry` prop wired to a new `scrySpell` dispatch action â†’ `castScrySpell` wrapper in `actions.ts` â†’ `cast_scry` RPC. Scry is **untargeted** (acts on the caster's own library) so it follows the `draw` plan shape, not a target picker. Mirrors the destroy/exile/mill precedent: spell effects are authored via **AI/JSON + Zod validation**, NOT the guided form (the form models only keywords/triggers/activated abilities â€” it has NO spell_effect widget for ANY spell). **CAVEAT â€” trigger-scry validates but does NOT execute yet:** the schema accepts `{type:'scry'}` inside a triggered ability, but `apply_triggered_ability_effects` applies trigger effects inline and can't park mid-resolution, so a trigger that scrys is a no-op. Making trigger-scry (and trigger-surveil) work needs generalizing the Tier-B park/resume to fire from within a (possibly multi-effect) trigger resolution â€” planned alongside surveil. **CAVEAT â€” no in-game decision UI yet:** casting a scry spell puts it on the stack and it parks on resolution (status awaiting_decision), but there is no client `<PendingDecisionPrompt>`/`usePendingDecisions`/`submitDecision` wrapper, so a human player currently has no way to submit the top/bottom ordering. The authoring + cast-to-stack path is complete; the resolution prompt UI is the remaining client-wiring piece for live play.
- **Surveil (migration 090) â€” Tier-B, mirrors scry exactly.** Look at top N of library, bin any number into the graveyard, rest back on top. `cast_surveil` + a shared `scry`/`surveil` park branch in resolve_top_of_stack (`action_type in ('scry','surveil')`, decision_type = the action_type, prompt `initcap(type)||' '||N`) + a `surveil` branch in submit_decision. submit_decision result: `{graveyard:[id...], top:[id...]}` â€” together must equal the revealed set (count/dup/subset validated). On resume: move graveyard ids to graveyard (`zone='graveyard'`, position `max+ord`, `is_tapped=false`, in submitted order), renumber remaining library (kept-top first then un-revealed), `finalize_stack_resolution`. Added `'surveil'` to the action_type CHECK. Authoring identical to scry: schema action `{type:'surveil', amount}`, LLM guide + "Surveil 1." example, `SpellPlan {kind:'surveil'}` + `getSpellPlan`/`canCastHandSpell`/`onSurveil`/`surveilSpell`/`castSurveilSpell`. Harness `castSurveil` + tests SV1-4. Same two caveats as scry (no trigger-execution, no in-game decision UI).
- **Targeted modal modes (migration 091) + apply_modal_spell extraction.** A chosen modal mode's actions may now target a creature (charm pattern: "Choose one â€” destroy target creature; or gain 3 life"). The target rides on the choose_mode submission: `submit_decision(choose_mode, {chosen:[idx], target_card_id})`. submit_decision's choose_mode branch detects whether any chosen mode has a creature-targeting action (`type in (deal_damage,destroy,exile,bounce,tap,untap,add_counters,pump)` AND target_type `"creature"` scalar or array-contains-creature) and, if so, REQUIRES `target_card_id` to be a battlefield creature in the session (else raises). **Extracted `apply_modal_spell(session, stack_item)`** â€” runs a resolved modal: per chosen mode, per action, a creature-target action â†’ `apply_creature_effect(session, type, target, action)` (behavior action type == apply_creature_effect kind, so no mapping needed; action json carries amount/power/toughness as params), else untargeted via `apply_triggered_ability_effects`. resolve_top_of_stack's modal_spell branch is now one line (`perform apply_modal_spell(...)`) and dropped its v_decision/v_mode_index/v_mode locals â€” same "centralize the tail" move as finalize_stack_resolution, so future modal changes touch ONE function. Harness tests MDT1 (destroy chosen creature), MDT2 (untargeted mode of a targeted modal needs no target), MDT3 (targeted mode without target rejected). Suite 41/41. **NOT yet authorable:** modal needs a new script shape (`spell_effect.modes` or similar) + a mode/target cast UI â€” bigger client feature, deferred; cast_modal_spell/cast_scry/cast_surveil are reachable from the harness but only scry/surveil have the spell-action authoring + cast button.
- **Pending-decision client UI (migration 092 + TS, no engine change).** Closes the "no in-game decision UI" caveat for scry/surveil/modal. Data: `getPendingDecisions(supabase, session)` (data.ts, wraps `get_pending_decisions`); `submitDecision(supabase, decisionId, result)` action (actions.ts, wraps `submit_decision`); types `PendingDecision`/`ScryOption`/`ModalModeOption` (types.ts). `useControllerGameState` fetches `pendingDecisions` in its Promise.all + adds a realtime sub on `game_pending_decisions`; exposes the array. ControllerListV4 picks `myPendingDecision = pendingDecisions.find(deciding_player_id === playerId)`, threads it + an `onSubmitDecision` action through `MainArea` (alongside `onChooseTriggerTarget`), and renders `<PendingDecisionPrompt>` next to `TargetedTriggerPrompt`. The prompt branches on decision_type: `ChooseModeBody` (toggle modes respecting min/max; if a chosen mode has a creature-target action â€” `modalModeIsTargeted` via CREATURE_TARGET_ACTION_TYPES + targetTypeMatches â€” show a battlefield-creature picker; submits `{chosen, target_card_id?}`), `ScrySurveilBody` (per-card Top vs Bottom(scry)/Graveyard(surveil) toggle, submits `{top,bottom}` or `{graveyard,top}`; order within a bucket = revealed order â€” drag-reorder is a future refinement). **Realtime gotcha (migration 092):** a new table emits postgres_changes only if it's in the `supabase_realtime` publication â€” `game_pending_decisions` wasn't, so 092 adds it (guarded by pg_publication_tables since ADD TABLE errors if already a member). Without it the prompt still appeared via coattails (the stack-item change from cast/resolve triggers a full reload) but a decision-only change wouldn't push. **Confirmed working in the running app by the user (2026-06-02)** â€” the decision prompt renders and the scry/surveil/modal flow completes end-to-end (typecheck + lint clean; harness 44/44).
- **Scry/surveil from a triggered ability â€” resumable trigger resolution (migration 093).** Closes the "trigger-scry validates but doesn't execute" caveat. New `apply_trigger_effects(session, stack_item, start_index) returns uuid` walks a trigger's `effects` from start_index: a normal effect is applied immediately (reusing `apply_targeted_triggered_ability_effects` per-effect â€” it already dispatches creature-target vs untargeted); a scry/surveil effect creates a pending decision, stashes the NEXT index on the stack item (`payload.resume_index`), parks it (`status='awaiting_decision'`), and returns the decision id (null = ran to completion). `resolve_top_of_stack`'s triggered_ability branch keeps the target_required fizzle check, then calls apply_trigger_effects(â€¦,0) and returns early `{awaiting_decision}` if parked. `submit_decision`'s scry & surveil tails, after the reorder/bin, look up the source stack item's action_type: if `triggered_ability`, RESUME via apply_trigger_effects(â€¦, resume_index) (which may park again on a later scry) and finalize only when it returns null; a standalone `scry`/`surveil` spell item still just finalizes. Proven by tests TSC1 (ETB scry parks+resolves), TSC2 (ETB surveil bins), TSC3 (an effect AFTER the scry runs only on resume â€” fixture "Scry Then Gain Test" = [scry, gain_life], life unchanged until submit). The refactor (per-effect application) did not regress the existing trigger tests. Suite 44/44.
- **Scry/surveil added to the guided Form (builder + form UI).** Two homes, both now functional: (1) **Trigger effect** â€” added to `BUILDER_EFFECT_TYPES` (+ BuilderEffect union, defaultEffect, effectToJson, parseEffects); the form's EffectEditor already renders a generic amount input, so no per-type UI needed. Works via migration 093. (2) **New "Spell effect (instant/sorcery)" section** â€” the form had NO spell-effect section before.
