Added `BuilderSpellEffect`/`BUILDER_SPELL_EFFECT_TYPES` (none|scry|surveil), `BuilderForm.spellEffect`, buildScriptFromForm emits `spell_effect.actions:[{type,amount}]` (+ included in the empty-script check), parseScriptToForm adds `spell_effect` to knownKeys + `parseSpellEffect` (returns the model only for a single scry/surveil action; ANYTHING else â€” destroy/exile/damage/multi-action â€” returns null so the editor stays in JSON mode, preserving prior behavior). New "Spell effect" section in CardBehaviorForm.tsx (select + amount). **Gotcha:** `CardBehaviorEditor.tsx`'s `emptyBuilderForm()` literal also needed the new `spellEffect` field (tsc caught it). Round-trips verified: scry-spell â†” form, surveil-trigger â†” form, destroy-spell â†’ null (JSON mode). The LLM guide already documents scry/surveil; the form vocab is independent.
- **Multi-action untargeted spell program + the scry/surveil graveyard fix (migration 094).** Two bugs the user hit authoring Opt ("Scry 1, then draw a card"): (1) `cast_scry`/`cast_surveil` never moved the spell card to the graveyard (unlike `put_action_on_stack`, which bins an instant/sorcery on cast â€” baseline ~L5354), so a scry instant stayed in hand; (2) the cast path dispatched only ONE effect, so scry+draw couldn't both happen. Fix: a non-permanent spell's `spell_effect.actions` is an effect PROGRAM resolved like a trigger's effects. New `cast_spell_effect(session, actions, source)` mirrors put_action_on_stack's timing rules + handâ†’graveyard move and pushes a `spell_effect` stack item carrying `{effects, controller_player_id}`. `resolve_top_of_stack` gained a `spell_effect` branch that runs `apply_trigger_effects(â€¦,0)` (parks on scry/surveil); `submit_decision`'s scry/surveil resume now fires for source action_type `in ('triggered_ability','spell_effect')`. Added `'spell_effect'` to the action_type CHECK. **Client cast path changed:** `getSpellPlan` now returns `{kind:'spell_effect', actions}` for any spell whose actions contain scry/surveil and are all in `UNTARGETED_SPELL_ACTION_TYPES` (scry/surveil/draw/gain_life/lose_life/mill/create_token) â€” this SUPERSEDES the old single-action `scry`/`surveil` plan kinds (removed). Dispatch â†’ `castSpellEffect` (actions.ts) â†’ `cast_spell_effect`. So scry/surveil spells (incl. Opt) now go through the program path and hit the graveyard; the standalone `cast_scry`/`cast_surveil` RPCs remain only for the harness/direct use. **This RESOLVES the earlier "make scry/surveil the spell's only action" caveat for untargeted combos** â€” Opt and similar now work end-to-end (test SE1: cardâ†’graveyard on cast, scry parks, draw runs on resume, 45/45). A spell mixing scry/surveil with a TARGETED action still isn't routed here (rare; would need target selection).
- **Form Spell-effect section is now a multi-action LIST (Opt is clickable).** `BuilderForm.spellEffect` changed from `BuilderSpellEffect | null` to `BuilderSpellEffect[]` (ordered list; empty = none). `BuilderSpellEffectType` gained `'draw'` (now scry|surveil|draw); `BUILDER_SPELL_EFFECT_TYPES` dropped the 'none' sentinel; added `defaultSpellEffect(type)`. buildScriptFromForm maps the list â†’ `spell_effect.actions`; `parseSpellEffect` now returns `BuilderSpellEffect[]|null` â€” accepts an actions array where EVERY action is a plain `{typeâˆˆscry/surveil/draw, amount}` (keys âŠ† {type,amount}), else null â†’ JSON mode (so targeted destroy/exile, recipient draws, unknown fields still bail). CardBehaviorForm.tsx renders the section as a list editor (+ Add spell action / type select / amount / âœ•), mirroring the trigger-effects pattern. `CardBehaviorEditor.tsx` `emptyBuilderForm()` now spreads `[...EMPTY_BUILDER_FORM.spellEffect]`. **getSpellPlan broadened:** routes to `spell_effect` when `allUntargeted && (hasScrySurveil || actions.length > 1)` â€” so a multi-action untargeted combo (e.g. Opt) works even via the form, while a single `draw` keeps its dedicated path. Round-trips verified (Opt â†” form; destroy & recipient-draw â†’ JSON mode). So Opt = [Scry 1, Draw 1] is now buildable by clicking in the form. No engine/migration change (094 already handles execution).
- **Validator catch-all gotcha (card-behavior-schema.ts):** `UnknownV2ActionSchema` accepts any action type NOT in `KNOWN_V2_ACTION_TYPES`. Adding a type name to that list WITHOUT also adding an explicit union member makes the catch-all reject it â†’ validation fails. Always add both together (learned adding pump/destroy/bounce/tap/untap).

- **Protection / colour model (mig 131, F3 slice 1).** Engine has NO colour column â€” a card's colours are derived from `cards.mana_cost` via the immutable `card_color_set(text) -> text[]` (full words white/blue/black/red/green; matches a protection effect's `payload.from`). Protection is just another `game_continuous_effects` row (effect_type `protection`, `payload.from`), authored in a card script's `continuous_effects` exactly like `flying` (register_card_continuous_effects reproduced + a protection arm; the Scryfall-keyword loop is NOT touched â€” bare "Protection" carries no colour). Accessors mirror the keyword accessors: `card_has_protection_from_color(session,card,color)` + the `_from_any(colors[])` fold. **T (can't-be-Targeted) seam = put_action_on_stack:** after the builder returns `v_built_payload`, if it has a `target_card_id` and the target has protection from any of `card_color_set(v_source_mana_cost)`, raise BEFORE paying mana. The trigger path (choose_triggered_ability_creature_target) checks vs the trigger SOURCE card's mana-cost colours. This central post-builder check means NO per-builder edits (every creature-target builder already emits `target_card_id`). D (damage) + B (block) gates are later slices.

- **Protection D (can't-be-Damaged) gate = COMBAT only (mig 132).** Targeted spell/ability/trigger damage is already covered by the T gate (a protected creature can't be chosen as the target). The only uncovered creature-damage path is combat (dealt without targeting). `resolve_combat_damage` (mig 127 lift) skips the `damage_marked` update at BOTH sites (attackerâ†’blocker, blockerâ†’attacker) when `card_has_protection_from_any(victim, game_card_color_set(dealer))`. **Damage is still ASSIGNED (CR 510.4)** â€” the `v_remaining_attacker_damage` decrement stays OUTSIDE the protection guard, so trample/remainder math is byte-identical; only the marking + creature-damage tally are gated. New helper `game_card_color_set(session, game_card) -> text[]` = `card_color_set(cards.mana_cost)`. Did NOT touch `apply_creature_effect` deal_damage (redundant with T gate). **Test gotcha:** a victim that takes LETHAL combat damage dies, and `put_in_graveyard` resets `damage_marked` to 0 â€” so assert the graveyard move, not `damage_marked`, for a creature that took lethal (only assert `damage_marked = 0` on a SURVIVOR whose damage was prevented). [[bug-303]]

- **Protection B (can't-be-Blocked) gate (mig 133).** declare_blocker (baseline lift â€” only def) rejects a blocker when `card_has_protection_from_any(attacker, game_card_color_set(blocker))` â€” i.e. the ATTACKER has protection from the BLOCKER's colour (CR 509.1b), one check after the flying-legality gate. Protection imposes NO "can't block" restriction on the protected creature itself â€” only the "can't be blocked by" direction (mirrors how the D gate still lets a protected creature deal its own damage). **F3 functional gates (T/D/B) are now complete; E (auras/equipment) deferred â€” not modelled.** **Design insight worth keeping:** once the B gate exists, the D-gate's *attacker-side* guard is unreachable in legal combat (a creature of the protected colour can't block the protected attacker, so it never deals it combat damage) â€” so a "protected attacker shielded from its blocker" test is impossible to set up; keep the SQL guard as defensive depth but only the *blocker-side* D case (a protected creature legally blocks/ is blocked by an enemy of its protected colour) is reachable + testable.

- **Attachment subsystem â€” Auras + Equipment (migs 134/135), the basis for protection's E gate.** `game_cards.attached_to uuid` (plain, no FK) links an Aura/Equipment to its host. A continuous effect authored `affected:'attached'` (aliases host/enchanted/equipped) registers with `affected_card_id = attached_to` so the existing accessors (card_effective_power, card_has_*) pick it up on the HOST; an unattached source grants nothing (register skips it). `attach_permanent(session, attachment, host)` = set attached_to + re-register. **Auras:** type_line ILIKE '%aura%'; `cast_card_from_hand` gained `p_target_card_id` (4-arg, dropped+recreated so 3-arg callers still resolve), validates the enchant target at announce; `handle_cast_permanent` (the cast_permanent handler, mig 104) attaches on resolution (re-validates; illegal target â†’ aura to graveyard). **Equipment:** `equip(session, equipment, target, generic)` dedicated RPC (sorcery speed, you control both, optional `equip_cost` from script, then attach) â€” chose a dedicated RPC over the activated_ability framework (simplest seam, mirrors cast_fight). **Cleanup is a trigger, not threaded into every removal site:** `cleanup_attachments_on_zone_change` AFTER UPDATE OF zone â€” when a card leaves the battlefield, its auras go to graveyard (put_in_graveyard) + its equipment detaches (stays), and a leaving attachment clears its own host effects + nulls attached_to. Kept AUTH-INDEPENDENT (no register/auth.uid() calls inside â€” direct effect deletes) so it's safe under any zone-change context, incl. postgres-run test updates. **Also added `pump` to register's script-authorable continuous-effect list** (was create_pt_pump-only) so +N/+N auras/equipment work via `{type:'pump', affected:'attached', payload:{power,toughness}}`. **F3 protection is now fully complete (T/D/B/E).**

- **Client protection/attachment wiring (V4 controller).** Per-card protection colours load via `getProtectionColors(session)` (reads game_continuous_effects effect_type='protection' â†’ affected_card_id â†’ [payload.from]) and fold onto BoardCard as `protection_colors` in use-controller-game-state, EXACTLY mirroring the existing `getActivePumpTotals`/`withPump` pattern (so an Aura/Equipment's +N/+N already shows with no extra work â€” pump effects fold by affected_card_id). A card's colours come from its mana_cost client-side via `manaCostColors` (mirrors server card_color_set). **Aura cast:** an Aura hand card (kind 'normal') intercepts handleCast â†’ an enchant-target picker â†’ castCardFromHand(card, undefined, target) [actions.ts gained a 4th target arg]. **Equip:** a battlefield Equipment shows an Equip button â†’ own-creature picker â†’ the `equip` RPC wrapper. **Pre-filter:** targetableCreatures drops protection-from-spell-colour creatures; the declare-blockers UI disables blockers whose colour the selected attacker is protected from (attacker.protection_colors âˆ© manaCostColors(blocker)). The server still enforces all of this â€” the client filter is UX only. **No automated UI test harness exists** â€” gate is tsc + lint + mirroring existing cast/picker patterns; the 350 engine tests are SQL-harness-only and unaffected by client edits.

- **Commander / command zone (mig 136, slice 1).** Added `'command'` to the game_cards zone CHECK; `game_cards.is_commander` + `command_zone_casts` (tax counter); `game_sessions.format` ('standard'|'commander'). **cast_commander(session, card, generic)** casts the caster's commander from zone='command' at sorcery speed (main phase, empty stack), paying printed cost then the tax as a SEPARATE `pay_mana_cost('{N}')` call (N = 2*command_zone_casts) â€” two calls keep the math simple and stay atomic in the one RPC tx; increments the counter; moves commandâ†’stack as a `cast_permanent` item so the existing handle_cast_permanent resolves it to the battlefield. **Commander returns to the command zone on death:** put_in_graveyard (baseline lift) redirects an is_commander card to zone='command' instead of graveyard â€” AUTO for now (CR 903.9 owner-choice + the non-death zones library/hand/exile are later refinements). Since move_lethal/destroy/SBA all route through put_in_graveyard, the death case is fully covered. **40 life:** set_commander_format(session) sets format + all players' life_total=40. Tests CM1-CM5. **Deferred (separate slices): commander DAMAGE (21-from-one tracking), deck legality (singleton + colour identity), and the deck-side commander designation/seeding.** Known nuance not yet handled: a commander redirected from battlefield still fires BOTH dies+leaves via fire_zone_change (real rules suppress 'dies' since it never reaches the graveyard).

- **Commander slice 2 â€” format-aware game start + commander damage (mig 137).** (1) `create_game_session` dropped the 0-arg form and is now `(p_format default 'standard')` â€” sets game_sessions.format + the host's starting life (40 commander / 20 standard); the harness's no-arg `create_game_session()` still resolves via the default. `join_game_session` reproduced to read the session format so EVERY joiner gets the right life (fixes the mig-136 late-joiner-at-20 gap). Client: createGameSession(supabase, format) passes it; the lobby dropped its separate set_commander_format call (still kept for flipping an existing game). (2) **Commander damage** = a `game_commander_damage(session,defender,source_card)` table (RLS: session players read; SECURITY-DEFINER writes â€” mirrors game_damage_prevention). Tracked at the ONE seam all player combat damage flows through: `apply_damage_to_player(..., is_combat=>true)` (mig 125 lift + a trailing block) â€” only when `p_is_combat` AND the source card `is_commander`. Upserts cumulative damage; at >=21 it sets the defender's life_total=0, and the end-of-combat maybe_finish_game_session turns that into the loss. So unblocked + trample commander damage both count; non-combat or non-commander damage doesn't. Tests CM6, CD1-3.

- **Commander slice 3 â€” deck side (mig 138).** `decks.commander_card_id` (a catalog cards.id; kept OUT of list_data = the other 99). `set_deck_commander(deck, card)` (owner-gated; null clears). **`spawn_deck_for_session(session, deck)`** is a NEW SQL RPC that replaces the untestable `spawn-deck` Deno edge function: seeds list_data into the library (shuffled via `row_number() over (order by random())` for 0-based zone_position) and, in a Commander game (`game_sessions.format='commander'`), puts the deck's commander into the command zone (is_commander=true) instead. One-deck-per-player guard (mirrors the edge fn). **The commander is EXCLUDED from the library seed** (`where v_format<>'commander' or v_commander is null or cid <> v_commander`) so a decklist that still lists the commander (import_deck_from_text dumps ALL cards incl. the commander into list_data) isn't double-seeded (once in library + once in command). Sample decklists in `docs/commander-decks/` (Krenko, Atraxa) for the paste-import flow. **import_deck_from_text (mig 139) now CAPTURES the commander:** it tracks the section header â€” the first card under a 'Commander' header â†’ the new deck's commander_card_id (still counted in list_data; spawn de-dups it from the library). No Commander section â†’ null (â˜… toggle still works). Tests DK5-7. Client: `spawnDeckForSession` now calls the RPC (edge fn is DEAD CODE, left in place â€” `supabase/functions/spawn-deck/` â€” to avoid deploy churn); `setDeckCommander` action; DeckManager got a per-card â˜… commander toggle; getDeckDetail/DeckDetail expose commander_card_id. Tests DK1-4. **DEFERRED:** the text importer (import_deck_from_text) still IGNORES a 'Commander' section line (line ~4333 baseline treats 'commander' like 'deck'/'sideboard') â€” capturing it into commander_card_id + full legality (100-card singleton, colour identity; no color_identity column yet) are later slices.

- **Deck-editor behavior readiness (client-only, no migration).** `getCardConfigStatus(card)` in lib/game/card-behavior.ts classifies a catalog card: **scripted** (script has actions/continuous_effects/triggered/activated/spell_effect), **vanilla** (no oracle_text, basic land, or oracle text that's ONLY engine-handled keywords after stripping `(reminder text)` â€” these play with no script), **needs** (has ability text but no script). The vanilla/needs split is a deliberate heuristic on oracle_text (HANDLED_KEYWORDS set). DeckManager shows a per-card badge + a deck summary (`N scripted Â· M vanilla Â· K need behavior`) + a **Behavior** link to `/cards/behavior?card=<id>`. getDeckDetail now selects `script, oracle_text` on deck cards. The behavior editor deep-links via `?card=`: the **page reads searchParams (server prop) and passes initialCardId** to CardBehaviorEditor â€” do NOT use useSearchParams in the editor (app-router build wants a Suspense boundary; the prop path avoids it). Heuristic verified by hand against 7 representative cards.

- **Deck editor insights + AI batch + colour identity (client-only, no migration).** `lib/game/deck-insights.ts` = pure, unit-tested helpers (manaValue, deckManaCurve/TypeBreakdown/ColorPips/AverageManaValue/LandCount, deckSingletonViolations, **cardColorIdentity** + **deckColorIdentityViolations**). DeckInsights.tsx renders curve bars / colour pips / types / singleton + colour-identity warnings. **Colour identity is DERIVED** (no color_identity column on `cards` â€” confirmed) from mana symbols in mana_cost AND oracle_text (so "{R}: ..." counts red) â€” approximate (misses colour indicators / "all colours"), fine as a builder guide. **Batch AI behavior gen:** DeckManager loops the deck's distinct 'needs'-behavior cards (getCardConfigStatus), POSTs each to `/api/cards/generate-behavior` ({name,type_line,oracle_text} â†’ {script}), saves via setCardScript; sequential, confirm dialog (tokens), progress counter, aborts the whole batch if the route 501s / says "not configured" (no ANTHROPIC_API_KEY). DeckManager also got copy-as-text/clone(import round-trip)/sample-hand/image-preview/sort/filter-to-needs. 9 unit tests in tests/unit/deck-insights.test.ts.

- **put_action_on_stack builders read effect amounts from the PAYLOAD, not the card script.** A `deal_damage_creature` cast via `putOnStack('deal_damage_creature', {target_card_id, amount, target_controller}, source)` MUST include `amount` â€” the builder calls `resolve_effect_amount(payload->>'amount', x_value)` and raises "amount must be positive" if it's missing (the card-script `amount:3` is the CLIENT's job to copy into the payload via getSpellPlan, the SQL never reads it). Tripped a protection test that omitted amount â†’ the builder raised before the protection check was reached.

- **RLS leak: two legacy `USING(true)` SELECT policies (mig 143).** game_cards `"Zichtbaar voor sessie-deelnemers"` + game_players `"Sessie deelnemers kunnen stats zien"` granted SELECT to ALL roles (anon + non-members) globally â€” Postgres OR-combines permissive policies, so they overrode the intended is_session_player gates. Fix: drop them; game_cards already had a member-scoped policy, game_players got one added. **The judge view + opponent-count display read ALL members' cards/mana via the normal client (no privileged judge role) â€” they work because the readers are session MEMBERS**, so member-scoping is safe but hiding hidden zones BETWEEN members (Slice B) would break the judge + counts (deferred; needs a privileged-judge concept + count RPC). game_sessions `USING(true)` is the deliberate join-by-unguessable-ID flow â€” left intact. `cleanup_finished_session(id)` (mig 144) deletes runtime rows for a finished session, keeps game_sessions + game_session_players. Both tested under the `authenticated` role via asPlayer (postgres bypasses RLS, so RLS tests MUST run as authenticated). [[project-roadmap]]

- **set_pt was engine-complete (mig 129) but had ZERO client wiring** until 2026-06-06 â€” the controller couldn't cast "becomes X/Y" (Frogify). Wiring a new targeted-creature spell kind touches ~8 spots in ControllerListV4 (SpellPlan union, getSpellPlan branch, canCast list, spellTargetController, requiresCreatureTarget, needsTarget, a picker JSX block, the on*Creature prop + handler) + a put*OnStack wrapper in actions.ts â€” all mirroring the `pump` path. **Engine-ahead-of-client drift is a recurring debt**: also unwired is any generic/hybrid-mana payment picker (every cast passes generic=null; the player floats specific mana via tapForMana, so auto-distribution is only suboptimal, never broken â€” picker is optimization, not an unblock).

- **Commander deck legality is a CLIENT verdict (no migration, no color_identity column).** `commanderDeckLegality(lines, commander)` in lib/game/deck-insights.ts combines exactly-100 (incl. commander, which is counted in `lines`) + singleton (deckSingletonViolations) + colour identity (deckColorIdentityViolations) into `{legal, cardCount, issues[]}`. DeckInsights renders a green/red verdict banner gated on `commanderCard` (a deck is only judged as Commander when it has a designated commander). Colour identity is DERIVED from mana_cost+oracle `{X}` symbols (approximate â€” builder guide, not a rules oracle). Tests in tests/unit/deck-insights.test.ts (14 total). **Now ALSO enforced server-side (mig 141):** `commander_deck_legality(deck_id) -> jsonb{legal,card_count,issues}` (PL/pgSQL mirror) + `card_color_identity(card_id)` (reuses card_color_set on mana_cost + the `{...}` symbols extracted from oracle_text via regexp_matches â€” NOT raw-text scan, else word letters pollute it). `spawn_deck_for_session` gained `p_enforce_legality boolean default true` and raises on an illegal Commander deck; the OLD 2-arg signature was DROPPED so only the enforcing one remains â€” the client (actions.ts) calls with 2 named args and the default makes production enforce with no client change; the TEST HARNESS spawnDeck passes `p_enforce_legality => false` (its fixtures are minimal). - **Multiplayer turn/priority were N-player-ready but did NOT skip ELIMINATED players (mig 140).** `advance_step` (active-player rotation) and `pass_priority` (priority rotation) both rotate by `seat_number` with a wrap-to-lowest, and `maybe_finish_game_session` already implements last-player-standing (alive = `life_total > 0`; alive==1 â†’ winner, ==0 â†’ draw) and is wired into combat damage (mig 127/132), spell resolution (`finalize_stack_resolution` mig 087) and `adjust_player_life` (baseline). The ONE gap: neither rotation filtered on `life_total > 0`, so in 3-4p Commander (where the game CONTINUES after a death) a dead seat still got priority (stalled the round) and became active player (untap/draw for a corpse). 2p hid this (game ends instantly at one death). Fix = add `life_total > 0` to the player COUNT that sets the all-passed threshold in pass_priority AND to all four seat-lookup subqueries (next-higher + wrap, in both fns). Reproduced pass_priority from mig 095, advance_step from baseline (no migration had redefined it â€” the valid baseline-fallback case per the Do-Not-Repeat). Note: `apply_damage_to_player` (mig 125) itself does NOT call maybe_finish â€” it relies on its caller (combat resolver / finalize_stack); `adjust_player_life` DOES. game_sessions.status âˆˆ {open,locked,finished} (no 'in_progress'). Tests MP1-MP5 in tests/feature/multiplayer.test.ts; harness now supports seat D / `numPlayers:4` + `advanceStep`/`adjustLife`/`eliminate`/`activePlayer`/`sessionResult` verbs.

- **(2026-06-27) Cast-planner sweep for the two new decks (Edgar Markov + Deadpool).** Audited every new cast-from-hand spell through `getSpellPlan` (the `_audit.mts` pattern: import getSpellPlan, feed `{zone:'hand', copied_script:null, cards:{script, type_line}}`, flag `kind:'normal'` when the script has spell_effect actions). Result: **FIXED** — `saw_in_half` (Saw in Half) + `grant_dies_effect` (Feign Death / Not Dead After All / Supernatural Stamina) were `kind:'normal'` (uncastable); added both to `TARGETED_SPELL_EFFECT_TYPES` so they cast as `targeted_spell_effect` (creature picker → `castSpellEffect(targetCardId)` → program resolver `apply_trigger_effects` → `apply_creature_effect`, the SAME proven path as `exile_and_manifest`). **The two deeper gaps were then FIXED (2026-06-27, mig 362):** (1) **Dark Ritual** (`add_mana`) was PURELY a client gap — my "not dispatched by the program resolver" claim was WRONG: `apply_trigger_effects`' final `else` delegates UNTARGETED effects to `apply_targeted_triggered_ability_effects` → `apply_triggered_ability_effects`, which DOES handle `add_mana` (adds to the caster's pool). Fix = add `add_mana` to `UNTARGETED_SPELL_ACTION_TYPES` (→ kind:spell_effect). LESSON: the program resolver `apply_trigger_effects` only branches DECISION/program types inline; simple untargeted effects (add_mana, gain_life, draw…) fall through to the delegate — don't conclude "unsupported" from grepping `apply_trigger_effects` alone. (2) **Harmless Offering** (`gain_control` permanent, `to:opponent`) — the ENGINE donate ALREADY existed (`apply_creature_effect.gain_control` honors `to:opponent`, **mig 353**; it picks the lowest-seat opponent of the `acting_controller`=caster), but the CAST path was unwired. Fix = `build_stack_payload_permanent_simple` accepts `kind=gain_control` + threads `to`; `handle_permanent_effect` injects `acting_controller`=caster (do NOT compute the opponent yourself — the gain_control branch does, off the caster; passing the opponent as acting_controller donates to the opponent's opponent). Front-end reuses the `permanent_effect` picker: getSpellPlan routes `gain_control` `to:opponent` → `permanent_effect` {effectKind:'gain_control', donate:true, targetController:'you'}; `castPermanentEffect` threads `to`. The permanent_effect picker already filters to YOUR permanents via targetController, so NO new plan kind/picker was needed. Tests DR1/HO1/HO2 (tests/feature/donate-and-mana-spell.test.ts), full suite 1812 pass.

- **(2026-06-27) Reusable "choose an opponent, then hand them a permanent" hook (mig 363).** The first donate cut picked the recipient deterministically (lowest-seat opponent) — an approximation in multiplayer. Replaced with a real choice built on the EXISTING `choose_player` decision infra (no new front-end: the controller already renders `choose_player` via `ChoosePlayerBody`, ControllerListV5:2482). Pattern: `handle_permanent_effect`, for kind=gain_control `to:opponent`, counts LIVING opponents — **1 opponent (1v1) → apply directly, no prompt**; **>1 → park a `choose_player` decision** (options = living opponents) whose `params.apply_permanent_effect` carries the permanent_effect payload (with `to` stripped). `submit_decision`'s choose_player branch: when `params ? 'apply_permanent_effect'`, runs `apply_creature_effect(kind, target_card_id, payload || {acting_controller: chosen})` then `resume_or_finalize`. Generalizes to any future "target opponent gains/receives this permanent" cast — park a choose_player with `apply_permanent_effect`. NOTE `resume_or_finalize` only FINALIZES a `permanent_effect` item (it re-runs the program only for triggered_ability/spell_effect), so `then`/search/graveyard riders AFTER the apply in handle_permanent_effect are SKIPPED on the deferred (choose_player) path — fine for gain_control donate (no riders), but a donate-with-riders card would need the riders moved into the resume. [[bug-1487]] Verified OK (already castable): Reanimate/Animate Dead (return_from_graveyard → spell_effect program via DECISION path), Olivia's Wrath/Languish (pump_all → spell_effect), Vandalblast/Bedevil (destroy permanent → permanent_effect), Abrade (modal), Blasphemous Edict (sacrifice → spell_effect), Deadly Rollick/Terminate/Crib Swap/New Blood (exile/destroy creature → creature_effect). [[bug-1486]] [[bug-1487]]

## Do-Not-Repeat

- 2026-07-13 — **Before regenerating a migration with new-migration.mjs, DIFF functions_src against the LATEST migration definition of every function you include.** Migrations sometimes redefine functions directly (mig 388 did cast_spell_effect) leaving functions_src stale; regenerating from the stale source silently REVERTS those changes (bug-1280 — adventure cost + cast-face watchers reverted by the first cut of mig 392, caught by the suite). Extract-and-compare per function; backfill functions_src first.

- 2026-07-12 — (b) Dual-type-line strikes THREE times now (bug-1019/1508/1512): grep for EVERY `type_line` string-includes check when touching cast logic — doesCardRequireStackTarget was missed twice. (c) Gating-probe fixtures MUST mirror the full real catalog row (oracle_text included) — a fixture without oracle_text green-lit broken gating.

- 2026-07-12 — Dual type_lines ('Creature — X // Instant — Adventure') have now caused the SAME bug class twice: server (bug-1019, mig 373) and client (bug-1508). Any `type_line.includes('instant'/'sorcery'/...)` check MUST split the front face first: `type_line.split(' // ')[0]`. Also: every cast path needs autoPay — castAdventure shipped without it and silently only worked with floating mana.

- 2026-07-11 — normalize* functions in lib/game/data.ts are field allowlists: adding a column to a SELECT without adding it to the matching normalizer silently drops it client-side (bug-1506, tv_code). Also: don't declare a data path healthy from DB/REST checks alone — walk the mapping layer to the component before concluding 'it's just UX'.
- (2026-06-27) **The app is LANDSCAPE-ONLY (cerebrum User-Pref line 11) — never key responsive layout off `max-height`/portrait-vs-landscape; key off WIDTH.** When making the controller opponent-row (`OpponentRowOverlay` in ControllerListV5) lay out as a grid, I first copied StackRail's `[@media(max-height:640px)]` pattern with `grid-cols-1` as default. WRONG: StackRail's height-gate is about *compacting for short screens*, a different concern; a height-gate gives a wide landscape tablet/TV (height >640px) only 1 column. Correct = width-scaled (`grid-cols-2 lg:grid-cols-3`, with a `grid-cols-1` guard for a 1-opponent heads-up game so the lone card isn't half-width). ROOT CAUSE: I generated the layout change BEFORE reading cerebrum's User Preferences (OpenWolf rule: check cerebrum first) — cerebrum is 336KB so I'd deferred it; grep the specific section (`## User Preferences`) instead of skipping. [[app-is-landscape-only]]
- (2026-06-26) **The `scions-spellcraft-build` workflow's embedded cheat-sheet vocabulary DIVERGES from the real Zod schema (lib/game/card-behavior-schema.ts) — its scripts can pass `validateCardScript` yet be semantically BROKEN because action/filter objects are non-strict (`z.object`, not `.strict()`), so wrong field names are SILENTLY STRIPPED.** Confirmed wrong-vs-schema: mana cost `amount` must be a STRING (`"{2}{B}"`), not a number or a `mana:` key; `add_counters[_all]` uses `counter_type:"plus_one_one"` (enum) not `counter:"+1/+1"`, and `add_counters_all` filters via flat `type_line`+`target_controller`, NOT a `filter:{}` wrapper; triggered abilities use `effects:[]` not `actions:[]`; `deal_damage`/`lose_life` self-damage uses `recipient:"controller"` not `target:`; trigger `filter` supports `nontoken`/`min_power` but NOT `token`/`max_power`; `enters_tapped.unless` count form is `{count:"basic_lands_you_control", at_least:N}`; `pump_all` power/toughness can't be NEGATED dynamically (CountAmountSchema has no `negate`), so "-X/-X" board-pumps (Olivia's Wrath) are needs_engine; `grant_keyword`/`tap` have no self-target from an activated ability. ALWAYS, after running the workflow: (1) `validateCardScript` every script, AND (2) deep-DIFF input vs `CardBehaviorScriptV2Schema.safeParse(...).data` to catch silently-stripped fields — validation alone is insufficient. This batch: 12/54 needed correction, 4 downgraded to needs_engine. [[bug-1484]]
- (2026-06-25) **Do NOT add per-player "manual table actions" to the controller** (free-hand life ±, counters ±, make-token, sacrifice buttons). The user explicitly rejected this: the **complete rules engine** is how state changes happen; letting every player mutate state by hand undermines the automation/trust model. Such state-mutation RPCs are JUDGE correction tools only. When an analysis lists "manual life adjust / token UI / sacrifice" as a missing capability, it is INTENTIONALLY absent — do not "fix" it. (I built it for ~14k tokens and had to revert it all.) [[the rules engine performs state changes]]
- (2026-06-18) **A spell can be ENGINE-supported but UNCASTABLE because the client cast planner `getSpellPlan` (components/controller/shared.ts) has no case for its action type** — it then falls through to `kind:'normal'` (vanilla, no target) and does nothing for a targeted instant. Reality Shift's `exile_and_manifest` was supported server-side (cast_spell_effect + creature target, mig 251) but unlisted client-side. When adding/triaging a card, check BOTH: (1) engine resolves the action, AND (2) getSpellPlan classifies it (CREATURE_EFFECT_MAP for stack creature-actions; UNTARGETED_SPELL_ACTION_TYPES for untargeted programs; TARGETED_SPELL_EFFECT_TYPES → the `targeted_spell_effect` kind for creature-targeted programs that resolve via cast_spell_effect). [[bug-reality-shift-uncastable]]
- (2026-06-18) **An ATTACKING CPU bot must call `resolve_combat_damage` itself.** `advance_step` does NOT auto-resolve combat damage (bug-601) and only the active/priority player may resolve it. The bot holds priority during its own `combat_damage` step, so `scripts/bot-runner.mjs` `tick()` now has a `myTurn && step==='combat_damage'` branch (helper loops the first-strike→regular two-pass flow) before `pass_priority`. Without it, a bot's attack dealt zero damage and nothing died. The ENGINE was fine (5/4 vs 4/4 both die when resolve runs) — the gap was the bot driver. Restart `--watch` after editing the runner. [[bug-bot-no-combat-damage]]
- (2026-06-18) **`MotionCard` renders its image with next/image `fill` (absolutely positioned) — it needs a parent with a real WIDTH.** `MotionCard className="w-full"` only works if the chain of ancestors has a resolved width. A wrapper div that is a flex item inside `flex-col items-center` gets `width:auto` (shrink-to-fit) → `w-full` resolves to 0 → image invisible (name-fallback only). This bit declare-attackers (extra rotate-90 wrapper div); the main board/blockers worked because MotionCard was a direct child of a width-sized button. Fix: put `w-full` (or a fixed width) on the wrapper too. [[bug-attacker-images-zero-width]]
- (2026-06-18) **A card in the controller is a `<button>`/`<motion.button>`, so an on-card affordance (zoom ⤢, board-preview 👁) must be a `<span role="button" tabIndex={0}>`, NOT a nested `<button>`** (nested native buttons are invalid HTML → React hydration warning). Always `stopPropagation` on its onPointerDown + onClick so it doesn't trigger the card's tap/drag (attack/block toggle, drag-to-attack). Reusable `ZoomBadge` + module-level `boardCardToZoomCard`/`stackItemToZoomCard` adapters feed the (portaled) `CardZoomOverlay`. [[feat-combat-zoom-preview]]
- (2026-06-18) **The TEST harness DB is `leyline_test`, NOT `postgres`.** `npm run test:db:setup` (scripts/setup-local-test-db.mjs) rebuilds `127.0.0.1:54322/**leyline_test**`; tests run there. The `postgres` DB on :54322 is the separate PLAY DB the app uses. When verifying that a migration landed, connect to `leyline_test` — I wasted time thinking mig 322 "didn't apply" because I queried `postgres`. (Also: adding RETURNS TABLE columns to a SQL function needs `drop function if exists` first — same return-type rule as the param-overload gotcha below.)
- (2026-06-18) **A `position:fixed`/`absolute` overlay rendered inside a framer-motion element that animates `x`/`y`/`scale` opens in the WRONG place** — the `transform` makes that ancestor the containing block, so `inset-0`+`items-center` centres on the animated box, not the viewport. Symptom: the Your-zones card zoom (CardZoomOverlay inside MyZonesSheet's `y`-animated bottom sheet) opened below the fold. Fix: render via `createPortal(node, document.body)` and use `fixed inset-0`. [[bug-zones-zoom-offscreen]]
- (2026-06-18) **Adding a param to an existing SQL function = `create or replace` makes a NEW overload, not a replace.** `pay_mana_cost` went 6→7 args; the generated migration must `drop function if exists public.pay_mana_cost(<OLD 6-arg signature>)` BEFORE the create, else both overloads coexist and 4-arg `perform` calls become ambiguous / hit the stale one. Hand-add the DROP at the top of the migration (new-migration.mjs only emits the create). Same pattern bit `add_mana_from_card` (6→7) and `add_bot_to_session` (1→2).
- (2026-06-18) **Harness `Scenario.payMana(seat, cost, opts)` and `setMana(seat, …)` take the SEAT as the first POSITIONAL arg** — they do NOT read `this.acting`. `s.as('A').payMana('{R}', {...})` silently passes seat=`'{R}'` → `players['{R}']` undefined → `auth.uid()` null → "Authentication required". Use `s.payMana('A', '{R}', {...})`. (Inconsistent with `activateMana`/`castPermanent`, which DO use `as()`/`this.acting`.)
- (2026-06-12) When seeding a NEW canonical functions_src file from a past migration, search ALL of supabase/migrations for the newest definition first — an archived version may be a dropped overload (add_mana_from_card: archive had 6-arg, mig 151 replaced it with 7-arg; re-emitting the stale one created a duplicate-overload 42725 error).

- [2026-06-11] **deck:upsert flags do not survive npm:** `npm run deck:upsert -- --apply --force` still runs a DRY RUN (npm consumes the flags; it even warns about --force). Call the script directly: `node --import tsx scripts/upsert-deck-scripts.mjs --apply [--force]`. Also: the token-dep scan only reads DECK-card scripts, so a token referenced from another TOKEN's script (Dragon Egg -> Dragon Hatchling) must be created on hosted manually.

- [2026-06-11] **PS 5.1 + git commit -m here-strings: no embedded double-quoted phrases.** A "quoted phrase with spaces" inside the message gets split by native arg passing (git sees pathspecs; commit fails). Reword to avoid inner double quotes, or commit via the Bash tool.

- **Windows Python file writes MUST pass encoding='utf-8'** (bug: mig 202 / SQLSTATE 22021 at db push). `open(path, 'w')` on Windows defaults to cp1252 â€” em-dashes become 0x97, invalid UTF-8. Node tools (writeFileSync, the Edit tool) are safe; Python heredocs are the hazard. The local setup script now STRICT-decodes every SQL file before applying (fatal TextDecoder) so an encoding regression fails at `npm run test:db:setup` with the filename, not at hosted `db push`.

<!-- Mistakes made and corrected. Each entry prevents the same mistake recurring. -->
<!-- Format: [YYYY-MM-DD] Description of what went wrong and what to do instead. -->

- [2026-06-08] **The Scryfall importer silently skipped EVERY planeswalker** (bug-447): `isExtraCardObject` used `typeLine.includes('plane')` to drop Planechase "Plane â€”" cards, but "plane" is a substring of "**plane**swalker" â†’ all planeswalkers dropped. Fix: word-boundary `/\bplane\b/.test(typeLine)`. **Lesson: type-line substring filters are landmines â€” `includes('plane')` âŠƒ planeswalker, and similar collisions lurk. Use word boundaries / exact type checks.** Also: when a card is "missing from the catalog", don't assume "the import wasn't run" â€” check whether a FILTER is dropping it (I wrongly told the user the import never ran; it ran but skipped PWs).

- [2026-06-05] **When reproducing a SQL function to add one line, copy the CURRENT definition â€” NOT `supabase/local-bootstrap/00_baseline.sql`.** The baseline is a stale snapshot; many functions are `create or replace`d by later migrations. mig 123 copied `resolve_top_of_stack` + `enqueue_triggered_ability` from the baseline and reverted them past mig 104 (registry dispatcher) and mig 114/116 (multi-target reach) â†’ "Unsupported stack action type: spell_effect" + broken multi-target triggers (bug-281). **Always `grep supabase/migrations/ for "function public.<name>"` FIRST and reproduce from the highest-numbered migration that defines it** (only fall back to the baseline if no migration redefines it). **This ALSO applies to CHECK constraints** (bug-283): when rebuilding a CHECK (e.g. game_continuous_effects_effect_type_check, game_stack_items action_type), grep the migrations for prior `add constraint` of the same name and include every value later migrations added (e.g. 'control' from mig 106) â€” the baseline constraint list is stale.

- [2026-06-07] **card-behavior-registry variant resolution: an OPTIONAL field shared by all variants of a type must not gate matching.** `resolveEffectDef` matches a variant when all its field keys are present on the effect. Adding `counter_type` (optional, omitted-by-default via `materializeDefault:false`) to BOTH `add_counters` shapes (base + add_counters_target) made the matcher require `counter_type` present â†’ the targeted variant stopped resolving (target field dropped on round-trip), and a naive "skip all optional fields" fix then broke `deal_damage` (whose `recipient` legitimately discriminates base-vs-target). Correct rule (now in `nonDiscriminatingKeys`): a key can only discriminate if it is NOT present on every variant of the type; exclude keys common to ALL variants from the required-match set. So `counter_type` (on both add_counters defs) is excluded, but `recipient` (only on base deal_damage) still discriminates. When adding a field to one variant, ask whether it's shared across all variants of that type.

- [2026-05-27] **MTG combat â€” multiple blockers damage order:** When multiple creatures block a single attacker, it is the **ATTACKER** (not the defender) who assigns damage order among blockers. The defender's declare blockers phase only determines *which* creatures block *which* attacker. Do not show a "stel schade-volgorde in" or damage-ordering UI element on the defender's declare blockers screen.

- [2026-06-02] **Test harness: an expected RPC rejection aborts the whole test transaction.** Each harness test runs in one `withRolledBackTx`. A failing RPC (e.g. asserting `resolve_top_of_stack` raises) puts that tx into `25P02` (aborted), so ANY statement after the `assert.rejects` fails too. Keep an expected-rejection as the LAST action in a test, or split the guard assertion into its own test (what MD1 needed). A future `expectReject` helper using SAVEPOINT/ROLLBACK TO would let a test continue after an expected failure. (Also: `asPlayer`'s cleanup is already try/catch-wrapped so it doesn't mask the real error with 25P02.)

- [2026-06-04] **getSpellPlan branch ORDER matters â€” put multi-action/decision spells before single-action cases.** A scry+draw spell (Opt) silently only drew: `getSpellPlan` checked the single `draw` action before the `spell_effect` (scry/surveil/multi-action) case, so `actions.find(type==='draw')` matched first and dropped the scry â†’ a `draw_cards` stack item, no decision. The engine/DB were 100% correct (a parked decision proved it); the bug was pure client classification. Fix: the `spell_effect` detection must come BEFORE the `draw` (and any other single-action) return. When adding a new spell kind, place broader/multi-action matchers ahead of narrow single-action ones. Also: when an in-game feature "does nothing," check whether the live CLIENT build is current AND whether the client is even producing the right stack `action_type` (query game_stack_items) before suspecting the SQL â€” the DB had everything right here. [[bug-155]]

- [2026-06-04] **A pending decision must freeze priority â€” a parked stack item is NOT 'pending'.** When scry/surveil/modal parks, the stack item goes status='awaiting_decision'. `pass_priority` counts only `status='pending'` items, so after a park it saw an empty stack and called `advance_step` â†’ the round advanced with the decision still open, and players kept passing. Fix (migration 095): `pass_priority` raises if any `game_pending_decisions` row is pending for the session (guard at the top). Client mirrors it: `passBlockReason` ('Resolve your decision' for the decider / 'Waiting for a decision' for others / 'Choose trigger target') disables the Pass button. `submit_decision`â†’`finalize_stack_resolution` resets priority (active player, pass_count 0) so the cycle restarts cleanly. submit_decision does NOT depend on priority (only deciding_player = auth.uid()), so the decider can submit even while priority shows the opponent. Regression: SC6. [[bug-156]]

- **More shared-decision choice types: tutor / discard / may (migration 096).** The pending-decision system is the generic seam â€” adding a choice = (1) a park branch in `apply_trigger_effects` that builds `options` + inserts a `game_pending_decisions` row with a new `decision_type`, (2) a `submit_decision` branch that validates + applies + resumes, (3) a `<PendingDecisionPrompt>` body. 096 added: **`game_pending_decisions.params jsonb`** (per-decision config, e.g. tutor destination), **`resume_or_finalize(session, item)`** helper (the shared "continue the program from resume_index, or finalize" tail â€” now used by scry/surveil/search/discard/confirm; standalone scry/surveil items finalize since their action_type isn't triggered_ability/spell_effect). New effect types (work in triggers AND spell_effect programs via apply_trigger_effects): **`search_library`** (tutor: options=library cards filtered by `filter.type_line` ilike; pick 0..count; `submit`â†’move to `to` hand/battlefield/top + **shuffle** + rebuild; decision_type `search_library`), **`discard`** (options=controller hand; min=max=least(count,handSize); decision_type `choose_cards`, params.to=graveyard), **`may`** (decision_type `confirm`, options=[], min/max 0, params.effects=inner; `submit {confirmed}` â†’ on true run inner via apply_targeted_triggered_ability_effects â€” **inner must be simple, no nested decision in v1**). Client: `CardPickBody` (multi-select up to max, for search_library+choose_cards, submits `{chosen:[ids]}`) and `ConfirmBody` (Yes/No â†’ `{confirmed}`). getSpellPlan: added them to `UNTARGETED_SPELL_ACTION_TYPES` + a `DECISION_SPELL_ACTION_TYPES` list; routing now = `allUntargeted && (hasDecisionEffect || length>1)`. Schema: added to KNOWN_V2_ACTION_TYPES + explicit union members (may.effects kept loose `z.array(z.record)` to dodge self-referential zod typing). LLM guide updated. Authored via JSON/AI (not the guided form). Tests TUT1/TUT2/DIS1/MAY1/MAY2 (51/51). **choose_player is the remaining 4th choice the user wanted â€” deferred** because it threads a chosen player into DOWNSTREAM effects, which needs `apply_triggered_ability_effects` to honor a specific recipient player id (a baseline-function change), unlike these three which are self-contained.
- **choose_player (migration 097) â€” done; the 4th choice.** Pick a player at resolution, then apply inner (player-directed) effects to them. **Key trick that avoided touching the baseline applier:** instead of adding a recipient-by-id param, `submit_decision` runs the inner effects with the CHOSEN player as the `p_controller_id` context and `recipient` forced to `'controller'` on each effect â€” so lose_life/deal_damage/gain_life/draw/mill all land on the chosen player via the unchanged `apply_triggered_ability_effects`. Effect spec: `{type:'choose_player', filter?:'opponent'|'any', effects:[...]}`. apply_trigger_effects parks decision_type `choose_player` with options = players (filtered; `left join profiles` for username, null in harness), min/max 1, params.effects=inner. submit validates the player is offered, then rewrites inner effects with `recipient:'controller'` and calls `apply_triggered_ability_effects(session, chosenPlayer, source, rewritten)` â†’ resume_or_finalize. Inner effects must be simple player-directed (no nested decision). Client `ChoosePlayerBody` (player buttons, username ?? 'Player'). Schema member + KNOWN_V2 + LLM + getSpellPlan lists updated. Tests CP1 (chosen opponent loses 3), CP2 (non-offered player rejected). **All four user-requested choices now live: tutor, discard, may, choose_player (53/53).**

## Decision Log

- 2026-07-11 — Tutorial mode: chose just-in-time hints (FirstTimeHints on layoutState) + a 'Practice vs CPU' lobby shortcut over a scripted tutorial. Rationale: scripted tutorials are expensive and break with engine changes; bot infra + stat-exclusion for bot games already existed, so practice mode was mostly packaging. Revisit scripted onboarding only if these prove insufficient for non-Magic players.

<!-- Significant technical decisions with rationale. Why X was chosen over Y. -->

- [2026-06-08] **Liliana âˆ’2 = loyalty targeting (already worked!) + a dynamic/negatable pump (mig 172).** Big surprise: **loyalty-ability TARGETING needed almost nothing** â€” activate_loyalty_ability already enqueues via enqueue_triggered_ability, which detects a creature-target requirement and the player then picks the target via choose_triggered_ability_creature_target (topStackItem â†’ chooseTriggerTarget â†’ resolveStack), the SAME flow as a targeted ETB trigger. The ONLY blocker was that **`pump` wasn't in `trigger_effect_target_type`'s creature-targetable list** (mig 130) â€” it had deal_damage/destroy/â€¦/set_pt but not pump â€” so a targeted pump was treated as untargeted and dropped. Added `pump` there. Then the **dynamic âˆ’X/âˆ’X**: apply_creature_effect's pump branch (reproduced from 162) now resolves `power`/`toughness` via resolve_dynamic_amount (so each can be a `{count,â€¦}` object) and **negates per a `"negate":true` on THAT value object** (Liliana: power & toughness each `{count:creatures_you_control, type_line:Zombie, negate:true}`); fixed numbers (incl. negative literals) still flow through resolve_dynamic_amount unchanged. A debuff to â‰¤0 toughness runs move_lethal. Schema: pump power/toughness became `number | PumpValueSchema`. **Liliana now: +1 âœ… (mig 171), âˆ’2 âœ… (mig 172, tests LIL3-4), âˆ’3 âŒ (cast-from-graveyard, stub).** 524/524. On `creature-damage-shields`.

- [2026-06-08] **Card catalog vs behavior script are TWO layers â€” the importer only does the first.** A user reported "Liliana isn't in the card database / deckbuilder selector". Root cause split: (1) the Scryfall importer (import-scryfall-cards.mjs) maps DATA ONLY â€” name/mana_cost/type_line/oracle_text/power_toughness/keywords/image_url â€” and **never sets `cards.script`**; oracle_text is English prose, not executable. (2) The deck text-importer (import_deck_from_text, mig 139) matches `lower(cards.name)` exactly, so a card with no `cards` row shows as "missing" in the deckbuilder. So "not in the selector" = no catalog row (run `npm run import:cards`), and "abilities don't work" = no authored `script` (separate: AI route /api/cards/generate-behavior or the editor). **When asked to 'implement a card', distinguish: MISSING from the catalog (import) vs lacking a SCRIPT (author it).** Don't run `npm run import:cards` unprompted â€” it upserts ~tens-of-thousands of rows to the real Supabase.

- [2026-06-08] **Conditional mill (mig 171, for Liliana +1 + graveyard-matters): `if_milled_type` + `then` on the mill effect.** "Mill N, if a <type> was milled, <then>". The mill branch of apply_triggered_ability_effects (reproduced from 163) tracks whether any milled card's type_line matched (checked BEFORE the card moves) and, once, recursively applies the `then` effects via apply_triggered_ability_effects (source as controller). **Liliana, Untouched by Death's REAL M19 abilities (I'd misremembered them as static/attack-trigger): +1 conditional mill (now âœ…), âˆ’2 target âˆ’X/âˆ’X where X=Zombies you control (needs loyalty-ability TARGETING â€” doesn't exist â€” + a dynamic negative pump), âˆ’3 cast Zombie spells from graveyard (the deferred cast-from-graveyard frontier).** Authored her with +1 working and âˆ’2/âˆ’3 as labelled no-op stubs (`unsupported_*` types pass the schema's UnknownV2Action passthrough and are ignored by the applier). Tests LIL1-2. 522/522.

- [2026-06-08] **Choose-a-creature-type (Tribal #6, mig 170): a new decision type that MIRRORS choose_player, with the chosen value INJECTED into count amounts.** apply_trigger_effects (reproduced from 163) parks a `choose_creature_type` decision (a curated fixed type list in options) carrying params.effects â€” same park/resume pattern as choose_player. submit_decision (reproduced from 154) validates the pick then rewrites the sub-effects, **`jsonb_set(e, '{amount,type_line}', chosen)` for any effect whose amount is a `{count:â€¦}` object**, and applies them via apply_triggered_ability_effects with the deciding player as controller. So Distant Melody authors `{count: creatures_you_control}` WITHOUT a type_line and the choice fills it in. Schema: choose_creature_type added to the action union + KNOWN_V2_ACTION_TYPES. **GAP surfaced (pre-existing, NOT this feature): the draw branch floors at `greatest(1, amount)`, so a dynamic/count draw of 0 draws 1** â€” "draw for each X" with X=0 draws 1; a 1-line fix needs an apply_triggered_ability_effects reproduction, deferred to its own migration (tested CCT2 with a non-zero count to avoid the edge). Client decision UI deferred. Tests CCT1-2. 520/520. On `creature-damage-shields`.

- [2026-06-08] **Planeswalker client UI (Tribal #4 slice 3): a CLIENT slice â€” surface loyalty in the V4 controller, no new server work.** actions.ts gained `activateLoyaltyAbility`; `declareAttacker` took a `string|null` defending player + optional planeswalker id (matching mig 169's 4-arg RPC). **Key gotcha: normalizeCardBehaviorToV2 returns a FIXED shape that DROPS unknown fields** â€” loyalty/loyalty_abilities were stripped before reaching the UI, so I added them to the `CardBehaviorScriptV2` TS type AND to normalizeV2Script's return (the schema/Zod alone isn't enough; the client reads the normalized object). ControllerListV4: CardActionSheet renders a Loyalty section (`â—† N` header from card.counters.loyalty + a `+N/âˆ’N` button per ability, gated on canCastSorceries + `loyalty+costâ‰¥0`, server enforces once-per-turn); `hasActions` extended so a PW with only loyalty abilities still opens the sheet. DeclareAttackersLayout reworked from a single implicit defender to an **attack-target picker** (opponent players + their planeswalkers, computed from boardCards where type_line~planeswalker; assignments became a `Set<cardId>` + a selected target). **Counter chips: label `loyalty`â†’â—† and HIDE the internal `loyalty_turn` once-per-turn marker** (HIDDEN_COUNTER_KEYS) so it doesn't render as a bogus counter. - [2026-06-08] **Other-scoped trigger events (roadmap Tribal #1 second half, mig 165): a BROADCAST alongside the self-fire, with new event names.** fire_card_triggers fires a card's OWN triggers only. (2) **the scan set = battlefield âˆª the changed card itself**, because a dying creature must be able to watch its OWN death (leaves-the-battlefield / last-known-info â€” Midnight Reaper triggers when it dies; at AFTER-trigger time it's already in the graveyard, so a plain `zone='battlefield'` scan would miss it). exclude_self=false includes self-death; =true is "another". - [2026-06-07] **Beast Within â€” "its controller creates a token" + multi-action targeted spells (mig 163).** Two reusable pieces, not Beast-specific. (1) **Multi-action targeted spell programs had no way to carry a target**: cast_spell_effect stored the program but no target, yet apply_trigger_effects reads `payload->>'target_card_id'`. Added `p_target_card_id` to cast_spell_effect (DROP the 4-arg first â€” bug-421 lesson, no repeat) â†’ stored on the spell_effect stack item. The harness/actions castSpellEffect gained a 4th targetCardId arg. This is the general fix for "destroy target permanent + <rider>" spells. (2) **create_token recipient = the destroyed permanent's controller, captured BEFORE destroy.** The token's controller must be read while the permanent is still on the battlefield â€” once destroyed it's in the graveyard and the controller is lost. So apply_trigger_effects captures `v_target`'s live controller ONCE before its effect loop, and injects it as `recipient_player_id` into any create_token with `recipient:"target_controller"`; apply_triggered_ability_effects then makes that player the token's owner AND controller (was hardcoded p_controller_id). **Why capture in apply_trigger_effects, not the dispatcher?** The two effects (destroy, create_token) are separate loop iterations / separate apply_targeted_triggered_ability_effects calls â€” by the time create_token runs, destroy already happened, so only a pre-loop capture sees the live controller. **Tokens weren't seeded in the test DB at all** (create_token filters is_token=true; the fixture had none and create_token was untested) â€” added `is_token` to the seed insert + a `Beast Token` (3/3) fixture. Schema: create_token gained `recipient:"target_controller"`. Tests BW1-3 (opponent's permanent â†’ opponent's Beast; own â†’ yours). 494/494, tsc/lint/build clean. On `creature-damage-shields`.

- [2026-06-07] **Counter doubling (Doubling Season) keys off the RECIPIENT's controller, so it needs ZERO acting-controller plumbing (mig 158, roadmap Counters #5 half 1).** The CR rule is "if an effect would put counters on a permanent YOU control, it puts twice that many" â€” the relevant player is the controller of the permanent RECEIVING the counters, not the effect's controller. Every placement site already knows the recipient, so no threading through build_stack_payload/handle_creature_effect (which was the blocker that would have made this a big feature). New helper `counter_factor(session, controller)` = `(2 ^ least(8, count(*)))::int` over battlefield permanents that player controls whose `effective_script(session,id)->>'doubles_counters'` is true (no doublers â†’ count 0 â†’ Ã—1; two Doubling Seasons â†’ Ã—4, multiplicative as the rules say). Each of the 4 placement sites multiplies only POSITIVE amounts by the factor: apply_creature_effect add_counters (target's controller), apply_triggered_ability_effects add_counters (source's controller) + add_counters_all (per-row `gc.controller_player_id`, so a mass effect doubles per RECIPIENT â€” DS5), apply_enters_with_counters (NEW.controller_player_id; NEW isn't in the table yet so counter_factor counts only the OTHER permanents â€” Hangarback enters with Ã—2). Removal/`all` and player counters (add_player_counters) deliberately untouched (players aren't permanents). **Deferred #5 half 2: dynamic "for each counter"/"X = number of counters" amount scaling (separate effect-amount feature, no overlap); also NOT doubled â€” Hardened Scales (additive +1) and proliferate's hardcoded +1.** Tests DS1-5. 474/474. On `creature-damage-shields`/`card-behaviours`.

- [2026-06-07] **âˆ’1/âˆ’1 counters = a BAG key `minus_one_one`, NOT a new column (mig 157, roadmap Counters #4 / Tier 2).** Storing âˆ’1/âˆ’1 in the existing `counters` jsonb bag means proliferate / counter-removal / judge-tools / display all handle it FOR FREE via the multi-counter infra â€” the only hot-path change is the layered P/T helpers subtract `coalesce((counters->>'minus_one_one')::int,0)` at the counter layer (reproduced card_layered_power/toughness from mig 149; the switch-aware public card_effective_* wrappers in 146 delegate to these, so untouched). - [2026-06-07] **"Enters with N counters" = a REPLACEMENT via a BEFORE INSERT/UPDATE-of-zone trigger, never an ETB add_counters trigger (mig 156, roadmap Counters #3).** A 0/0 that "enters with two +1/+1 counters" (Walking Ballista, Hangarback) would die to the 0-toughness SBA before any ETB trigger could resolve â€” so the counters MUST be present as the card enters. `apply_enters_with_counters()` BEFORE INSERT OR UPDATE OF zone on game_cards (same chokepoint pattern as redirect_commander_zone_change, mig 142): on entering the battlefield, read the effective script INLINE (`coalesce(NEW.copied_script,(select script from cards where id=NEW.card_id))` â€” effective_script() can't see the uncommitted NEW row) and, if `enters_with_counters {amount, counter_type?}` is present, set NEW.plus_one_counters (or NEW.counters bag) BEFORE the row lands. - [2026-06-07] **Counter REMOVAL = negative amount + `all` flag on the existing add_counters family, NOT a new effect type (mig 155, roadmap Counters #1).** Removing counters reuses the whole add_counters pipeline (source/target/mass/spell): a NEGATIVE `amount` subtracts (clamped at 0 via adjust_counter_bag / greatest), `all:true` clears a kind. Honors counter_type (plus_one_oneâ†’fast column, else bag). **Critical: removing +1/+1 lowers toughness â†’ can be lethal/0-toughness**, so every +1/+1 reduction re-runs `move_lethal_damaged_creatures_to_graveyard` (handles BOTH 704.5f 0-toughness and 704.5g lethal). - [2026-06-07] **Multi-counter model = ADDITIVE jsonb bag, never a rewrite of `plus_one_counters` (mig 153 proliferate, mig 154 Tier 1 + poison).** `plus_one_counters` (int) is on the P/T HOT PATH â€” folded into card_effective_power/toughness, layers (anthem/switch/cda), combat, lethal SBA. - [2026-06-07] **Assassin's Trophy â€” a targeted removal can PARK a decision for the AFFECTED player (mig 152).** "Destroy target permanent an opponent controls. Its controller may search their library for a basic land â†’ battlefield, then shuffle." The rider differs from the `then` self-riders (caster, simple effects): it's a DECISION for the DESTROYED permanent's controller. Key insight: the dispatcher already lets a handler park a decision â€” return `jsonb_build_object('awaiting_decision', true, 'decision_id', â€¦)` + set the stack item status='awaiting_decision' (exactly handle_scry's contract); and submit_decision's search_library branch searches the DECIDING player's library, so parking with deciding_player_id = the affected controller "just works" (basic â†’ their battlefield, shuffle). So handle_permanent_effect: capture the target's controller BEFORE the destroy (it resets to owner), apply the removal + caster `then` riders, then if `controller_searches_basic_land` park a min_choices=0 (may) search for that player. No new decision plumbing. Authoring = a boolean payload flag â†’ needed a NEW `'boolean'` registry field kind (checkbox in the form; optional booleans behave like optional effect-lists: skipped in effectDefault/parse-absent, dropped from JSON when false) + opponent-controlled removal target options (permanent_opponent / nonland_permanent_opponent â€” Assassin's Trophy targets "a permanent an opponent controls"). Schema/LLM/client (getSpellPlan + castPermanentEffect thread the flag). Tests ATR1-2 (destroy â†’ opponent search â†’ basic to battlefield; may-decline) + builder round-trip. 445/445. On targeted-spell-riders branch.

- [2026-06-07] **Commander-identity mana = a special `add_mana` colour `'commander'`, client-resolved + engine-validated (mig 151).** Command Tower / Arcane Signet ("add one mana of any colour in your commander's colour identity") â€” the colours are dynamic (depend on the commander), so the script can't list fixed colours. - [2026-06-07] **CDA (layer 7a) is read from the SCRIPT, not game_continuous_effects (mig 149, F2.2f).** A characteristic-defining ability is INHERENT to the card, so storing it as a continuous-effect row (and reproducing register/the CHECK) is the wrong shape. Instead a top-level script key `cda: {power:{count,plus?}, toughness:{...}}` is read live by `card_cda_value(session, card, which)` (counts creatures_you_control / lands_you_control / cards_in_graveyard + a `plus` offset). card_layered_power/toughness (reproduced from mig 146) just gained the CDA in the base coalesce: `set(7b) â†’ cda(7a) â†’ printed`. So set overrides CDA overrides printed; a non-CDA card returns null â†’ falls through unchanged. NO register/effect_type change. Fixture Wild Tracker Test (*/* = creatures you control, counts itself); tests CD1-5. **The P/T LAYER SYSTEM is now complete: 7a CDA, 7b set, 7c counters, 7d pumps/anthems, 7e switch â€” all live and ordered correctly (424/424).** Authoring (Zod top-level `cda`) deferred; engine reads jsonb directly. - [2026-06-06] **Routing COMBAT creature damage through the shield resolver must DEFER the lethal sweep (mig 148, F2.1e).** resolve_combat_damage marks all combat damage then runs ONE move_lethal sweep at the end (simultaneity â€” a creature dealt lethal still deals its own damage). apply_damage_to_creature's own per-call sweep would break that, so it gained `p_run_sweep boolean default true`; combat routes both creature sites (attackerâ†’blocker, blockerâ†’attacker) through it with run_sweep=false and keeps its single end-of-step sweep. The 6-arg version was DROPPED so the targeted caller (apply_creature_effect, 6 args) resolves to the new 7-arg with run_sweep defaulting true (plpgsql resolves the call at execution, so apply_creature_effect needn't be redefined). Protection (colour) gate preserved â€” the resolver call only happens for non-protected victims; the creature-damage tally counts the resolver's return (shields shrink it). resolve_combat_damage reproduced from CURRENT = mig 132. Tests CB1-4; all prior combat tests (over-assignment/first-double-strike/deathtouch/protection) green (419/419). [[project-roadmap]]

- [2026-06-06] **Commander return-to-command â€” a BEFORE-UPDATE trigger chokepoint + a standing preference, NOT per-event decisions (migration 142).** Slice 1 (mig 136) auto-returned a commander only on death (put_in_graveyard, graveyard only) and ignored owner choice. Generalised via a single `redirect_commander_zone_change` BEFORE UPDATE OF zone trigger on game_cards: a COMMANDER leaving the BATTLEFIELD to graveyard/exile/hand/library is rewritten to the command zone (if the owner's `game_session_players.commander_redirect` preference is on, default true). **Why a trigger:** it intercepts EVERY mover (put_in_graveyard, apply_creature_effect exile/bounce, combat lethal, SBA, sacrifice, direct writes) in one place â€” no per-mover reproduction (and it fixes the slice-1 exile/bounce gap where the commander was lost). **Why a standing preference, not a per-event pending-decision (which the roadmap floated):** the movers are SYNCHRONOUS and called mid-combat/mid-SBA; parking an async decision there would be a large, risky rework. A per-player toggle captures the agency synchronously. **Dies-suppression falls out for free + correct:** fire_zone_change_triggers (AFTER) fires 'dies' only on battlefieldâ†’graveyard; the BEFORE trigger rewrites NEW.zone to 'command' first, so 'dies' doesn't fire on a redirect, but DOES when the owner opts out (zone stays graveyard). put_in_graveyard reproduced from mig 136 WITHOUT its bespoke commander branch (trigger is now the single source of truth). SCOPE: battlefield-source only (the 99% case) â€” from-stack (countered) / from-library (milled/drawn, genuinely a "may") deferred. NO client UI for the toggle (default is the common case; set_commander_redirect RPC exists if needed). Tests RC1-6 (396/396). Harness: spawnCommander gained a zone arg + setCommanderRedirect; fixture "Reaper Commander Test" (diesâ†’draw) proves suppression.

- [2026-06-05] **Phase 4 / F1b â€” restart the priority round on a new stack object (migration 124). F1 now complete.** Fixes the respond-then-pass short-circuit: pass_priority counts consecutive passes and resolves once all N pass, but no path reset that count when a player ADDED to the stack â€” so after A passed (count=1), B casting in response then passing (count=2) resolved B's spell before A could respond. **MINIMAL universal fix: one AFTER INSERT trigger on game_stack_items** (`reset_priority_round_on_stack_change`) sets priority_pass_count=0 for the session â€” instead of reproducing ~8 cast/ability functions. Correct for triggered-ability enqueues too (a new trigger on the stack â‡’ fresh round), and even during combat (a block/attack trigger overriding declare_blocker's `greatest(0,player_count-1)` preset to 0 is correct â€” a real priority round is needed when a trigger fires; when none fires, no stack insert, preset stands). Guarded on `priority_pass_count <> 0` so a simultaneous-trigger batch updates turn_state once. priority_player_id left untouched (caster keeps priority; resolve/step code hands it to the active player when due). - [2026-06-05] **Phase 4 / F1a â€” APNAP ordering of simultaneous triggered abilities (migration 123).** Kickoff of the rules-engine "frontier" phase. User chose (AskUserQuestion) to complete ALL of Phase 4 incl. the heavy frontier, THEN Commander as a real format. **ARCHITECTURE DECISION (user asked "what would you suggest, layering gets worse with more players"): stay in PL/pgSQL; build the hard pieces (layer resolver, replacement resolver) as single ISOLATED, exhaustively-tested functions rather than ad-hoc interception.** Rationale: more players scales VOLUME, not the complexity class; the genuinely hard part (CR 613 layers / CR 616 replacement ordering) is hard in any language and isn't easier in TS; a TS rewrite would mean re-deriving all RLS/auth/SECURITY-DEFINER for no algorithmic win; isolation keeps a future TS port of just the resolver cheap. **AUDIT findings:** priority (pass_priority) is already multiplayer-correct in structure (priority_pass_count, seat rotation, resolve-when-all-pass); the real gaps are APNAP trigger ordering (this slice), replacement effects (none yet), and the continuous-effect model being FLAT-ADDITIVE (card_effective_power = base + counters + Î£pumps; no set/CDA/switch layers, no timestamps) â€” that's F2's layer resolver. **THIS SLICE (F1a):** enqueue_triggered_ability stamps `apnap_rank` (controller's seat distance from active player, 0=active); NEW order_pending_triggers(session) renumbers the not-yet-`apnap_ordered` trigger batch (enqueued consecutively â†’ contiguous position band) so rank 0 sits lowest = resolves LAST (stack is LIFO; position carries only a non-unique index so renumbering within the band is safe); resolve_top_of_stack settles before picking the top. - [2026-06-05] **Phase 4 â€” "can't be countered" (migration 120).** Scoped via AskUserQuestion (smallest Phase-4 item). **KEY DECISION: read the property at counter-RESOLUTION time, not stamp a flag through every cast path.** "Can't be countered" is a static spell property authored as a top-level `cant_be_countered: true` on the V2 script. - [2026-06-05] **Near-term authoring â€” DUAL-SHAPE variant mechanism (form-only, NO migration).** Made targeted `deal_damage` (Lightning Bolt) and targeted `add_counters` authorable in the GUIDED form. **No engine/Zod change needed** â€” the engine already cast these scripts (getSpellPlan routes deal_damageâ†’damage plan, add_countersâ†’add_counters plan) and Zod already allowed target_type on them; the ONLY gap was that the guided-form registry was one-def-per-`type`, with deal_damage/add_counters occupying that slot with their untargeted (recipient / on-self) shape, so a targeted one fell to JSON mode. **Design (Approach A â€” resolve variant by FIELDS, no JSON pollution):** EffectDef gained optional `variant`; the form-list KEY is `variant ?? type` (unique). Added 2 variant defs: `deal_damage_target` (spell-only â€” the engine routes a trigger "damage any target" vs each opponent, so triggers keep the recipient shape; new `damageTargetField` offers any/creature/creature-opp/player/opponent) and `add_counters_target` (spell+trigger, reuses creatureTargetField). **Resolution:** `resolveEffectDef(effect)` picks the def among defsForType whose field-keys are all present, most-fields-wins (so the on-self add_counters {amount} doesn't shadow the targeted {amount,target}); `effectKeyOf(effect)` gives the dropdown's selected key; `effectFromJson` now TRIES each def for the type and returns the first that strict-parses (variants are key-disjoint: recipient vs target_type, so â‰¤1 matches); `effectToJson`/`effectDefault` resolve by variant/key. Form: the effect-type `<select>` value is `effectKeyOf(effect)` and field rendering uses `resolveEffectDef` (was `effectDef(effect.type)`) â€” both the trigger and spell-action editors + the nested may/choose_player effect-list reuse the same EffectEditor, so they all got it. builder `defaultEffect`/`defaultSpellEffect` params loosened to accept a variant key string. **Characterization tests:** 3 cases flipped JSONâ†’form (trigger/spell targeted add_counters, may-with-targeted-add_counters-inner); added Lightning Bolt + targeted-add_counters round-trips + dual-shape defaults. **GOTCHA the design avoids:** storing a variant discriminator in the JSON would pollute scripts; inferring from fields keeps scripts clean and back-compatible. 289/289, tsc/lint clean. **Pattern for future dual-shapes:** add a def with a unique `variant` + a discriminating field; resolution is automatic.

- [2026-06-05] **Phase-3 targeting reach, slice 1 â€” general MULTI-TARGET removal (migration 112).** First effect with an arbitrary-length target set.
